### [1] [Dimension lower bounds in random geometry via Lipschitz functions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10496)
*Manan Bhatia,Ewain Gwynne,Brin Harper*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文证明了与刘维尔量子引力（Liouville quantum gravity, LQG）度量相关的若干自然集合的豪斯多夫维数（Hausdorff dimension）下界，包括3-星点集（Hausdorff维数至少为2）、边界上的2-星点集和度量网（至少为1），以及两个度量网的交集（至少为2）。证明主要基于拓扑方法，核心思路是将所考察的集合表示为利普希茨函数（Lipschitz function）的非恒定集。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LQG度量是随机几何中的核心研究对象，其相关集合（如星点集、度量网）的豪斯多夫维数是理解LQG几何结构的关键指标。本文旨在为这些维数提供严格的下界证明，并验证关于3-星点集Hausdorff维数至少为2的最优性猜想。

Method: 采用拓扑方法，核心技巧是将待研究的集合转化为Lipschitz函数的非恒定集（non-constancy sets），通过分析这些函数的行为来建立Hausdorff维数的下界。该方法不仅适用于LQG，也涵盖了一般的平面长度度量（如Kendall的Poisson道路度量）。

Result: 1) 3-星点集在LQG度量下的Hausdorff维数至少为2；2) 边界上的2-星点集和度量网的Hausdorff维数至少为1；3) 两个度量网的交集Hausdorff维数至少为2；4) 在LQG的特例中，得到了2-星点集和度量网相对于欧几里得度量（Euclidean metric）和LQG度量的更优维数下界。

Conclusion: 本文建立的维数下界支持了关于3-星点集Hausdorff维数为2的最优性猜想，且证明方法具有一般性，可推广至更广泛的平面长度度量空间。结果深化了对LQG度量几何结构的认识。

Abstract: We prove lower bounds for the Hausdorff dimensions of various natural sets associated with the Liouville quantum gravity (LQG) metric. We prove that the set of 3-star points (i.e., starting points of three disjoint geodesics) has Hausdorff dimension at least two with respect to the LQG metric, which is conjectured to be optimal. Our proof works for a general class of planar length metrics which also includes, e.g., Kendall's Poisson roads metric. We additionally prove a dimension lower bound of one for the set of 2-star points intersected with the boundary and for the metric net intersected with the boundary, as well as a dimension lower bound of two for the intersection of two metric nets. In the particular setting of LQG, we obtain sharper lower bounds for the Hausdorff dimensions of the set of 2-star points and the LQG metric net, with respect to both the Euclidean metric and the LQG metric. Our proofs are primarily topological. The key idea is to express the sets of interest in terms of non-constancy sets of Lipschitz functions.

</details>


### [2] [Quasisymmetric rigidity of the Brownian sphere](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10973)
*Jason Miller,Yi Tian*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文证明了布朗球（Brownian sphere）几乎必然没有非平凡拟对称自同构（quasisymmetric automorphism），即拟对称刚性（quasisymmetric rigidity），并表明两个独立布朗球几乎必然不是拟对称等价的，同时给出了其共形结构几乎必然由度量结构决定的新证明。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 布朗球作为随机度规测度空间（random metric measure space）和随机平面地图（random planar maps）的标度极限（scaling limit），其几何与共形性质的研究是随机几何领域的核心问题。理解其自同构群和等价关系有助于揭示随机曲面（random surfaces）的内在结构特征。

Method: 利用拟对称映射（quasisymmetric mapping）理论，结合布朗球的度量结构与共形结构之间的内在联系，通过论证其度量结构几乎必然唯一确定共形结构，进而证明拟对称自同构的平凡性。

Result: 布朗球几乎必然没有非平凡拟对称自同构；两个独立布朗球几乎必然不是拟对称等价的；布朗球的共形结构（conformal structure）几乎必然由其度量结构（metric structure）决定。

Conclusion: 布朗球具有拟对称刚性这一强唯一性性质，进一步巩固了其作为随机曲面典范对象的地位，并为随机几何与量子引力（Liouville quantum gravity）中的相关研究提供了基础性工具。

Abstract: The Brownian sphere, also known as the Brownian map, is a canonical random metric measure space homeomorphic to the two-dimensional sphere $\mathbf S^2$. It can be interpreted as the uniform measure on surfaces homeomorphic to $\mathbf S^2$, in the sense that it arises as the scaling limit of many natural models of random planar maps chosen uniformly from a given class. It is also equivalent to the $\sqrt{8/3}$-Liouville quantum gravity sphere. We prove that the Brownian sphere is quasisymmetrically rigid, meaning that, almost surely, it has no nontrivial quasisymmetric automorphisms. We also show that two independent Brownian spheres are almost surely not quasisymmetrically equivalent. Our argument also gives a new proof that the conformal structure of the Brownian sphere is almost surely determined by its metric structure.

</details>

### [3] [Dynamical Amrein-Berthier Uncertainty for Fractional Schrödinger Flows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10685)
*Piero D'Ancona,Diego Fiorletta*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文证明了分数阶薛定谔流（fractional Schrödinger flows）的动力学期Abrein-Berthier不确定性原理（dynamical Amrein-Berthier uncertainty principles），指出在有限测度集合上的两次时间局域化会导致解的非平凡估计，并揭示了分数阶指数α > 1/2的关键阈值条件及其与集合间相互作用能（interaction energy）的关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 不确定性原理是量子力学和调和分析的核心主题。目前对于分数阶薛定谔方程（fractional Schrödinger equation）是否满足类似Amrein-Berthier型不确定性原理（即两个时间点上的空间局域化能否约束解的整体行为），尚缺乏系统性理论结果。本文旨在填补这一空白，并揭示分数阶指数α以及集合几何性质对不确定性原理成立条件的影响。

Method: 利用自由哈密顿量H = (-Δ)^α的分数阶核（fractional kernel）的平稳相位结构（stationary phase structure），建立L²范数的定量估计。对于1/2 < α < 1的情形，引入并利用集合对(E, F)的自然相互作用能（interaction energy）I_γ(E, F)的有限性条件，其中γ = n(1-α)/(2α-1)。此外，对于一维分数阶哈密顿量(-∂_x²+V)^α和高阶哈密顿量(-Δ)^m+V，在适当的加权散射假设（weighted scattering assumptions）和衰减势（decaying potentials）条件下推广上述结果。

Result: 对于α > 1/2的自由分数阶薛定谔流，对于任意两个有限测度集合E, F和任意非零时间T，存在定量估计‖u(t)‖_{L²} ≲ ‖u(0)‖_{L²(E^c)} + ‖u(T)‖_{L²(F^c)}，其中t为任意实数。当α ≥ 1时，E和F可为任意有限测度集合；当1/2 < α < 1时，需要额外满足相互作用能I_γ(E, F) < ∞的条件，这等价于集合在无穷远处具有足够快的联合衰减。特别地，非零解不可能在两个不同时间点具有紧支集（compact support）。该结果也推广至一维分数阶哈密顿量和高阶哈密顿量情形。

Conclusion: 本文建立的动力学期Abrein-Berthier不确定性原理揭示了分数阶薛定谔流的独特性质：分数阶指数α的阈值α > 1/2由分数阶核的平稳相位结构决定，且当α较小时（1/2 < α < 1），集合的无穷远衰减行为成为不确定性原理能否成立的关键。这些结果深化了对分数阶薛定谔方程解的时空局域化限制的理解。

Abstract: We prove dynamical Amrein-Berthier uncertainty principles for fractional Schrödinger flows. For the free Hamiltonian $H=(-Δ)^α$ on $L^2(\mathbb{R}^n)$, with $α>\frac{1}{2}$, we show that two--time localization on finite measure sets $E,F$ forces the quantitative estimate \begin{equation*} \|u(t)\|_{L^{2}}\lesssim_{E,F,T,n,α} \|u(0)\|_{L^{2}(E^{c})} + \|u(T)\|_{L^{2}(F^{c})}, \qquad T\neq0,\ t\in \mathbb{R} \end{equation*} for $u(t)=e^{-itH}u(0)$ at every time. The threshold $α>\frac{1}{2}$ is tied to the stationary phase structure of the fractional kernel. If $α\ge1$ the sets can be arbitrary finite measure sets; if $\frac{1}{2}<α<1$ we impose the finiteness of a natural interaction energy \begin{equation*} \textstyle \mathcal{I}_γ(E,F) = \int_{\mathbb{R}^n \times \mathbb{R}^n} \mathbf{1}_{F}(x)|x-y|^{2γ}\mathbf{1}_{E}(y)\,dx\,dy<\infty, \qquad γ= \frac{n(1-α)}{2 α-1} \end{equation*} of the pair $(E,F)$, essentially equivalent to a sufficiently fast joint decay of the measure of the sets at infinity. In particular, compact support at two distinct times is impossible for a nonzero solution. We also prove corresponding results for one dimensional fractional Hamiltonians $(-\partial_x^2+V)^α$ under weighted scattering assumptions, and for higher order Hamiltonians $(-Δ)^m+V$ for suitable classes of decaying potentials $V$.

</details>


### [4] [Long-wave KdV hierarchy approximation of the NLS hierarchy with nonzero boundary conditions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10687)
*Robert Wegner*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文研究了在长波极限下，具有非零边界条件的NLS层次（NLS hierarchy）中某些重整化守恒量（renormalized conserved quantities）被KdV层次（KdV hierarchy）的能量近似的问题。证明表明，NSL层次的Lax算子（Dirac算子）的透射系数（transmission coefficient）在非相对论极限下可由Schrödinger算子（KdV层次的Lax算子）的透射系数近似，从而在层次之间建立了形式化的近似结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在可积系统理论中，非线性薛定谔方程（NLS）层次与Korteweg-de Vries（KdV）层次之间存在深层联系，但前者在长波极限下对重整化守恒量的近似行为尚未得到系统研究。作者希望将这一近似关系推广至所有正整数阶，并给出定量刻画。

Method: 通过证明NLS层次的Lax算子（即非相对论极限下的Dirac算子）的透射系数可由KdV层次的Lax算子（即Schrödinger算子）的透射系数近似，建立两个层次之间的形式近似关系。随后利用能量方法（energy methods）和已有的适定性结果（well-posedness results）对该近似进行定量分析。

Result: 成功将近似结果推广到所有 $n \in \mathbb{N}$，并给出了透射系数之间近似的严格证明。借助能量方法和已有适定性理论，量化了NLS层次与KdV层次之间的形式近似结果。

Conclusion: 本文在长波和非相对论极限下，严格建立了NLS层次的重整化守恒量可由KdV层次的能量近似，且该近似对任意正整数阶均成立，深化了两个可积层次之间关系的理解。

Abstract: We study the approximation of certain renormalized conserved quantities for the NLS hierarchy with nonzero boundary conditions, in the long-wave regime, by the energies of the KdV hierarchy. We extend this to all $n \in \mathbb{N}$ by proving an approximation result for the transmission coefficient of the Lax operator of the NLS hierarchy, which is a Dirac operator in the nonrelativistic regime, by the transmission coefficient of a Schrödinger operator, which is the Lax operator of the KdV hierarchy. This yields a formal approximation result between the hierarchies, which we quantify using energy methods and previously established well-posedness results.

</details>

### [5] [Unsupervised Deep Learning for Limited-Angle STEM-EDX Tomography -- Application to 3D Chemical Analysis of Phase-Change Memory Devices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10547)
*Daniel del Pozo Bueno,Serge Brosset,Theo Monniez,Gabriele Navarro,Philippe Ciuciu,Zineb Saghi*

Main category: eess.IV

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于深度图像先验与全变分正则化（DIP-TV）的无监督深度学习框架，并扩展为多通道形式（DIPm-TV），用于解决有限角度STEM-EDX断层扫描中的缺失楔伪影和低信噪比问题。在合成数据和Ge-Sb-Te（GST）存储器件实验数据上证明，该方法可在严重角度受限条件下实现近各向同性的三维元素重建，揭示器件运行中的成分异质性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: STEM-EDX断层扫描虽能实现纳米尺度三维成分与元素图谱，但受限于有限倾斜角度和低剂量条件：有限角度采集导致缺失楔伪影（missing-wedge artefacts），引起伸长和各向异性分辨率；低剂量数据进一步降低重建质量与定量可靠性。现有方法在严重角度受限条件下表现不佳。

Method: 引入基于深度图像先验（Deep Image Prior, DIP）与全变分正则化（total variation regularization, TV）的无监督深度学习框架DIP-TV，并扩展为多通道版本DIPm-TV，通过利用不同元素图谱之间的空间相关性进行联合重建。在合成3通道体模上验证其对严重缺失楔伪影的补偿能力，并与同步迭代重建技术（SIRT）和压缩感知方法进行对比。

Result: 在合成数据上，DIP-TV方法能够在约100°缺失角度范围和中等噪声条件下补偿严重缺失楔伪影，性能优于SIRT和压缩感知方法。在GST存储器件实验中，采用−40°至+40°、步长5°的有限角度采集，剂量为2.0×10⁵ e⁻/Å²。多通道方法无需外部结构先验（如高角环形暗场像），仅利用EDX信号即可实现逐体素元素重建，重建体展现近各向同性空间分辨率，并揭示与器件运行相关的成分异质性。

Conclusion: 该方法能够在实验可实现的样品几何中实现三维化学表征，克服了传统方法因严重角度限制而失效的问题，为纳米尺度器件的成分分析提供了新的无监督深度学习解决方案。

Abstract: Energy Dispersive X-ray (EDX) tomography in Scanning Transmission Electron Microscopy (STEM) enables 3D compositional and elemental mapping at the nanoscale, but its use is limited by restricted tilt ranges and low-dose conditions required to avoid beam damage. Limited-angle acquisition introduces missing-wedge artefacts such as elongation and anisotropic resolution, while noisy low-dose data further degrade reconstruction quality and quantitative reliability. Here, we introduce an unsupervised deep learning framework based on Deep Image Prior with total variation regularization (DIP-TV) for limited-angle STEM-EDX tomography. We extend it to a multi-channel formulation (DIPm-TV) that jointly reconstructs multiple elemental maps by exploiting spatial correlations. Using a synthetic 3-channel phantom, we show that the method compensates for severe missing-wedge artefacts corresponding to approximately $100^\circ$ of missing angular range under moderate noise, outperforming simultaneous iterative reconstruction technique and compressed sensing approaches. We apply the method to 3D chemical analysis of Ge-Sb-Te (GST) memory devices in virgin (as-fabricated) and SET (crystalline) operational states. Samples were prepared as cross-sectional focused ion beam lamellae and acquired under a limited-angle tilt range from $-40^\circ$ to $+40^\circ$ with $5^\circ$ steps and a dose of $2.0\times10^5$ $e^-/Ang^2$. The multi-channel approach enables voxel-by-voxel elemental reconstruction using only EDX signals without external structural priors such as high-angle annular dark-field imaging. The reconstructed volumes show near-isotropic spatial resolution and reveal compositional heterogeneities associated with device operation. This approach enables 3D chemical characterization in experimentally accessible sample geometries where conventional methods fail due to severe angular limitations.

</details>


### [6] [Low-Dose 3D Bonding Mapping Through "Soft" Core-Loss EELS Tomography and Unsupervised Deep Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10893)
*Mario Pelaez-Fernandez,Daniel del-Pozo-Bueno,Adrien Teurtrie,Serge Brosset,Maya Marinova,Phillipe Ciuciu,Marta Estrader,German Salazar-Alvarez,Francesca Peiró,Raul Arenal,Sonia Estradé,Zineb Saghi,Francisco De la Peña*

Main category: eess.IV

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种结合高剂量效率的软芯损失电子能量损失谱（EELS）方法和多通道深度图像先验（DIPm-TV）无监督算法，实现了对束敏感纳米材料FeO/Fe₃O₄核壳纳米立方体的低剂量、高分辨率三维化学构型与键合映射。该方法仅需少量投影即可获得约1 nm各向同性分辨率的氧化态体积重构，揭示出传统方法无法分辨的薄外层FeO壳层和内部空洞。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在扫描透射电子显微镜（scanning transmission electron microscopy, STEM）中，高空间分辨率下解析束敏感纳米材料的三维化学构型面临根本性矛盾：分析信号所需的高电子剂量与断层重构所需的大量投影之间存在折衷。现有方法难以兼顾剂量效率与三维信息保真度。

Method: 方法包含两项关键进展：一是利用Fe-M₂,₃边的无标样"软"芯损失EELS方法，相比传统Fe-L₂,₃边获得约50倍的剂量效率提升，仅将后者用作FeO和Fe₃O₄的标准参考源；二是引入多通道深度图像先验结合全变分正则化（multi-channel deep image prior with total variation regularization, DIPm-TV），一种无监督光谱断层成像方法，在稀疏视角和低剂量条件下通过利用空间相关性联合重构多个通道。

Result: 模拟数据集表明，仅需在-70°至+70°范围内使用9个投影即可获得高质量重构，无需高角环形暗场（HAADF-STEM）信号或对称性约束。应用于FeO/Fe₃O₄纳米立方体时，Fe-M₂,₃ EELS图显示出更高的信噪比和空间分辨率，揭示了包裹磁铁矿壳层的薄外层FeO壳层。DIPm-TV实现了约1 nm各向同性分辨率的氧化态体积重构，保留了立方体形貌，恢复了外层FeO壳层并揭示出一个内部小空洞——这些特征均为传统重构方法所无法获取。

Conclusion: 本研究建立了一条利用浅层芯损失边的低剂量二维及三维分析映射路径，可在保持光谱保真度和可靠三维信息的同时，实现数量级的剂量降低，为束敏感材料的分析成像提供了可行方案。

Abstract: Resolving the 3D chemical configuration of beam-sensitive nanomaterials at high spatial resolution remains a persistent frontier in scanning transmission electron microscopy (STEM). The main limitation lies in the trade-off between high electron dose required for analytical signals and the large number of projections needed for tomographic reconstruction. Here, we achieve dose-efficient 3D bonding mapping of FeO/Fe$_3$O$_4$ core-shell nanocubes with high resolution via electron energy loss spectroscopy (EELS). Our approach relies on two developments. First, a standardless "soft" core-loss EELS methodology exploiting Fe-M$_{2,3}$ edges provides ${\sim}50\times$ higher dose efficiency than conventional Fe-L$_{2,3}$ edges, using the latter only as a source of FeO and Fe$_3$O$_4$ standards. Second, we introduce multi-channel deep image prior with total variation regularization (DIPm-TV), an unsupervised method for spectroscopic tomography that jointly reconstructs multiple channels by exploiting spatial correlations under sparse-view and low-dose conditions. Using simulated datasets, high-quality reconstructions are obtained from as few as nine projections over $-70^\circ$ to $+70^\circ$, without HAADF-STEM signal or symmetry constraints. Applied to FeO/Fe$_3$O$_4$ nanocubes, Fe-M$_{2,3}$ EELS maps show improved SNR and spatial resolution, revealing a thin outer FeO shell surrounding the magnetite shell. DIPm-TV yields ${\sim}1$ nm isotropic resolution oxidation-state volumes preserving cubic morphology, recovering the outer FeO shell, and revealing a small internal void, features not accessible with conventional reconstruction methods. This work establishes a pathway for low-dose 2D and 3D analytical mapping of beam-sensitive materials using shallow core-loss edges, enabling orders-of-magnitude dose reduction while maintaining spectral fidelity and reliable 3D information.

</details>

### [7] [Testing Heavy Dark Matter Decay as the Origin of KM3-230213A](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09986)
*KM3NeT Collaboration,O. Adriani,J. A. Aguilar,A. Albert,A. R. Alhebsi,S. Alshalloudi,F. Ameli,M. Andre,L. Aphecetche,M. Ardid,S. Ardid,J. Aublin,F. Badaracco,B. Baret,A. Bariego-Quintana,L. Vacheret,V. Valsecchi,V. Van Elewyck,G. Vannoye,E. Vannuccini,G. Vasileiadis,F. Vazquez de Sola,A. Veutro,S. Viola,D. Vivolo,A. van Vliet,L. Voorend,E. de Wolf,S. Zavatarelli,D. Zito,J. D. Zornoza,J. Zúñiga*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文探讨了超高能中微子事件 KM3-230213A 源自质量在 PeV 尺度以上的重暗物质粒子衰变的假说，利用沉积能量、到达方向和完整探测器蒙特卡洛模拟计算不同衰变道的预期信号分布，并评估银河系与河外暗物质的相对贡献。结果显示，在 95% 置信水平下暗物质质量大于约 100 PeV，最佳拟合寿命在 $10^{26}$–$10^{27}$ s 范围内，但该参数区间与其他中微子望远镜及伽马射线观测的现有上限存在张力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验超高能中微子事件 KM3-230213A 是否由质量超过 PeV 标度（PeV scale）的重暗物质粒子衰变产生，从而为暗物质间接探测提供可能的新信号来源。

Method: 利用事件沉积能量（deposited energy）和到达方向（arrival direction），结合完整探测器蒙特卡洛模拟（Monte Carlo simulation）计算不同衰变道（decay channel）的预期信号分布，并分别评估银河系（Galactic）与河外（extragalactic）暗物质的相对贡献。

Result: 在假定事件源于暗物质的条件下，95% 置信水平（C.L.）下暗物质质量大于约 100 PeV，最佳拟合寿命（best-fit lifetime）在 $10^{26}$–$10^{27}$ s 区间；该参数区域与其他中微子望远镜及伽马射线观测的现有约束存在张力（tension）。

Conclusion: KM3-230213A 事件若确为暗物质衰变所致，则其暗物质质量下限约为 100 PeV，但该解释与现有天文观测的上限相冲突，暗示需进一步检验或考虑其他起源。

Abstract: This work explores the hypothesis that the ultra-high-energy neutrino event KM3-230213A originates from the decay of a heavy dark matter particle with a mass above PeV scale. The analysis exploits the deposited energy and arrival direction of the event as well as a complete detector Monte Carlo simulation to compute the expected signal distributions for different decay channels and assesses the relative contributions from Galactic and extragalactic dark matter. Assuming a dark matter origin of the event, we find that the preferred mass at 95% C.L. is larger than about 100 PeV in all scenarios considered, with best-fit lifetimes in the range $10^{26}$-$10^{27}$ s. These preferred regions are in tension with existing bounds from other neutrino telescopes and gamma-ray observations.

</details>

Xu,Z. Xu,Z. Xu,Z. Xu,Z. Xu,S. Yadav,K. Yang,X. Yang,Y. Yang,Y. Yang,Z. Yang,Z. Yang,Z. Yang,H. Yeung,H. Yin,X. Yin,C. Y. Yu,J. Yu,K. Yu,X. Yuan,Y Yuan,J. A. Zamora Saa,M. Zavertyaev,M. Zdybal,F. Zenesini,C. Zeng,M. Zeng,S. H Zeng,C. Zhang,C. Zhang,D. Zhang,J. Zhang,L. Zhang,Q. Z. Zhang,R. Zhang,S. Zhang,S. L. Zhang,Y. Zhang,Z. Zhang,J. Zhao,Y. Zhao,A. Zhelezov,S. Z. Zheng,X. Z. Zheng,Y. Zheng,T. Zhou,X. Zhou,V. Zhovkovska,L. Z. Zhu,X. Zhu,X. Zhu,Y. Zhu,V. Zhukov,J. Zhuo,D. Zuliani,G. Zunica,X. Zuo*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 利用LHCb实验在13 TeV质子-质子对撞数据（积分亮度5.4 fb⁻¹）中测量了半轻子衰变分支比$\mathcal{R}(J/ψ)$，结果为$0.51 \pm 0.12\text{(stat)} \pm 0.08\text{(syst)}$，与标准模型轻子普适性（lepton flavor universality）预言在1.8个标准差内一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验轻子普适性，即标准模型（Standard Model）中不同代轻子与规范玻色子耦合强度相同的预言。通过测量$\mathcal{R}(J/ψ)$，可探究$\tau$轻子与$\mu$轻子在$B_c^+$介子半轻子衰变中的行为是否一致，从而寻找超出标准模型的新物理信号。

Method: 基于LHCb实验2016–2018年采集的质子-质子（proton-proton）对撞数据，质心系能量（center-of-mass energy）为13 TeV，积分亮度（integrated luminosity）5.4 fb⁻¹。测量了$\mathcal{R}(J/ψ) \equiv \mathcal{B}(B_c^+ \to J/ψτ^+ ν_τ)/\mathcal{B}(B_c^+ \to J/ψμ^+ ν_μ)$这一比值。

Result: 测量值为$\mathcal{R}(J/ψ) = 0.51 \pm 0.12\text{(stat)} \pm 0.08\text{(syst)}$，统计不确定度（statistical uncertainty）为0.12，系统不确定度（systematic uncertainty）为0.08。

Conclusion: 测量结果与标准模型在轻子普适性框架下的预言在1.8个标准差（standard deviations）内相符，未发现显著的超出标准模型新物理迹象。

Abstract: A measurement of the ratio of semileptonic branching fractions $\mathcal{R}(Jψ)$, defined as $\mathcal{R}(J/ψ) \equiv \mathcal{B}(B_c^+ \to J/ψτ^+ ν_τ)/\mathcal{B}(B_c^+ \to J/ψμ^+ ν_μ)$, is reported using a sample of proton-proton collision data corresponding to an integrated luminosity of 5.4 fb$^{-1}$ recorded by the LHCb experiment in 2016--2018 at a center-of-mass energy of 13 TeV. The measured value is found to be $\mathcal{R}(J/ψ) = 0.51 \pm 0.12\text{(stat)} \pm 0.08\text{(syst)}$, which is within 1.8 standard deviations of the predictions from the Standard Model assuming lepton flavor universality.

</details>


### [9] [Performance of the Eos detector with water](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10234)
*Eos Collaboration,S. Arora,M. Askins,A. J. Bacon,Z. Bagdasarian,A. Baldoni,L. Bartoszek,M. Bergevin,Y. Bezawada,E. Blucher,J. Boissevain,R. Bonventre,E. J. Callaghan,D. F. Cowen,K. DeHolton,M. Diwan,M. Dubnowski,P. Englezos,S. Gadamsetty,C. Grant,B. Harris,M. R. Hebert,S. Jeon,T. Kaptanoglu,A. Katt,J. R. Klein,T. Kroupova,L. Lebanowski,S. Lynch,A. Mastbaum,C. Mauger,G. Mayers,M. Miller,J. Nachtman,S. Naugle,J. Newby,M. Newcomer,A. Nikolica,G. D. Orebi Gann,A. Phipps,L. Pickard,R. C. Pitelka,L. Ren,A. Rincon,R. Rosero,N. Rowe,H. J. Ryoo,J. Ryshkewitch,J. Saba,S. Schoppmann,J. Shen,M. Smiley,H. Song,H. Steiger,B. Tam,E. Tiras,W. H. To,M. R. Vagins,R. Van Berg,J. Wallig,G. Wendel,M. Wetstein,M. Wurm,G. Yang,M. Yeh,E. D. Zimmerman,A. Zummo*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文介绍了位于加州大学伯克利分校的四吨光学探测器Eos的首批实验结果。Eos旨在展示基于闪烁体的“混合”探测器技术在未来中微子探测器中的性能。实验期间，内外容器均注满水，利用纯切伦科夫光作为校准介质，通过部署光学和放射性校准源进行详细标定，并比较模拟与实验数据以验证重建算法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 展示Eos探测器的首批实验结果，验证基于闪烁体的“混合”探测器技术在未来中微子探测器中的性能潜力。

Method: 采用四吨光学探测器Eos，内部靶容器和外部缓冲容器均注满水作为仅产生切伦科夫光（Cherenkov light）的介质，部署光学和放射性校准源（calibration sources）进行详细探测器标定，并通过校准模型进行模拟，与不同源位置和旋转角度下的实验数据进行比较。

Result: 完成了基于水介质的详细探测器校准，实现了多种重建算法（reconstruction algorithms）的测试，并对比了校准模型模拟与不同类型校准源、源位置和旋转下的实验数据。

Conclusion: Eos探测器成功展示了基于水介质的标定能力，为后续部署闪烁材料（scintillating material）并验证混合探测器技术（hybrid detector technology）奠定了基础。

Abstract: In this manuscript we present the first results from Eos, a four tonne optical detector located at the University of California, Berkeley. The primary goal of Eos is to demonstrate the performance capabilities of scintillation-based, 'hybrid' detector technology for future neutrino detectors. The data presented were collected while both the inner target vessel and the outer buffer vessel were filled with water. The water target acts as a well-understood medium that produces only Cherenkov light, which can be used to calibrate and develop the detector model and reconstruction algorithms prior to the deployment of scintillating material. Using deployed optical and radioactive calibration sources, a series of detailed detector calibrations are performed. These enable a suite of tests for various reconstruction algorithms. Simulations that use calibrated models are compared with the data across a variety of different types of calibration sources, source positions, and rotations.

</details>

TL;DR: 本文通过BESIII实验在质心能量4.128至4.226 GeV、总积分亮度7.33 fb⁻¹的e⁺e⁻对撞数据中，测量了电磁达利兹衰变（electromagnetic Dalitz decay）D*⁺ₛ → e⁺e⁻D⁺ₛ的分支比（branching fraction），结果为(7.28±0.61_stat±0.31_syst)×10⁻³，精度较此前结果提高了2.5倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: D*⁺ₛ → e⁺e⁻D⁺ₛ电磁达利兹衰变分支比的精确测量，可为理论模型参数提供约束，同时有助于通过相对测量方法确定D*⁺ₛ → π⁰D⁺ₛ和D*⁺ₛ → γD⁺ₛ的绝对分支比。

Method: 基于BESIII实验采集的e⁺e⁻对撞数据（质心能量4.128–4.226 GeV，总积分亮度7.33 fb⁻¹）进行测量。

Result: 测得分支比B(D*⁺ₛ → e⁺e⁻D⁺ₛ) = (7.28 ± 0.61_stat ± 0.31_syst) × 10⁻³，与先前结果一致，精度提升了2.5倍。

Conclusion: 该结果为约束理论模型参数以及利用相对方法确定D*⁺ₛ → π⁰D⁺ₛ和D*⁺ₛ → γD⁺ₛ的绝对分支比提供了重要输入。

Abstract: The branching fraction of the electromagnetic Dalitz decay $D^{*+}_{s}\to e^{+}e^{-}D^{+}_{s}$ is measured with an $e^{+}e^{-}$ collision data sample collected by the BESIII experiment at center-of-mass energies between 4.128 and 4.226 $\mathrm{GeV}$, corresponding to a total integrated luminosity of 7.33 $\mathrm{fb}^{-1}$. The measurement yields the branching fraction ${\mathcal{B}(D^{*+}_{s}\to e^{+}e^{-}D^{+}_{s})=(7.28\pm0.61_{\mathrm{stat}}\pm0.31_{\mathrm{syst}})\times10^{-3}}$. The result is consistent with the previous one, with a 2.5-fold improvement in precision. This provides an important input for constraining the parameters of theoretical models and for determining the absolute branching fractions of $D^{*+}_{s}\to π^{0}D^{+}_{s}$ and $D^{*+}_{s}\to γD^{+}_{s}$, measured with a relative method.

</details>


### [11] [Agentic Hybrid RAG for Evidence-Grounded Muon Collider Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10381)
*Ruobing Jiang,Dawei Fu,Cheng Jiang,Tianyi Yang,Zijian Wang,Youpeng Wu,Yong Ban,Yajun Mao,Qiang Li*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文提出一种面向缪子对撞机（muon collider）研究的证据驱动型混合RAG框架——agentic hybrid RAG，结合稀疏词汇检索与稠密语义检索（hybrid retriever）以及智能体推理模块（agentic reasoning），并构建了该领域首个检索增强型科学问答基准。实验表明，混合检索提供最强检索基础，智能体推理在受控证据扩展与答案合成方面最为有效，整体框架在检索效果、答案质量、证据覆盖与事实依据上均优于代表性基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高能物理（high-energy physics, HEP）领域日益探索智能体辅助分析工作流，高效定位、整合与验证科学证据成为关键能力。尽管检索增强生成（retrieval-augmented generation, RAG）为科学问答提供了有前景的框架，但如何在保持检索精度的同时整合智能体推理（agentic reasoning）仍是核心挑战。

Method: 提出agentic hybrid RAG框架，包含混合检索器（hybrid retriever），融合稀疏词汇检索（sparse lexical retrieval）与稠密语义检索（dense semantic retrieval）；并引入智能体推理模块（agentic reasoning module），支持查询分解（query decomposition）、证据扩展（evidence expansion）与基于证据的答案生成（grounded answer generation）。此外，构建了缪子对撞机领域首个检索增强型科学问答基准，包含策展文献语料库及专门的检索与答案生成评测集。

Result: 混合检索（hybrid retrieval）提供了最强的检索基础；智能体推理在受控证据扩展与答案合成方面表现最佳。基于该原则，agentic hybrid RAG在检索效果、答案质量、证据覆盖（evidence coverage）与事实依据（factual grounding）上一致优于代表性的检索与RAG基线。

Conclusion: 该基准与框架为证据驱动的科学问答及未来面向大规模科学文献的高能物理分析智能体（HEP analysis agents）提供了基础。

Abstract: Muon collider research spans accelerator physics, detector instrumentation, and high-energy phenomenology, with relevant evidence scattered across a rapidly expanding and heterogeneous body of scientific literature. As high-energy physics (HEP) increasingly explores agent-assisted analysis workflows, efficiently locating, integrating, and verifying scientific evidence becomes an essential capability. While retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) offers a promising framework for scientific question answering, integrating agentic reasoning without compromising retrieval precision remains a key challenge. In this work, we present agentic hybrid RAG, an evidence-grounded RAG framework for muon collider research. The framework combines a hybrid retriever, integrating sparse lexical and dense semantic retrieval, with an agentic reasoning module for query decomposition, evidence expansion, and grounded answer generation. To enable systematic evaluation, we construct the first benchmark for retrieval-augmented scientific question answering in the muon collider domain, comprising a curated literature corpus together with dedicated retrieval and answer-generation benchmarks covering major detector and physics research topics. Extensive evaluation shows that hybrid retrieval provides the strongest retrieval backbone, while agentic reasoning is most effective for controlled evidence expansion and answer synthesis. Built on this principle, agentic hybrid RAG consistently outperforms representative retrieval and RAG baselines in retrieval effectiveness, answer quality, evidence coverage, and factual grounding. Together, the benchmark and framework provide a foundation for evidence-grounded scientific question answering and future HEP analysis agents operating over large-scale scientific literature.

</details>


### [12] [A Multimodal Domain-Adversarial Network for Fragmentation Background Suppression in AMS Heavy Nuclei Measurements](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10637)
*Zhen Liu,Valerio Formato,Muhammad Waqas*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文提出一种多模态域对抗神经网络（Multimodal Domain-Adversarial Neural Network, MDA）方法，利用硅径迹探测器与飞行时间探测器的异构数据融合及域对抗训练策略，有效抑制国际空间站上阿尔法磁谱仪（AMS）在测量稀有宇宙射线原子核通量时由探测器材料内碎裂反应产生的强干扰本底，并以磷核（P）为例验证了该方法的可行性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 阿尔法磁谱仪（AMS）对宇宙射线核通量进行高精度测量时，随着探测核素电荷数（Z）增大、丰度降低，由较重的宇宙射线在探测器材料（尤其是径迹探测器第1层与第2层之间）中发生的碎裂反应所产生的本底逐渐成为主要误差来源。现有方法对这类本底的抑制能力不足，迫切需要一种高效且适用于稀有核素测量的背景抑制技术。

Method: 提出一种多模态域对抗神经网络（MDA）。该模型通过专用子网络分别处理硅径迹探测器与飞行时间探测器的异构数据，并采用多头注意力机制（multi-head attention）进行特征融合；同时引入域对抗训练策略（domain-adversarial training），学习对探测器效应不敏感的不变表示（invariant representations），使得基于蒙特卡罗模拟（Monte Carlo simulation）训练的模型能够可靠迁移至真实飞行数据。

Result: 以磷核（P）为基准测试，验证了MDA模型在抑制碎裂本底方面的有效性。该方法展现了良好的背景抑制能力。

Conclusion: 该多模态域对抗神经网络提供了一种鲁棒且通用性强的框架，可用于AMS对其它稀有宇宙射线原子核通量的精确测量。

Abstract: The Alpha Magnetic Spectrometer (AMS) aboard the International Space Station provides high-precision measurements of cosmic-ray nuclei fluxes from charge Z=1 to Z=28 and beyond. With negligible charge confusion from non-interacting nuclei, the precision of nuclei flux measurements is primarily limited by fragmentation backgrounds originating from heavier cosmic rays interacting within detector materials, particularly between tracker Layers 1 and 2 (L1-L2). As AMS extends its measurements to heavier and rarer nuclei, these fragmentation backgrounds become increasingly dominant, necessitating advanced background suppression methods. To address this challenge, we introduce a Multimodal Domain-Adversarial (MDA) neural network designed to effectively suppress these interaction backgrounds. The MDA model fuses heterogeneous data from the silicon tracker and time-of-flight detectors using specialized sub-networks combined via multi-head attention. Crucially, a domain-adversarial training strategy is employed to learn invariant representations, enabling the model, which is trained on Monte Carlo simulations, to be reliably applied to flight data. Using phosphorus (P) as a benchmark, we demonstrate its background suppression capabilities. This approach provides a robust, generalizable framework applicable to the measurement of other rare cosmic-ray nuclei with AMS.

</details>


### [13] [$Λ$(1520) as a probe of resonance-driven deuteron formation at the LHC](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10668)
*Sushanta Tripathy,Peter Christiansen*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种通过长寿命共振态Λ(1520)衰变产生的质子与kaon的关联，利用代理质量观测量M_(d/2)K来区分高能碰撞中氘核产生的聚并（coalescence）与统计热模型（statistical thermal model）这两种机制，模拟结果显示该峰值仅在聚并场景下出现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高能质子-质子和核碰撞中大量产生轻核（如氘核），但其产生机制尚未明确，因为核子聚并（nucleon coalescence）和统计热模型（statistical thermal model）均能复现LHC的产额数据，亟需一种能够区分两种机制的观测量。

Method: 利用长寿命共振态Λ(1520) → pK的衰变链，若衰变产生的质子通过聚并形成氘核（deuteron），则氘核与kaon保持空间关联；通过构造代理质量观测量M_(d/2)K（由kaon和氘核四动量的一半构成），可在聚并场景下重建共振峰。使用Thermal-FIST和带有氘核聚并后处理（coalescence afterburner）的PYTHIA进行模拟验证。

Result: 模拟结果显示，M_(d/2)K峰值仅在聚并（coalescence）场景中出现，在统计热模型场景中不存在，表明该观测量可直接区分两种产生机制。

Conclusion: 该观测量为实验上直接探测共振态馈入的氘核产生以及高能碰撞中晚期聚并动力学（late-stage coalescence dynamics）提供了新的探针。

Abstract: Light nuclei such as deuterons are produced abundantly in high-energy proton-proton and nuclear collisions despite their tiny binding energies. Their production mechanism remains unresolved, as both nucleon coalescence and statistical thermal models reproduce inclusive LHC yields. We propose a direct invariant-mass observable that discriminates between these scenarios using the long-lived $Λ(1520) \to {\rm pK}$ resonance. If decay protons coalesce into deuterons, the produced nuclei remain correlated with the kaon, allowing the resonance peak to be reconstructed experimentally through proxy masses, $M_{\rm (d/2)K}$, formed from kaons and half the deuteron four-momentum. Using Thermal-FIST and PYTHIA with a deuteron coalescence afterburner, we show that a $M_{\rm (d/2)K}$ peak emerges only in the coalescence scenario. This observable provides a direct experimental probe of resonance-fed deuteron production and of late-stage coalescence dynamics in high-energy collisions.

### [14] [Understanding Energy Dependent Hadronic Calorimeter Response from a Machine Learning Perspective](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10960)
*Shuai-Chun Wang,Huang-Ran Shen,Wan-Bing He,Wei-Hu Ma,Peng-Jie Li,De-Qing Fang,Yu-Gang Ma*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了利用机器学习进行强子能量重建的方法，分析了闪烁光、切伦科夫光、带电粒子和完整三维簇射拓扑等多种信号通道的作用。在不考虑探测器效应、能量范围至10 GeV条件下，当充分利用所有信号通道和三维簇射信息时，强子簇射的固有分辨率可达约 (10.8±0.3)%/√(E/GeV)。与传统信号求和法相比，机器学习方法在10%有限采样分数下将能量分辨率从 (57.6±3.7)%/√(E/GeV) 提升至 (34.1±2.8)%/√(E/GeV)，展示了多通道信息和空间簇射特征在高粒度与双读出量能器设计中结合机器学习的巨大潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 未来高能物理实验对精度要求不断提高，提升强子量能器（hadronic calorimeter）的能量分辨率仍是一项关键挑战。

Method: 采用机器学习（machine learning）方法对强子能量重建进行系统研究，考虑了闪烁光（scintillation light）、切伦科夫光（Cherenkov light）、带电粒子（charged particles）以及强子簇射（hadronic shower）的完整三维拓扑信息，能量范围覆盖至10 GeV，且未考虑探测器效应（detector effects）。

Result: 充分利用所有信号通道和三维簇射信息时，强子簇射的固有分辨率约为 (10.8±0.3)%/√(E/GeV)。在10%有限采样分数下，基于机器学习的重建将能量分辨率从传统信号求和法的 (57.6±3.7)%/√(E/GeV) 提升至 (34.1±2.8)%/√(E/GeV)。

Conclusion: 多通道信息与详细的空间簇射特征对强子能量重建至关重要；将高粒度（high-granularity）和双读出（dual-readout）量能器设计同基于机器学习的重建技术相结合，在未来实验中具有显著潜力。

Abstract: To meet the precision requirements of future high-energy physics experiments, improving the energy resolution of hadronic calorimeters remains a critical challenge. This work presents a systematic investigation of hadronic energy reconstruction using machine learning, highlighting the roles of various signal channels, including scintillation light, Cherenkov light, charged particles, and the full three-dimensional topology of hadronic showers in the energy range up to 10 GeV. Throughout this study, detector effects are not taken into account. Under these conditions, the intrinsic resolution of hadronic showers reaches approximately $(10.8\pm0.3)\% / \sqrt{E/GeV}$ when all signal channels and the full 3D shower information are fully utilized. Compared with the traditional signal-summing approach, machine-learning-based reconstruction can significantly improve energy resolution, even under a limited sampling fraction of 10\%, enhancing it from $(57.6\pm3.7)\%/\sqrt{E/GeV}$ to $(34.1\pm2.8)\%/\sqrt{E/GeV}$. These results highlight the critical importance of both multi-channel information and detailed spatial shower features in hadronic energy reconstruction, and demonstrate the substantial potential of combining high-granularity and dual-readout calorimeter designs with machine-learning-based reconstruction techniques for future experiments.

</details>


### [15] [ALETHEIA: Autonomous Loop for Experimental Theory and HEP Inference Across-data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11024)
*Vincent Alexander Croft*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文提出了ALETHEIA——一种自动构建用于物理基础模型（physics foundation models）流形学习的自完备工具。它通过主动学习循环（active-learning loop）实现置换不变（permutation-invariant）的逐事件表示，并成功应用于中性流Drell-Yan过程中的四算子六维标准模型有效场论（SMEFT）分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有文献通常将表示学习与算子扩展两个任务混为一谈。ALETHEIA旨在解耦这两个任务：主动学习负责在固定算子内容下最快锁定模型系数，而物理扩展则根据残差结构决定何时开启新算子。

Method: 核心表示是ManifoldInformer——一种置换不变的逐事件编码器ψ_θ，经池化后连接至闭式岭回归头（closed-form ridge head）。主动学习循环监控残差算子指纹：当单个超出张成空间（out-of-span）方向占主导时，将该方向追加至ψ_θ（ψ-扩展）并重新拟合。扩展算子通过Arize-Phoenix张成空间解锁，按照SMEFT幂次计数排序。

Result: 该表示的潜在空间能够恢复SMEFT截面的解析变形切线（morphing tangents，R²=0.999）和曲率（curvatures，R²=0.954）。通过监控迹可直接读取“学习正确”（每次扩展使σ₁下降）和“学习完全”（σ₁低于噪声本底）两个概念。

Conclusion: ALETHEIA提供了一种自动化、可自完备的方法来监测和构建物理基础模型中的流形学习过程，通过解耦主动学习与物理扩展，实现了对未知物理流形的高效、可解释表示学习。

Abstract: ALETHEIA is a self-completing tool for monitoring the learning of manifolds in physics foundation models from data. It provides a method to automatically build physics foundation models for permutation-invariant per-event representations of unknown physics manifolds. This process is demonstrated here for dimension-six Standard Model Effective Field Theory (SMEFT) content of four operators in neutral-current Drell-Yan, whose input is unordered event-level features, and we drive it with an active-learning loop that separates two jobs that the literature usually conflates. Active learning completes a representation: given a fixed operator content, an acquisition rule chooses the working points that pin the model's coefficients fastest. The physics expands it: which new operator to switch on is read from the residual structure, ordered by SMEFT power counting, never guessed by the acquisition. The representation is the ManifoldInformer, a permutation-invariant per-event encoder $ψ_θ$ pooled into a closed-form ridge head; its latent recovers the analytic morphing tangents ($R^2=0.999$) and curvatures ($R^2=0.954$) of the SMEFT cross section. The loop monitors a residual-operator fingerprint: when a single out-of-span direction dominates, it appends that direction to $ψ_θ$ ($ψ$-extension) and refits. The acquisition arm unlocks new operators through an Arize-Phoenix span, such that the concepts of ``learning correctly'', in which each extension collapses $σ_1$; and ``learned completely'', in which $σ_1$ is below the noise floor; are read directly off the monitored trace.

</details>


### [16] [The SHiP/NA67 experiment at the ECN3 high-intensity beam facility at the CERN SPS](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11039)
*Matei Climescu*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: SHiP/NA67 是一个在 CERN SPS 上获批的高强度束流倾倒实验，旨在搜寻质量在 100 MeV 到数 GeV 范围内的弱相互作用粒子（如重中性轻子、暗光子、暗标量、类轴子粒子和轻暗物质），同时利用倾倒产生的高通量中微子开展标准模型与中微子物理研究，预计在 15 年运行时间内收集 6×10²⁰ 个质子打靶。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索目前实验覆盖不足的弱相互作用粒子（feebly interacting particles）区域，这些粒子的质量处于 O(100 MeV) 到数 GeV 范围；同时利用束流倾倒产生的高通量中微子开展标准模型（Standard Model）物理研究，特别是每年的约 10³ 个 ν_τ 事例可用于研究 τ 中微子（ν_τ）现象学。

Method: 采用高强度束流倾倒实验（beam dump experiment）方案，在 CERN 的 SPS 加速器 ECN3 实验厅与新建的束流倾倒设施（Beam Dump Facility, BDF）联合运行，收集 6×10²⁰ 个质子打靶，运行约 15 年。实验包含多个探测器子系统以覆盖不同的信号特征。

Result: 预期对大多数在此质量范围内预测新粒子的模型具有领先灵敏度，包括重中性轻子（heavy neutral leptons）、暗光子（dark photons）、暗标量（dark scalars）、类轴子粒子（axion-like particles）和轻暗物质（light dark matter）；每年可收集约 10³ 个 ν_τ 事例，支持 τ 中微子现象学研究。

Conclusion: SHiP/NA67 实验已于 2024 年获批，将填补弱相互作用粒子探索领域的重要空白，并推动中微子物理尤其是 ν_τ 方向的研究。文章总结了其物理动机、实验概念、探测器子系统、预期灵敏度及时间线。

Abstract: The Search for Hidden Particles (SHiP/NA67) is a general-purpose, high-intensity beam dump experiment approved in 2024 for the future exploitation of the ECN3 experimental hall at the CERN Super-Proton-Synchrotron in conjunction with the new Beam Dump Facility (BDF). It will collect $6\times10^{20}$ protons on target over $\sim$15 years of operation. SHiP is designed to probe the largely underexplored domain of feebly interacting particles with masses in the $\mathcal{O}(100~\mathrm{MeV})$ to few-GeV range, providing leading sensitivity to most models predicting particles within this range, notably heavy neutral leptons, dark photons, dark scalars, axion-like particles and light dark matter. The intense flux of neutrinos of all flavours produced in the dump additionally enables a rich Standard Model and neutrino-physics programme with notably $\mathcal{O}(10^3)$ $ν_τ$ per year of operation, thus bringing forward a study of $ν_τ$ phenomenology. This contribution summarises the physics motivation, the experimental concept and the detector subsystems, and outlines the expected sensitivity and timeline.

</details>

### [17] [Confidence, Statistical Evidence and Relative Belief with Applications to a Problem in Particle Physics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10256)
*Michael Evans,Siqi Zheng*

Main category: physics.data-an

TL;DR: 本文基于证据原则（principle of evidence），探讨相对信念推断（relative belief inferences）在泊松信号加背景噪声模型（Poisson model for a signal with background noise）中的不确定性量化（uncertainty quantification）区间构建，并将其与 Feldman-Cousins 区间进行对比。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 概率论通过证据原则为未观测响应事件提供了支持、反对或无证据的明确定义，但标准贝叶斯分析中即使无先验信息时，报告推断仍需反映似然排序（likelihood ordering）。现有方法可能无法同时满足这些要求，因此需要一种既能体现证据原则又能在重复抽样意义下控制误差的推断框架。

Method: 采用相对信念推断方法构建不确定性量化区间；该方法满足似然排序约束，并通过控制推断误差来满足频率学派（frequentist）要求（如达到给定置信水平）。将该方法应用于泊松信号加背景噪声模型，并与 Feldman-Cousins 区间进行对比分析。

Result: 相对信念推断区间在满足证据原则所要求的似然排序的同时，还能通过误差控制实现频率学派的置信水平要求。与 Feldman-Cousins 区间的对比显示了该方法的特性与优势。

Conclusion: 相对信念推断为泊松信号加背景噪声模型中的不确定性量化提供了一种同时满足证据原则和频率学派要求的区间构建方法，可作为 Feldman-Cousins 区间的一个有效替代方案。

Abstract: Probability theory provides a clear definition of what is meant by evidence in favor, against or none either way, of an event occurring for an unobserved response, via the principle of evidence. This is immediately applicable when carrying out a proper Bayesian analysis. Even without a prior, this imposes restrictions on reported inferences as these need to reflect the likelihood ordering. Relative belief inferences satisfy this requirement and, when the errors in these inferences are controlled, they also satisfy repeated sampling, or frequentist, requirements such as achieving given confidence levels. Relative belief inferences are considered here for the construction of intervals for uncertainty quantification in the context of a Poisson model for a signal with background noise. These intervals are contrasted with the well-known Feldman-Cousins intervals for this problem.

</details>

### [18] [Filamentary Transport and Thermoelectric Effects in Mushroom Phase Change Memory Cells](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10262)
*Md Samzid Bin Hafiz,Helena Silva,Ali Gokirmak*

Main category: physics.app-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过二维有限元电热计算研究Ge₂Sb₂Te₅蘑菇型相变存储单元在Reset和Set操作中的热电效应与丝状电子输运，发现电流极性通过热电效应显著影响操作能量、功率和电流需求，并指出编程区域体积在接触尺寸大于10 nm时不再缩放，且更大接触面积虽引入变异性但可能提升可靠性与耐久性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解Ge₂Sb₂Te₅蘑菇型相变存储单元中热电效应与丝状电子输运对Reset和Set操作的影响，揭示电流极性、热边界条件与编程区域（programming region）位置、形状及体积之间的关联。

Method: 采用二维有限元电热计算（2D finite-element electrothermal computational study），在模型中考虑非晶Ge₂Sb₂Te₅中空间激活能（activation energy）变化以及相变动力学（phase-change dynamics），并对比不同电流极性与热边界条件。

Result: 电流从顶部电极流向窄4 nm底部电极（Reset操作）时，可比相反极性节省约3倍能量与功率，并降低约2倍电流，达到相同Reset电阻。丝状导电（filamentary conduction）、电击穿（electrical breakdown）、热失控（thermal runaway）及局部晶化受电流极性与热边界条件影响，编程区域体积在接触尺寸大于10 nm后不再缩放。更大接触面积会增大器件间与周期间的变异性，但可能提升可靠性与耐久性。

Conclusion: 热电效应与丝状输运在相变存储操作中起关键作用，电流极性的选择可显著降低能耗与电流需求；编程区域存在尺寸缩放极限，而更大接触面积在引入变异性的同时有利于提高可靠性与耐久性。

Abstract: We performed a 2D finite-element electrothermal computational study of thermoelectric effects and filamentary electronic transport in Ge$_2$Sb$_2$Te$_5$ mushroom phase change memory cells during Reset and Set operations, accounting for spatial activation energy variations in amorphous Ge$_2$Sb$_2$Te$_5$ and phase-change dynamics. Reset operations with current going from the top electrode to the narrow 4 nm bottom electrode require $\sim$3x less energy and power, and $\sim$2x lower current to achieve the same Reset resistance, compared to the opposite polarity, due to thermoelectric effects. Filamentary conduction, electrical breakdown, thermal runaway, and local crystallization of amorphous Ge$_2$Sb$_2$Te$_5$ depend on current polarity and thermal boundary conditions, and determine the location, shape, and volume of the programming region, which may be significantly smaller than the semi-cylindrical mushroom region. The programming volume does not scale with contact dimensions larger than 10 nm. Larger contact areas introduce increased device-to-device and cycle-to-cycle variability due to filamentary conduction but are expected to lead to higher reliability and endurance.

### [19] [Calling the Brane Next Door: The Kaluza-Klein Tower as a Gravitational Information Channel](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09969)
*Karim Benakli*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种在高维框架中，通过引力在相邻膜世界（brane-world）之间进行通信的理论方案。Kaluza-Klein（KK）模式被重新解释为通信载波，其质量、波函数、膜重叠因子和传播相位共同构成一个多输入多输出（MIMO）信道矩阵。在阈值以上，KK模式作为额外的传播子信道开放，信息可编码在其中；而在阈值以下，通信仅通过无质量引力子维持。尽管该信号的产生和检测高度依赖模型且当前技术不可行，但信道结构本身是明确的，KK塔的谱与模态结构可能揭示隐藏世界的几何信息。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索仅通过引力（gravity）进行通信的可能性，即居住在相邻膜上的两个世界是否能够仅通过引力实现信息传递。这源于对额外维度和膜世界场景中引力传播的深入理解需求。

Method: 基于一个最小的高维框架（higher-dimensional framework），其中标准模型（Standard Model）场被局限在我们的膜上，而引力在体空间（bulk）中传播。通过推导膜到膜的引力子传播子（brane-to-brane graviton propagator），得到膜间链路的延迟转移核（retarded transfer kernel），并识别了从倏逝（evanescent）到传播（propagating）的Kaluza-Klein模式的转变。KK塔被赋予了通信载波的新角色，其各种参数定义了MIMO信道矩阵。

Result: 在第一个KK阈值以下，通信信道是有效四维的，仅由无质量引力子介导。在阈值以上，有质量KK模式作为额外的传播子信道（subchannels）开放，信息可编码在其占据模式、相对相位、到达时间结构以及普通信号变量中。紧致化（compactification）决定了KK质量、波函数、膜重叠因子和传播相位，共同定义了MIMO信道矩阵。在分辨模式极限（resolved-mode limit）下，KK塔产生近似并行的子信道，适用于容量界、注水法（water-filling）、有效秩（effective rank）和稀疏占用码（sparse occupancy codes）等标准信息论概念。

Conclusion: 相邻的膜世界可能在紧致空间（compact space）中与我们相隔微观距离，但由于唯一的共享相互作用是引力，因此仍保持隐藏。第一个可观测的迹象可能不是刻意发送的信息，而是KK塔本身的谱与模态结构，这将揭示邻近隐藏世界的部分几何信息。

Abstract: Could two worlds localised on neighbouring branes communicate through gravity alone? We investigate this question in a minimal higher-dimensional framework in which Standard Model fields are confined to our brane while gravity propagates through the bulk. From the brane-to-brane graviton propagator we derive the retarded transfer kernel of the inter-brane link and identify the transition from evanescent to propagating Kaluza-Klein modes. The central idea is to give the Kaluza-Klein tower a new role: not only as a spectrum of massive gravitational states, but as a set of communication carriers. Below the first KK threshold the channel is effectively four-dimensional and is mediated only by the massless graviton. Above threshold, massive KK modes open as additional propagating subchannels, and information may be encoded in their occupation pattern, relative phases, and arrival-time structure as well as in ordinary signal variables. The compactification determines the KK masses, wavefunctions, brane overlap factors, and propagation phases, which together define a multi-input multi-output (MIMO) channel matrix. In the resolved-mode limit, the tower yields approximate parallel subchannels, to which standard information-theoretic notions such as capacity bounds, water-filling, effective rank, and sparse occupancy codes apply. The production and detection of such signals are highly model-dependent and not assumed to be feasible with known technology. Nevertheless, the channel structure is well defined: a neighbouring brane-world could be separated from us by a microscopic distance in the compact space while remaining hidden because the only shared interaction is gravity. The first observable signature may not be a deliberate message, but the spectral and modal structure of the Kaluza-Klein tower itself, revealing partial information about the geometry of a nearby hidden world.

</details>


### [20] [Maximal Transcendentality of the Double-Scaled PCM](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09972)
*Evgeny Sobko*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文证明了大N主手征模型（Principal Chiral Model）在强耦合双标度区（double-scaling regime）中最大超越性（maximal transcendentality）到所有阶成立，并发现耦合常数自然平移后真空能展开系数仅由奇数zeta值（odd zeta values）的有理系数多项式构成，前35阶计算揭示了超越最大超越性的隐藏数论结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在前期工作引入的双标度区框架下，进一步严格证明该模型的真空能展开具有最大超越性，并探索展开系数中更深层的数论规律。

Method: 采用全阶（to all orders）证明方法，对强耦合大N主手征模型进行形式化分析；通过引入耦合常数的自然平移（natural shift of the coupling constant），将真空能展开系数表达为奇数zeta值的有理系数多项式；并具体计算了前35阶进行验证和数论规律探测。

Result: 最大超越性在所有阶上严格成立；真空能展开系数经耦合常数平移后纯由奇数zeta值的有理系数多项式构成；前35阶计算显示出超越最大超越性的额外数论正则性（number-theoretic regularities）。

Conclusion: 该模型在双标度区的真空能结构具有比最大超越性更丰富的隐藏数论结构，值得进一步研究。

Abstract: We prove, to all orders, maximal transcendentality of the strongly coupled large-N Principal Chiral Model in the double-scaling regime introduced in our earlier work. We also prove that, after a natural shift of the coupling constant, the coefficients of the vacuum-energy expansion are expressed purely as polynomials in odd zeta values with rational coefficients. The first 35 explicitly computed orders reveal further number-theoretic regularities, pointing to hidden structure beyond maximal transcendentality.

### [21] [Zeta Functions and the Superstring](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09977)
*Grant N. Remmen*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文计算了超弦振幅在固定动量转移下的梅林变换（Mellin transform），发现向前极限下该变换退化为黎曼ζ函数（Riemann zeta function），非零动量转移时构成ζ函数的形变，并由梅林变换导出了有效场论展开的闭合表达式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索超弦振幅（superstring amplitude）在能量域的梅林变换（Mellin transform）的数学结构，揭示其与黎曼ζ函数（Riemann zeta function）之间的深层联系，并建立与有效场论（effective field theory）展开的对应关系。

Method: 在固定动量转移下计算超弦振幅关于能量的梅林变换；分别在向前极限（forward limit, t=0）和一般动量转移（t≠0）情形下分析变换形式；利用整数次减除下的色散关系（dispersion relation）导出有效场论展开。

Result: 向前极限下梅林变换退化为黎曼ζ函数；非零动量转移时变换结果构成ζ函数的形变（deformation）；导出了有效场论在固定t下关于s逐阶展开的闭合形式表达式（closed-form expression）。

Conclusion: 超弦振幅的梅林变换与黎曼ζ函数存在深刻数学联系，其形变结构源自弦振幅的物理属性；该方法为在有限动量转移下导出有效场论展开提供了新的解析途径。

Abstract: The superstring amplitude's Mellin transform in energy is computed at fixed momentum transfer. In the forward limit, it is shown that this transformed amplitude reduces to the Riemann zeta function, while for $t\neq 0$ it represents a deformation of $ζ$. This object exhibits remarkable mathematical properties as a result of physical attributes of the string amplitude. For integer subtractions, the dispersion relation defined by the Mellin transform yields the effective field theory expansion of the string amplitude order by order in $s$ at finite $t$, for which a new closed-form expression is derived.

</details>


### [22] [Resonance and Differential Reduction of Feynman Integrals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09978)
*Ruth Britto,Thomas W. Grimm,Arno Hoefnagels*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出利用费曼积分（Feynman integrals）作为GKZ系统解的共振性质（resonance），构造缩减算子（reduction operators）来收缩费曼图的边，从而将微分方程系统约化至主积分（master integrals），并在一圈图、日出图（sunrise graphs）和香蕉图（banana graphs）上进行了具体构造。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 费曼积分作为GKZ偏微分方程系统的解通常呈现共振（resonance）现象，这种非一般性（non-genericity）会导致系统可约化至子系统。利用这一性质来系统性地缩减费曼图边数，从而降低微分方程系统的复杂度并识别主积分（master integrals）。

Method: 利用GKZ系统的共振性质构造缩减算子（reduction operators），这些微分算子（differential operators）能够收缩费曼图（Feynman graphs）的边，其作用自然与费曼图的切割（cuts）相容。保留的GKZ数据导出代数关系，从而识别一个完全约化至主积分（master integrals）的更小系统。

Result: 在一圈图（one-loop）、日出图（sunrise graphs）和香蕉图（banana graphs）上完成了缩减算子的构造，并讨论了物理运动学（physical kinematics）下的限制条件。发现缩减算子通常能同时移动传播子幂次（propagator powers）和时空维度（spacetime dimension），但某些组合可以隔离出纯维度移动（pure dimension shift）并同时收缩指定边。

Conclusion: 所构造的缩减算子可用于闭合给定积分的微分方程系统，并通过代数关系将系统约化至更小的主积分系统，为费曼积分的系统化计算提供了新途径。

Abstract: Feynman integrals may be viewed as generalized hypergeometric functions, and specifically as solutions of GKZ systems of partial differential equations that typically exhibit resonance. Resonance is a type of non-genericity implying reducibility to subsystems. We use this resonance to construct reduction operators, which are differential operators that can contract edges of Feynman graphs. Correspondingly, their action is naturally compatible with cuts of Feynman graphs. Reduction operators may be used to close the system of differential equations for a given integral. The remaining GKZ data lead to algebraic relations identifying a smaller system that is fully reduced to master integrals. We develop the construction for one-loop, sunrise and banana graphs and discuss restrictions to physical kinematics. While reduction operators can generally shift both propagator powers and spacetime dimension, certain combinations isolate a pure dimension shift together with contraction of a chosen edge.

</details>


### [23] [Where is tree-level heterotic string theory?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09980)
*Mathieu Boisvert,Waltraut Knop,Leonardo Rastelli*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在具有半最大超对称性（half-maximal supersymmetry）的十维理论中，延续树级S矩阵自举（tree-level S-matrix bootstrap）对量子引力的研究，发现线性雷吉轨迹（linear Regge trajectories）作为树级量子引力自举的稳健特征而涌现，并揭示了胶子扇区中表示-通道正定性与有效场论数据迹分解之间的张力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验在最大超对称性自举中发现的弦论式结构（string-like structures）是否在超对称性减弱及非平面规范扇区（non-planar gauge sectors）中仍然成立，从而验证树级S矩阵自举在量子引力中的普适性。

Method: 通过施加解析性（analyticity）、交叉对称性（crossing symmetry）、幺正性（unitarity）及雷吉有界性（Regge boundedness），对超引力与超杨-米尔斯（super Yang-Mills）的弱耦合紫外完备化（UV completions）空间施加约束。引力扇区中，允许区域的边界由单一线性雷吉轨迹上的极值振幅或其凸组合解释；胶子扇区则需处理非平面问题中表示-通道正定性与迹分解之间的冲突。

Result: 引力扇区中，允许区域边界主要由支持在单一线性雷吉轨迹上的极值振幅或此类振幅的凸组合（convex combinations）解释。胶子扇区中，非平面问题暴露出表示-通道正定性与有效场论数据迹分解（trace decomposition）之间的张力，阻碍了直接以引力耦合常数$G$或杨-米尔斯耦合常数$g_{\rm YM}$进行归一化。

Conclusion: 线性雷吉轨迹作为树级量子引力自举的稳健特征涌现；胶子/引力子耦合自举（coupled gluon/graviton bootstrap）可能是直接约束规范相互作用与引力相互作用相对强度的必要途径。

Abstract: We continue the tree-level S-matrix bootstrap program for quantum gravity, now in ten-dimensional theories with half-maximal supersymmetry. This setting includes the heterotic string and allows us to test whether the string-like structures found in the maximally supersymmetric bootstrap persist with less supersymmetry and in non-planar gauge sectors. Imposing analyticity, crossing symmetry, unitarity, and Regge boundedness, we constraint weakly coupled UV completions of supergravity and super Yang-Mills. In the gravitational sector, much of the boundary of the allowed region is explained by extremal amplitudes supported on a single linear Regge trajectory, or by convex combinations of such amplitudes. In the gluon sector, the non-planar problem reveals a tension between representation-channel positivity and the trace decomposition of the EFT data, obstructing a direct normalization by $G$ or $g_{\rm YM}$; a coupled gluon/graviton bootstrap may be necessary to directly constrain the relative strength of gauge and gravitational interactions. Overall, our results support the emergence of linear Regge trajectories as a robust feature of the tree-level quantum-gravity bootstrap.

</details>


### [24] [Testing F-theory GUTs with the Axiverse](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09982)
*Michael Nee,Mario Reig,Timo Weigand*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文证明，在F-理论大统一理论（F-theory GUTs）中，耦合到光子的轴子满足一个耦合-质量比上限 $g_{aγ}/m_a \leq C\, \frac{α_{\rm em}}{2π}\frac{1}{m_πf_π}$，该上界在有效理论的受控区域内无法被任意突破，且任何显著超出QCD轴子带的类轴子粒子（ALP）的发现都将证伪F-理论GUTs。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究F-理论大统一理论（F-theory GUTs）中轴子-光子耦合与质量比是否受到理论上界约束，以及这些约束对超出QCD轴子带的类轴子粒子（ALP）是否存在排除性预言。

Method: 在F-理论GUT框架中，通过超电荷通量（hypercharge flux）实现拓扑GUT对称性破缺，引入非普适全纯阈值修正（non-universal holomorphic threshold corrections）到规范动能函数，从而产生与QCD解耦但耦合到光子的ALP。通过分析D-瞬子（D-instantons）破缺ALP移位对称性的机制，计算轴子势能并推导耦合-质量比的上界。

Result: 导出了耦合-质量比 $g_{aγ}/m_a$ 的上界，其中QCD轴子饱和该上界（$C = \mathcal{O}(1)$）。所有非普适ALP的耦合-质量比均远低于QCD轴子预言。在具有大阈值修正的模型中，即使引入中间能标的不完整GUT多重态，该上界仍然成立。在几何区域（$\alpha'$ 展开受控）内，不存在参量上高于QCD轴子带的ALP。

Conclusion: F-理论GUTs在有效理论的受控区域内是“可证伪的”——任何显著高于QCD轴子带的ALP发现（如轴子诱导的宇宙双折射）都将排除F-理论GUTs在受控区域内的有效性。

Abstract: We show that axions coupled to photons in F-theory Grand Unified Theories (GUTs) satisfy the coupling-to-mass relation $g_{aγ}/m_a \leq C\, \frac{α_{\rm em}}{2π}\frac{1}{m_πf_π}$, with $C$ a calculable coefficient. This bound is saturated for the QCD axion with $C = \mathcal{O}(1)$ and holds in field theoretic and perturbative heterotic GUT constructions. In F-theory, topological GUT symmetry breaking by hypercharge flux introduces axion-like particles (ALPs) coupled to photons without coupling to QCD. These ALPs arise from the non-universal holomorphic threshold corrections to the gauge kinetic functions induced by the hypercharge flux. When gauge couplings approximately unify near the string scale, as required in phenomenologically viable models, the shift symmetries of these ALPs are broken by D-instantons whose action is controlled by the size of the threshold corrections to the gauge couplings. Small corrections imply unsuppressed instantons and heavy ALPs. We compute the resulting axion potentials and show that the coupling-to-mass ratio $g_{aγ}/m_a$ for every non-universal ALP lies well below the QCD axion prediction. We consider possible loopholes to this result -- some of which could lead to $C\gg 1$ -- and argue that none of them allows for $g_{aγ}/m_a$ to be arbitrarily above the QCD axion prediction within regions of control for the effective action. The bound persists in models with large threshold corrections, where new incomplete GUT multiplets at intermediate energy scales are required. As a result, in the geometric regime, where the $α'$ expansion is under control, no ALP parametrically above the QCD axion band exists. Our results make F-theory GUTs falsifiable: finding an ALP far above the QCD band, for example discovering axion-induced cosmic birefringence, rules out F-theory GUTs in regimes of control of the effective theory.

</details>


### [25] [Ramond from Random: Weil-Petersson Volumes for Super-Riemann surfaces with NS Boundaries and R Punctures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09990)
*Clifford V. Johnson*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文利用随机矩阵模型（random matrix model）统一处理超黎曼曲面（supersymmetric Riemann surfaces）模空间中的Neveu-Schwarz（NS）边界和Ramond（R）穿孔，首次给出了包含R穿孔的Weil-Petersson（WP）体积的闭式公式，并揭示了此前未知的谱曲线（spectral curve）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 包含Ramond（R）穿孔的超黎曼曲面模空间的Weil-Petersson（WP）体积，因其超共形结构退化带来的计算复杂性，在微分几何与代数几何方法下难以处理，相关结果较少，且描述R穿孔的谱曲线（spectral curve）尚未被找到。

Method: 采用随机矩阵模型（random matrix model）方法，将Neveu-Schwarz（NS）边界和Ramond（R）穿孔置于统一框架下处理；利用近期发展的技术计算闭式公式；并通过拓扑递归（topological recursion）从谱曲线重新推导WP体积。

Result: 给出了包含2m个R穿孔和n个NS边界的WP体积$V^{(2m)}_{g,n}(\{b_i\})$的多种闭式公式；发现了体积及其子扇区之间若干显著关系；展示了此前缺失的谱曲线。

Conclusion: 随机矩阵模型方法能有效统一处理NS和R两种扇区，填补了R穿孔情形下谱曲线缺失的空白，并验证了拓扑递归在推导WP体积中的适用性。

Abstract: The Weil-Petersson (WP) volumes of the (compactified) moduli space of ${N}=1$ supersymmetric Riemann surfaces with Neveu-Schwarz (NS) boundaries are frequently discussed in the literature. Such surfaces can also have marked points called Ramond (R) punctures, where the superconformal structure degenerates. Computing the volumes when these R punctures are included is more challenging for the usual differential and algebraic geometry approaches, and they are therefore less well explored. In particular, the spectral curve describing the inclusion of R punctures is apparently unknown, so far. However, the right random matrix model approach can handle the NS and~R sectors on an equal footing. Such a construction is presented, showing how to use a recently developed technique to readily compute many closed-form formulae for $V^{(2m)}_{g,n}(\{b_i\})$, the WP volumes for genus $g$ with $n$ NS-boundaries of geodesic lengths $b_i$ ($i{=}1,\ldots,n$), and $2m$ R-punctures. Several striking relations between volumes (and subsectors thereof) emerge naturally in this approach. Moreover, the hitherto missing spectral curve is presented, and its use for (re-)deriving the $V^{(2m)}_{g,n}(\{b_i\})$ is demonstrated by using topological recursion.

</details>


### [26] [Anomaly-driven evaporation endpoints of a two-dimensional regular black hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09983)
*Damien A. Easson*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过将四维微扰物质进行球面约化（spherical reduction）得到与膨胀子耦合的二维理论，并利用该理论与Fabbri-Farese-Navarro-Salas（FFN）膨胀子耦合反常模型，重新研究了Bardeen-like黑洞的晚期反作用端点问题。结果表明，在有限半径的静止分支上混合方程强制$J'(r_\infty)=0$且$r_\infty=\sqrt{2}\,\ell$；而在有限半径零分支上，除$p=2$的边界情况外，所有幂律分支均被排除，该幸存分支遵循更强的态尾衰减条件，呈现出残余物（remnant-like）特征或高度约束的软零（soft-null）替代方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 四维微扰物质的球面约化实际得到的是与膨胀子（dilaton）耦合的二维理论，而非通常假定的最小耦合共形物质。这一区别表明，Barenboim、Frolov和Kunstatter研究的规则二维Bardeen-like黑洞在考虑量子反作用后的晚期端点问题值得重新审视。

Method: 将Polyakov量子扇区替换为FFN膨胀子耦合反常模型，推导相应的半经典场方程，并对有限半径处的渐近允许晚期分支进行分类分析。

Result: 对于任何具有有限非零共形因子的静止有限半径分支，晚期混合方程强制$J'(r_\infty)=0$且$r_\infty=\sqrt{2}\,\ell$，该结果与局域膨胀子反常约定无关。有限半径零分支中，排除普通强宇宙审查恢复指数零边界；除$p=2$的边界情况外，$p>1$的通用幂律分支$e^{2ρ}\sim v^{-p}$同样被排除。在FFN模型中，$p=2$分支携带有限仿射通量，要求更强的态尾衰减$s_φ=O(v^{-2})$。

Conclusion: 自然的有限半径结果具有残余物（remnant-like）特征，而幸存零分支则是高度约束的软零（soft-null）替代方案。

Abstract: Spherical reduction of four-dimensional minimally coupled matter yields a two-dimensional theory with dilaton-coupled matter rather than minimally coupled conformal matter. We use this distinction to revisit the backreacted late-time endpoint problem for the regular two-dimensional Bardeen-like black hole considered by Barenboim, Frolov, and Kunstatter. Replacing the Polyakov quantum sector by the dilaton-coupled anomaly model of Fabbri, Farese, and Navarro-Salas (FFN), we derive the corresponding semiclassical field equations and classify the asymptotically allowed late branches at finite radius. For any quiescent finite-radius branch with finite nonzero conformal factor, the late-time mixed equation enforces $J'(r_\infty)=0$, and hence $r_\infty=\sqrt{2}\,\ell$, independently of the local dilaton-anomaly convention. For finite-radius null branches satisfying the stated state-tail assumptions, the ordinary strong-cosmic-censorship-restoring exponential null boundary is excluded. Generic power-law branches $e^{2ρ}\sim v^{-p}$ with $p>1$ are likewise excluded, except for the borderline case $p=2$, which is the only remaining null loophole of this type. In the FFN model, the settled realization of this loophole carries finite affine flux and requires the stronger state-tail decay $s_φ=O(v^{-2})$. The natural finite-radius outcome is remnant-like, while the surviving null branch is a highly constrained soft-null alternative.

### [27] [Bootstrap Cone of the Multicritical Deconfined Quantum Critical Point](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09985)
*Zhijin Li,Tinhong Shen*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过共形自举（conformal bootstrap）方法为退禁闭量子临界点（DQCP）的多临界性（multicriticality）场景提供了有力证据，发现QMC和模糊球数据与自举锥高度一致，支持DQCP是一个带有相关SO(5)单态标量场的幺正不动点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 退禁闭量子临界点（DQCP）作为超越朗道-金兹堡-威尔逊（Landau-Ginzburg-Wilson）范式的非常规相变典型例子，其性质长期存在争议——伪临界性（pseudo-criticality）与多临界性（multicriticality）两种解释相互对立，亟需判定性证据。

Method: 采用共形自举（conformal bootstrap）方法，结合大规模量子蒙特卡洛（Quantum Monte Carlo, QMC）数据和模糊球（fuzzy sphere）数据，利用导航算法（navigator algorithm）定位自举锥（bootstrap cone）的顶点并提取极值解，进而比较算子乘积展开（operator product expansions, OPEs）系数和高阶谱。

Result: 自举锥与QMC数据高度吻合；自举解与模糊球数据在OPE系数及高阶谱上展现出显著一致性；自举锥将QMC和模糊球数据统一纳入一个带有相关SO(5)单态标量场的幺正共形场论（CFT）框架中。

Abstract: The deconfined quantum critical point (DQCP) provides a prominent example of the unconventional phase transitions beyond the Landau-Ginzburg-Wilson paradigm and its nature has been controversial for decades. The DQCP has been extensively studied and the results lead to two opposite scenarios with pseudo-criticality or multicriticality. The pseudo-criticality is a prevailing scenario of DQCP which interprets the approximately scale invariant numerical results with the walking behavior near complex fixed points. In contrast, the multicriticality scenario conjectures the DQCP is a unitary fixed point with a relevant $SO(5)$ singlet scalar. In this work we provide substantial evidence for the multicriticality scenario using conformal bootstrap. We start with the observation that the large scale Quantum Monte Carlo (QMC) results nearly saturate the bootstrap bounds. After imposing suitable sparseness condition the bootstrap bound forms a sharp cone in the three-dimensional parameter space. The bootstrap cone is close to the QMC data. We use the navigator algorithm to locate the apex of the cone and extract the extremal solutions. We find striking consistencies between the bootstrap solutions and the fuzzy sphere data of DQCP, including the coefficients in the operator product expansions (OPEs) and the higher spectrum! The bootstrap cone unifies the QMC and the fuzzy sphere data into a unitary conformal field theory with a relevant $SO(5)$ singlet scalar, thus strongly supporting the multicriticality scenario of DQCP. The agreement between the conformal bootstrap, QMC and fuzzy sphere results is a surprise towards solving DQCP and decoding the profound phase diagram of the two-dimensional quantum magnets.

### [28] [On BPS Branes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09996)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超对称BPS态在超引力与量子引力理论中具有基础性地位，但并非所有BPS电荷都能对应存在BPS黑膜（BPS black-brane）吸引子解。因此，需要系统地区分BPS膜电荷锥（$C_{\rm BPS-B}$）与BPS黑膜电荷锥（$C_{\rm BPS-BB}$），并阐明二者的物理含义与对偶关系。

Method: 基于超引力有效场论（supergravity effective field theory），通过红外极限下的BPS黑膜吸引子解（attractor solutions）定义并区分两类电荷锥，并利用电-磁配对（electric-magnetic pairing）提出对偶性猜想。

Result: 定义了$C_{\rm BPS-B}$（BPS膜电荷锥）与$C_{\rm BPS-BB}$（BPS黑膜电荷锥）两个概念；提出了两个核心猜想：1）在任意超对称量子引力理论中，$C_{\rm BPS-BB}$中的整数荷态一定由BPS态实现；2）当$C_{\rm BPS-B}$不依赖于模场时，它是$C_{\rm BPS-BB}$在电-磁配对下的对偶锥。

Conclusion: 本文为超引力与量子引力中的BPS态存在性及电荷锥对偶性提供了猜想与初步证据，为理解BPS谱的完整结构及其与黑膜吸引子解的关系奠定了基础。

Abstract: We study supersymmetric BPS branes (BPS-B) in supergravity theories. Some of these states are anticipated by BPS black-brane (BPS-BB) solutions of supergravity. In particular, we define and distinguish the cone generated by BPS branes from the subcone of charges that admit BPS black-brane attractor solutions in the infrared limit of the supergravity effective field theory. We denote these cones by $C_{\rm BPS-B}$ and $C_{\rm BPS-BB}$, respectively. We conjecture that, in any supersymmetric theory of quantum gravity, every integrally charged state lying in $C_{\rm BPS-BB}$ is realized by a BPS state in the spectrum. Furthermore, we conjecture and present evidence that when $C_{\rm BPS-B}$ is moduli independent, it can be determined as the cone dual to the $C_{\rm BPS-BB}$ under the electric-magnetic pairing.

Abstract: We derive new 3d $\mathcal{N}=2$ dualities with $\mathrm{U}(N)$ gauge groups involving pairs of two-index tensors interacting through a quartic superpotential, (anti)-fundamentals and possibly an adjoint. ### [31] [Hawking--Page Universality, Thermodynamic Dipoles and Categorical Defects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10680)
*Emilio Torrente-Lujan*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文利用公共热力学矢量场（common thermodynamic vector field）重新审视了霍金-佩奇相变（Hawking--Page transition），指出Davies点和Hawking--Page点的绕数（winding number）分别为-1和+1，构成零总荷但非零有符号一阶矩的配对；经Davies标度归一化后给出普适比率C_S和C_T，并在多种AdS黑洞背景下验证了该构造，最后提出了面向范畴性或非可逆对称扇区的缺陷分辨版本（defect-resolved version）。

Method: 引入公共热力学矢量场（common thermodynamic vector field），通过求解其零点定位Davies点和Hawking--Page点，并计算其绕数（winding number）；再用Davies标度（Davies scales）对一阶矩进行归一化，得到普适比率C_S和C_T；将该构造推广至Schwarzschild--AdS、大正则系综下的Reissner--Nordström--AdS、任意维荷电非旋转黑洞以及固定角速度的Kerr--AdS等多种AdS黑洞背景。

Result: 在基本AdS分支（elementary AdS branch）中，Davies点和Hawking--Page点的绕数分别为w_D=-1和w_HP=+1，两者总电荷为零但非零有符号一阶矩（signed first moment）；经Davies标度归一化后给出普适比率，四维情形下C_S=2、C_T=2/√3-1；约化几何（reduced geometry）给出的势垒（barrier）在四维中为B=1/3，在一般d维中为B(d)=1/[(d-1)(d-3)]。

Conclusion: 该拓扑构造在多种AdS黑洞背景下均成立，验证了其普适性；最后提出面向范畴性（categorical）或非可逆对称扇区（non-invertible symmetry sectors）的缺陷分辨版本（defect-resolved version）作为进一步推广方向。

Abstract: We reconsider the Hawking--Page transition using the common thermodynamic vector field whose zeros include the Davies and Hawking--Page points. In the elementary AdS branch their winding numbers are $w_{\rm D}=-1$ and $w_{\rm HP}=+1$, so the pair has zero total charge but a non-zero signed first moment. After normalization by the Davies scales this moment gives the familiar universal ratios $C_S$ and $C_T$; in four dimensions $C_S=2$ and $C_T=2/\sqrt{3}-1$. We check the construction for Schwarzschild--AdS, grand-canonical Reissner--Nordström--AdS, charged non-rotating black holes in arbitrary dimension, and Kerr--AdS at fixed angular velocity. The same reduced geometry gives a barrier $B=1/3$ in four dimensions and $B(d)=1/[(d-1)(d-3)]$. Finally we propose a formulation involving a defect-resolved version for categorical or non-invertible symmetry sectors.

### [32] [Chiral Plasma under Strong Magnetic Fields: A Holographic Analysis of Transport Phenomena](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10689)
*Michael Lublinsky,Hadas Tzarfati*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过全阶梯度重求和（all-order gradient resummation）和全息对偶（holographic duality）方法，系统研究了手征等离子体（chiral plasma）在任意强恒定磁场与弱电场中的输运现象，计算了十三个依赖于动量与磁场的输运系数函数，并重新审视了负磁电阻（negative magnetoresistance）和手征磁波（chiral magnetic waves）等效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 手征等离子体存在于早期宇宙原初等离子体、重离子碰撞产生的夸克-胶子等离子体以及狄拉克和外尔半金属中，其核心特征是手征反常（chiral anomaly）导致轴矢流不守恒，并涌现出反常诱导的输运现象。现有研究多局限于流体力学极限，亟需建立超越该极限、适用于任意强度磁场的理论框架。

Method: 采用全阶梯度重求和技术推导电矢流和轴矢流（axial current）的本构关系（constitutive relations），引入十三个依赖于动量与磁场的输运系数函数。利用全息对偶方法，在探针极限下以 Schwarzschild–AdS$_5$ 时空中的 $U(1)_V \times U(1)_A$ Maxwell–Chern–Simons 理论作为现实等离子体的理论实验室，计算这些输运系数。

Result: 得到了在任意强恒定磁场和弱电场条件下电矢流与轴矢流的本构关系，并计算了全部十三个输运系数函数。这些系数同时依赖于动量和磁场强度。基于此框架，重新分析了负磁电阻和手征磁波现象。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了超越朴素流体力学极限（naive hydrodynamic limit）的手征等离子体输运理论，证明全息方法可有效处理任意强度磁场下的反常输运问题，为非微扰区域的输运现象提供了统一的理论描述。

Abstract: Chiral plasma appears in several areas of physics, historically starting from primordial plasma in the early Universe, then in quark-gluon plasma produced in heavy ion collisions, and, more recently, in Dirac and Weyl semimetals. The major signature of the plasma is the non-conservation of the axial current due to the chiral anomaly and the emergence of new, anomaly-induced transport phenomena. In this paper, we study the plasma exposed to arbitrarily strong constant magnetic and weak electric fields. Employing all-order gradient resummation, we write down constitutive relations for electric and axial currents parameterized by thirteen momentum- and magnetic- field-dependent transport coefficient functions. The latter are computed utilizing a theoretical lab for a realistic plasma, namely a holographic $U(1)_V \times U(1)_A$ Maxwell--Chern--Simons theory in Schwarzschild--AdS$_5$, in the probe limit. As an application, we revisit the phenomena of negative magnetoresistance and chiral magnetic waves, beyond the naive hydrodynamic limit.

</details>


### [33] [Pair creation amplitudes for a real scalar field coupled to a time-dependent surface in d+1 dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10800)
*C. D. Fosco,B. C. Guntsche*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了一个实标量场（real scalar field）在经历时间依赖形变的表面附近，在狄利克雷型边界条件（Dirichlet-like boundary conditions）下的粒子对产生现象。将表面偏离无限平面的展开保留至四阶，给出了真空中粒子对发射率的角分布，该分布取决于表面的几何与动力学以及发射对的动量。验证了领头阶贡献与有效作用量（effective action）虚部所得结果的相容性，并阐明了在四阶时，双粒子对通道（two-pair channel）的开张如何修正单粒子对概率与有效作用量虚部之间的关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前已有研究通过有效作用量虚部来理解动态边界下的粒子产生，但尚未系统考虑高阶（四阶）修正以及多粒子对通道对概率幅的贡献。本文旨在填补这一空白，明确高阶修正下概率与有效作用量虚部关系的变化。

Method: 将表面形变相对于无限平面进行展开，保留至四阶项，并采用狄利克雷型边界条件。通过量子场论中的散射振幅计算，分析真空-粒子对过程的发射率的角分布与表面几何、动力学以及发射对动量的依赖关系。

Result: 给出了真空中粒子对发射率随角度、表面几何与动力学参数以及发射对动量变化的表达式。验证了领头阶结果与有效作用量虚部方法的一致性；发现当考虑四阶项时，双粒子对通道的开张使得单粒子对概率与有效作用量虚部之间的简单关系发生修正。

Conclusion: 动态形变表面附近的实标量场中，粒子对产生率的高阶修正与低阶结果存在结构性的差异，主要体现在双粒子对通道的影响上。该工作为理解动态边界条件下多粒子过程的量子场论机制提供了更完整的框架。

Abstract: We study the pair creation phenomenon for a real scalar field $\varphi$ in the presence of a surface that undergoes time-dependent deformations, while imposing Dirichlet-like boundary conditions. Including terms up to fourth order in the departure of the surface from an infinite plane, we present results for the angular dependence of the emission rate for the vacuum-to-pair process as a function of the geometry and the dynamics of the surface, as well as of the momenta of the emitted pair. We check the consistency of the leading contribution with previous results obtained from the imaginary part of the effective action, and clarify how the relation between exclusive probabilities and the imaginary part of the effective action is modified at fourth order by the opening of a two-pair channel.

### [34] [On Calabi-Yau Threefolds For Unified LVS Inflation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10850)
*Pramod Shukla*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个统一框架，通过单个卡拉比-丘（Calabi-Yau, CY）三维流形上的不同定向体（orientifold）实现三种基于Kähler模的暴涨模型（纤维暴涨、多瞬子暴涨和（环）吹胀暴涨），并在Kreuzer-Skarke数据库中针对 h^{1,1} ≤ 6 的几何结构进行了系统扫描，发现了满足条件的候选CY三维流形及其数量分布。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 所需CY三维流形需具备K3或T^4纤维化结构、两个对角del Pezzo除子（divisor）以及一个定义为P^1在T^2上纤维化的“Wilson”除子。研究对Kreuzer-Skarke数据库中 h^{1,1}（CY）从1到6的CY几何结构进行详细扫描，分析了约100,000个CY几何及约一百万个toric除子的拓扑结构。

Result: 在 h^{1,1}(CY) ≤ 4 范围内，仅发现2个CY三维流形满足要求；在 h^{1,1}(CY) = 5 和 h^{1,1}(CY) = 6 时，分别发现14个和45个候选CY几何结构。

Conclusion: 上述候选CY三维流形可用于弦论框架下的宇宙学模型构建，特别是Kähler模暴涨模型的进一步应用与拓展。

Abstract: Fibre inflation, Poly-instanton inflation and (Loop) Blow-up inflation are among the most popular Kähler moduli based inflationary models realized in the standard LARGE volume scenarios (LVS). In this article, we present a unified framework in which all these three LVS inflationary models can be realized by using (different orientifolds of) a single Calabi-Yau (CY) threefold. In fact, the desired CY threefold needs to have a K3- or ${\mathbb T}^4$-fibration structure along with two diagonal del Pezzo divisors, and a so-called `Wilson' divisor which corresponds to a surface realized as a ${\mathbb P}^1$ fibration over ${\mathbb T}^2$s. For classification purpose, we perform a detailed scan of the CY geometries with $1 \leq h^{1,1}({\rm CY}) \leq 6$ that arise from the triangulation of the four-dimensional reflexive polytopes of the Kreuzer-Skarke database. In this regard, after scanning around 100,000 CY geometries and the corresponding topologies of around a million of toric divisors, we find two CY threefolds satisfying these requirements for $1 \leq h^{1,1}({\rm CY}) \leq 4$, while there are 14 and 45 candidate CY geometries for $h^{1,1}({\rm CY}) = 5$ and $h^{1,1}({\rm CY}) = 6$, respectively. We discuss the extended applications of such CY threefolds for cosmological model building in string theoretic frameworks.

### [35] [Spacetime from Operator Algebras](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10924)
*Vyshnav Mohan,Larus Thorlacius*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于量子场算子代数（operator algebras）重建时空几何（spacetime metric and curvature）的新框架，在牛顿常数趋于零的极限下，将完整非线性爱因斯坦方程（Einstein equations）表达为算子代数语言，并利用随机矩阵理论（random matrix theory）完成从III型冯·诺依曼代数（type III von Neumann algebra）到I型代数（type I von Neumann algebra）的扩充，进而将代数维度与黑洞熵（Bekenstein-Hawking entropy）及其对数修正关联起来。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统上，从量子引力理论中涌现出经典时空几何的机制尚不清晰，Jacobson的熵-面积推导虽提供了联系，但依赖于Bekenstein-Hawking熵的面积律。本文旨在发展一种无需熵-面积假设、直接从算子代数出发重建时空几何并导出爱因斯坦方程的新方法，同时为判断量子理论是否具有涌现引力描述提供判据。

Method: 在牛顿常数趋于零的极限下，使用量子化物质场（quantized matter fields）的算子代数重构度规（metric）和曲率张量（curvature tensor）。通过添加模哈密顿量（modular Hamiltonian）扩充III型冯·诺依曼代数；对该扩充代数施以随机矩阵理论完备化（random matrix theory completion）并执行系综平均（ensemble averaging），最终得到I型冯·诺依曼代数。

Result: 该框架成功将完整非线性爱因斯坦方程表达为算子代数语言，无需依赖Bekenstein-Hawking熵的面积律。在永恒黑洞（eternal black hole）情形下，得到的I型代数维度等于Bekenstein-Hawking熵加上普适对数修正。此外，边界理论（boundary theory）中探针算子（probe operators）的复杂度（complexity）可作为体时空半经典有效场论（bulk semiclassical effective field theory）有效性的一种诊断。

Conclusion: 该工作为时空几何从算子代数中涌现提供了一种新的形式化框架，并建立了从全息理论（holographic theory）在有限N下的离散谱到半经典算子代数的非微扰修正模型。该框架同时可作为判据，用于判定给定量子理论的半经典极限是否存在涌现引力描述。

Abstract: Under suitable assumptions, geometric objects such as the spacetime metric and curvature tensor can be reconstructed from the algebra of operators of quantized matter fields in the limit of vanishing Newton's constant. In this framework, the full non-linear Einstein equations can be expressed in the language of operator algebras, extending Jacobson's derivation without invoking the area law for Bekenstein-Hawking entropy. These assumptions can then be used as a criterion for determining whether the semiclassical limit of a given quantum theory admits an emergent gravitational description. Going in the other direction, the discrete spectrum of a holographic theory at finite N can be modelled by adding non-perturbative corrections to semiclassical operator algebras. The type III von Neumann algebra that arises in the vanishing Newton's constant limit can be enlarged by adjoining its modular Hamiltonian. A random matrix theory completion of this enlarged algebra, followed by ensemble averaging, results in a type I von Neumann algebra whose minimal projectors approximate those of the underlying microstates. In the case of an eternal black hole, the dimension of the type I algebra equals the Bekenstein-Hawking entropy with universal logarithmic corrections. The complexity of probe operators in the boundary theory provides a diagnostic of the validity of the corresponding bulk semiclassical effective field theory.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 首先回顾已知解的形式；然后分析保证超对称性的约束条件，并显式计算时空的Killing旋子；接着利用BPS界饱和条件推导黑洞质量与热力学量；最后将极端解推广到含宇宙学常数的情形。

Result: 证明了该带电加速黑洞的超对称解恰好饱和BPS界；基于此结果计算了黑洞的质量，并完成了热力学分析；成功将极端解推广至包含宇宙学常数的一般情形。

Conclusion: 该超对称加速黑洞解是BPS态，其质量与热力学可由超对称性完全确定；引入宇宙学常数的推广进一步丰富了超引力中精确解的分类。

Abstract: We examine supersymmetry of charged and accelerating black holes embedded in a Bertotti-Robinson universe, in the context of $N=2$, $D=4$ supergravity. After a review of the solution, we study the constraints that guarantee supersymmetry and explicitly compute the Killing spinors of the spacetime. We show that the supersymmetric solution saturates the BPS bound, and we use this result to compute the mass of the black hole and to analyze the thermodynamics of the solution. Finally, we present a generalization of the extremal solution to include the cosmological constant.

### [37] [Analytic Derivation of Vertical Chromaticity in the Fermilab Muon $g{-}2$ Storage Ring](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09903)
*Eremey Valetov,Kyoko Makino,Martin Berz*

Main category: physics.acc-ph

TL;DR: 本文推导了费米实验室μ子g-2存储环的垂直色度（vertical chromaticity）ξ_y的闭合解析表达式。通过哈密顿量泰勒展开与逐阶运动方程积分，获得了均匀磁偶极子（DI）和组合功能偶极-静电四极子（DIQ）元件的垂直二阶像差。将各元件映射沿周期色散轨道合成，得到了连续环DIQ360模型垂直色度的闭合形式表达式，其函数形式与同一环的水平结果（参见参考文献）直接类似。与COSY INFINITY微分代数计算的比较表明，在μ子g-2静电四极电压V_esq ∈ [10, 26] kV范围内，三种环模型（DIQ360闭合形式及模块化DIEQ_ON、DIEQ）的一致度达到10^{-11}量级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 此前工作中已获得同一存储环的水平色度（horizontal chromaticity）闭合解析表达式，但垂直色度的解析结果尚缺。垂直色度的精确解析表达对于理解μ子g-2存储环的束流动力学特性、优化环设计及提高实验精度具有重要意义。

Method: 采用哈密顿量（Hamiltonian）泰勒多项式展开方法，对动力学变量进行展开并逐阶（order by order）积分运动方程。分别推导了均匀磁偶极子（DI）和多功能偶极-静电四极子（DIQ）元件的垂直二阶像差（vertical second-order aberrations），并将各元件映射沿周期色散轨道（periodic dispersion orbit）组合，得到连续环DIQ360模型的垂直色度闭合形式表达式。

Result: 获得了垂直色度ξ_y的闭合解析表达式，其函数形式与同环水平色度结果直接类似。与COSY INFINITY微分代数（differential-algebra）计算进行对比验证，在μ子g-2静电四极电压V_esq ∈ [10, 26] kV范围内，三种环模型（DIQ360闭合形式以及DIEQ_ON、DIEQ逐元件组合）之间的一致度达到10^{-11}量级。

Conclusion: 本文成功推导了费米实验室μ子g-2存储环垂直色度的闭合解析表达式，数值验证表明该表达式具有极高的精度（10^{-11}量级）。该结果在函数形式上与同环的水平分析结果一致，验证了分析方法的普适性和可靠性，为环设计与高精度实验提供了理论工具。

Abstract: We derive the vertical chromaticity $ξ_y$ of the Fermilab Muon g-2 storage ring in closed analytic form. Expanding the Hamiltonian as a Taylor polynomial in the dynamical variables and integrating the equations of motion order by order, we obtain the vertical second-order aberrations of the homogeneous magnetic dipole ($\mathtt{DI}$) and the combined-function dipole-and-electrostatic-quadrupole element ($\mathtt{DIQ}$) used in the muon $g{-}2$ ring. Composing the per-element maps over the periodic dispersion orbit yields a closed-form expression for the vertical chromaticity $\xichromy$ of the continuous-ring $\mathtt{DIQ360}$ model, in direct functional analogy with the horizontal result of our earlier work on the same ring (Ref.~\refcite{ChromCPO11}). Comparison against COSY INFINITY differential-algebra computation shows agreement at the $10^{-11}$ level across all three ring models ($\mathtt{DIQ360}$ closed form and the modular $\mathtt{DIEQ\_ON}$, $\mathtt{DIEQ}$ via per-element composition) for muon $g{-}2$ electrostatic-quadrupole (ESQ) voltages $\Vesq \in [10, 26]\,\mathrm{kV}$.

### [38] [Random Matrix Theory for Chaotic Wave Scattering and Transport](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10957)
*Yan V. Fyodorov,Dmitry V. Savin*

Main category: nlin.CD

TL;DR: 本文综述了基于随机矩阵理论（random matrix theory）的混沌波散射与开放系统输运方法，从非厄米哈密顿量（non-Hermitian Hamiltonian）出发，系统讨论了散射矩阵、反应矩阵、时间延迟和复共振等探针，强调由对称性、开放性和通道耦合控制的普适统计规律，并涵盖非微扰方法与普适结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 混沌波散射与输运的普适统计规律（universal statistics）是开放系统动力学的核心问题。本文旨在系统梳理随机矩阵方法（random matrix approaches）在该领域的进展，弥补微扰方法在处理强耦合与有限吸收等情形时的不足。

Method: 采用有效非厄米哈密顿量（non-Hermitian Hamiltonian）框架，通过散射矩阵（scattering matrix）、反应矩阵（reaction matrix）、时间延迟（time delays）和复共振（complex resonances）等互补探针分析开放混沌动力学。以最大熵（maximum-entropy）描述固定能量散射，并扩展至能量关联、共振与本征函数统计等领域。

Result: 揭示了开放量子与波混沌系统中由对称性（symmetry）、开放程度（openness）和通道耦合（channel coupling）控制的普适统计行为。非微扰方法（non-perturbative methods）能够有效捕捉有限吸收（finite absorption）诱导的波混沌现象以及能量关联等复杂特征。

Conclusion: 随机矩阵理论为开放混沌系统提供了统一的非微扰分析框架，其普适结构广泛适用于量子输运（quantum transport）和波混沌（wave-chaotic）现象，对理解有限吸收等实际效应具有重要指导意义。

Abstract: We review random matrix approaches to chaotic wave scattering and transport in open systems. Starting from the effective non-Hermitian Hamiltonian formulation, we discuss the scattering matrix, reaction matrix, time delays, and complex resonances as complementary probes of open chaotic dynamics. We emphasize universal statistics governed by symmetry, openness, and channel coupling. Topics include the maximum-entropy description of fixed-energy scattering and its applications to quantum transport, energy correlations, resonance and eigenfunction statistics, and selected wave-chaotic phenomena induced by finite absorption. The focus throughout is on non-perturbative methods and universal structures underlying open quantum and wave chaotic systems.
