### [39] [Geometric Matching of Local Static Regions in Cosmological Spacetimes with an Evolving Lapse](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09945)
*Seokcheon Lee*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过Israel拼接条件（Israel junction conditions）研究广义宇宙学时间（GCT）框架下局部静态时空区域（如Schwarzschild内部）能否嵌入具有时间依赖的lapse函数的膨胀宇宙学背景中，发现可拼接条件等价于GCT背景运动方程，应解释为几何一致性条件（GCC）而非新动力学方程，从而阐明局部静止引力系统与变化宇宙学时间归一化之间的兼容性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 广义宇宙学时间（GCT）框架通过修改lapse函数拓展了标准FLRW描述，但这类偏离ΛCDM的构造必须与局部引力和实验室物理的观测稳定性兼容。在标量-张量理论（scalar-tensor theories）中，这种兼容性通常依赖动力学屏蔽机制（dynamical screening mechanisms）。本文旨在检验局部静态时空能否无需薄壳（thin shell）条件而一致地嵌入具有时间依赖lapse的宇宙学背景中。

Method: 将静态Schwarzschild内部嵌入膨胀的GCT-FLRW外部，利用Israel拼接条件（Israel junction conditions）确定允许这种匹配的背景膨胀类别，并通过外曲率（extrinsic curvature）连续性推导Friedmann型关系。

Result: 外曲率的连续性导出一个Friedmann型关系，该关系与GCT背景运动方程一致。该关系应被解释为几何一致性条件（GCC），而非新的动力学方程。拼接本身不引入新动力学，但提供了一个GCC，使具有固定局部时钟（local clocks）的区域可嵌入具有演化lapse的宇宙学时空中。

Conclusion: 该分析阐明了局部静态引力系统如何在不改变局部物理标准描述的前提下，与不同于局部原时（proper time）的宇宙学时间归一化保持兼容。

Abstract: The generalized cosmological time (GCT) framework introduces a modified lapse function, N(t)\propto a^{b/4}, as a geometric extension of the standard FLRW description. Like other departures from $Λ$CDM, such constructions must remain compatible with the observed stability of local gravitational and laboratory physics. In scalar--tensor theories, this compatibility is usually achieved through dynamical screening mechanisms that suppress additional degrees of freedom in dense environments. In this work, we examine whether a locally static spacetime region can be consistently embedded within a cosmological background described by a time-dependent lapse. By embedding a static Schwarzschild interior into an expanding GCT--FLRW exterior, the Israel junction conditions are used to determine the class of background expansions that admit such a matching in the absence of a thin shell. The continuity of the extrinsic curvature yields a Friedmann-type relation that coincides with the GCT background equations of motion. This relation should be interpreted not as a new dynamical equation, but as a geometric consistency condition (GCC) associated with the matching of the two spacetime regions. In this sense, the junction does not introduce new dynamics, but provides a GCC under which a region with fixed local clocks can be embedded in a cosmological spacetime with an evolving lapse. Therefore, the analysis clarifies how locally static gravitational systems can remain compatible with a cosmological time normalization that differs from that of local proper time while preserving the standard description of local physics.

</details>


### [40] [Static Spherically Symmetric Chaplygin and Polytropic Fluid Solutions in Teleparallel $F(T)$ Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10100)
*Alexandre Landry*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在协变远距平行 F(T) 引力框架下，利用非线性 Chaplygin 和多变流体构造了静态球对称时空的精确解，并发展了一套通用重建程序，得到了致密天体、黑洞、虫洞等多种分支解，系统分析了其视界、喉结构、奇点、能量条件与稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 广义相对论（General Relativity, GR）之外的非线性引力理论需要新的解析解框架，而协变远距平行 F(T) 引力（covariant teleparallel F(T) gravity）在球对称时空中的精确解构造仍缺乏统一方法。

Method: 采用协变余标架/自旋联络（covariant coframe/spin-connection, CSC）形式，推导场方程和守恒律；针对幂律（power-law）构型，发展通用重建程序（reconstruction procedure），系统确定 F(T) 模型与各类物质状态方程（equation of state）的相容解。

Result: 获得常量半径、致密天体、黑洞（black-hole-like, BH-like）和虫洞（wormhole-like, WH-like）等多支重建解分支；Chaplygin 扇区自然产生有效暗能量（dark-energy）和外奇物质（exotic-matter）区域，可支持可穿越虫洞几何；多变（polytropic）扇区提供了恒星内部与致密天体的物理模型。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了统一协变框架，用于构造和解释广义相对论之外的致密天体、有效宇宙学扇区和规则核心强场几何；非线性扭转修正（nonlinear torsion corrections）在塑造解空间中起关键作用，解的分支可在 Coley–Landry 不变量分类框架（invariant classification framework）下组织。

Abstract: We investigate static, spherically symmetric (SS) spacetimes in covariant teleparallel $F(T)$ gravity sourced by nonlinear Chaplygin and polytropic fluids. Using the covariant coframe/spin-connection (CSC) formalism, we derive the corresponding field equations and conservation laws governing admissible matter distributions and nonlinear torsion sectors. A general reconstruction procedure is developed, allowing the systematic determination of teleparallel $F(T)$ models for arbitrary coframe ansätze and fluid equations of state. Focusing on power-law configurations, we obtain several classes of reconstructed solution branches, including constant-radius, compact-object-like, black-hole-like (BH-like), and wormhole-like (WH-like) branches. The Chaplygin sector naturally generates effective dark-energy and exotic-matter regimes capable of supporting traversable wormhole geometries, while the polytropic sector provides physically relevant models for stellar interiors and compact objects. We discuss the associated horizon and throat structures, torsion singularities, energy conditions, and stability properties of the reconstructed branches. The resulting geometries are organized within the Coley--Landry invariant classification framework, highlighting the role of nonlinear torsion corrections in shaping the solution space. Overall, this work provides a unified covariant framework for the construction and interpretation of compact objects, effective cosmological sectors, and regular-core strong-field geometries beyond General Relativity.

Result: 新增248个配置，其中197个为新模拟的偏心轨道；目录总数达到2129例。通过计算与理论无限分辨率外推之间的失配（mismatch）评估波形精度，并分析了并合时间、轨道数、最终质量、最终自旋、反冲速度以及引力辐射的峰值振幅、频率和光度的收敛性质。

Conclusion: 新版RIT目录大幅扩充了偏心双黑洞波形数据，并通过多分辨率收敛性研究建立了系统性的误差估计框架，为引力波天文学提供更完备且可靠的数值相对论波形模板。

Abstract: This fifth release of the RIT public catalog of numerical relativity binary black hole waveforms http://ccrg.rit.edu/~RITCatalog introduces an additional 248 configurations, prioritizing 197 newly simulated eccentric orbits. This update brings the catalog to a total of 2129 cases. All waveforms are corrected for center-of-mass drift and extrapolated to future null infinity. To rigorously estimate waveform errors, we conduct multiple-resolution convergence studies on 10 eccentric simulations (up to 33 orbits to merger) using three global resolutions increasing by factors of 1.2, plus a comprehensive six-resolution study for a single 18-orbit configuration. We evaluate waveform accuracy by computing mismatches against theoretical infinite-resolution extrapolations. Additionally, we analyze the convergence properties of key physical observables: merger times, number of orbits, final masses, final spins, recoil velocities, and the peak amplitude, frequency, and luminosity of the gravitational radiation.

*Nesibe Derin Sivrioglu,Robert R. Caldwell*

Main category: gr-qc

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过提出最终黑洞的最低准正则模（lowest quasinormal mode）标志着低频域的结束，建立了一个解析模型（analytic model），将总发射能量表达为质心系（center of mass frame）中黑洞速度的函数，模型不含任何自由参数。

Result: 模型预测总初始能量的13.8%以引力辐射形式发射，与数值相对论（numerical relativity）结果高度一致。该结果还可用于计算非线性贡献（nonlinear contribution）对引力记忆（memory）的影响，即引力波爆发通过后时空的持续畸变。

Conclusion: 该分析模型成功预测了等质量黑洞正面碰撞的引力辐射能量，无需自由参数即可与数值相对论相符。未来更高速的数值相对论模拟将进一步检验模型在相对论性速度（relativistic speeds）下的适用性，加深对这一极端碰撞过程的理解。

Abstract: What is the spectrum of gravitational radiation produced by the head-on collision of two equal-mass black holes? The emission is dominated by low frequency bremsstrahlung, producing a flat energy spectrum. But where does the spectrum turn over? We propose that the lowest quasinormal mode of the final black hole marks the end of the low-frequency domain. The result is an analytic model of the total emitted energy as a function of the black hole velocity in the center of mass frame. With no free parameters, the model predicts that 13.8% of the total initial energy is emitted in gravitational radiation, in good agreement with numerical relativity. This result also enables calculation of the nonlinear contribution to the memory, a persistent distortion of the spacetime after passage of the gravitational wave burst. Advances in numerical relativity simulations will enable tests of our model for increasingly relativistic speeds, providing insight into this extreme collision.

### [43] [Hawking Temperatures of Dynamical Black Holes from the RVB--Residue Method:Vaidya and Kinnersley Geometries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10220)
*Wen-Xiang Chen*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文发展了一种基于局部留数的RVB方法扩展，用于计算动态黑洞的霍金温度。该方法通过将近视界径向函数解析延拓到复平面，从逆视界函数在简单极点处的留数提取霍金温度，并成功应用于Vaidya黑洞和Kinnersley黑洞，证明了温度应理解为局部近视界量而非全局平衡温度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非稳态黑洞（non-stationary black holes）通常不存在全局类时Killing矢量（global timelike Killing vector），因此无法直接沿用稳态黑洞的霍金温度定义，需要发展一种局部、近视界（near-horizon）和准静态（quasi-stationary）的温度计算方法。

Method: 基于留数（residue）的RVB方法扩展：将近视界径向函数解析延拓（analytically continue）到复平面，在局部视界对应的简单极点（simple pole）处计算逆视界函数（inverse horizon function）的留数，从而提取局部霍金温度。

Result: 在Vaidya黑洞中，该方法复现了标准局部 trapping-horizon 温度 T=1/(8πM(v))；在任意加速的Kinnersley黑洞中，该方法得到了依赖于时空点的局部霍金温度，与广义 tortoise-coordinate 方法结果一致。

Conclusion: RVB-留数方法可以从稳态黑洞自然地推广到动态和非球对称黑洞，前提是温度被解释为局部近视界量（local near-horizon quantity）而非全局平衡温度（global equilibrium temperature）。

Abstract: This paper develops a local residue-based extension of the Robson--Villari--Biancalana method for calculating Hawking temperatures of dynamical black holes. Since non-stationary black holes generally do not admit a global timelike Killing vector, their temperature must be understood in a local, near-horizon, and quasi-stationary sense. By analytically continuing the near-horizon radial function into the complex plane, the Hawking temperature can be extracted from the residue of the inverse horizon function at the simple pole corresponding to the local horizon. This residue prescription is first applied to the Vaidya black hole, where it reproduces the standard local trapping-horizon temperature (T=1/(8πM(v))). The method is then extended to the arbitrarily accelerating Kinnersley black hole, whose horizon depends on time and angular coordinates. In this case, the RVB--residue method yields a point-dependent local Hawking temperature consistent with the generalized tortoise-coordinate approach. The results show that the RVB--residue method can be naturally generalized from stationary black holes to dynamical and non-spherical black holes, provided that the temperature is interpreted as a local near-horizon quantity rather than a global equilibrium temperature.

### [44] [Tuning A Rotating Black Hole Spectrum with Dark Matter Halo: Quasibound States, Scalar Cloud, Black Hole Bomb and Superradiant Scattering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10332)
*David Senjaya*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文研究了嵌入Dehnen暗物质晕中的旋转黑洞的谱动力学，揭示了准束缚态与超辐射散射如何共同刻画系统的物理响应，并表明Dehnen晕通过其内斜率参数γ直接调控了共振谱和能量提取通道。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在真实天体环境中，黑洞通常被暗物质晕（dark matter halo）包围，然而现有研究较少系统地考察暗物质晕的结构参数（如密度轮廓的内斜率）对旋转黑洞的准束缚态（quasibound state）和超辐射散射（superradiant scattering）的联合影响。

Method: 从精确的Schwarzschild–Dehnen解出发，利用Newman–Janis算法构造其旋转对应体，得到包含结构化晕影响的轴对称几何。采用解析渐近匹配方法（analytical asymptotic matching method）推导准束缚态频谱，并解析地获得超辐射放大因子表达式。

Result: 准束缚态频率的实部保持类氢结构，但通过有效质量标度ρ₀r₀³/(γ-3)被晕系统性移动；更致密、更延伸、更尖锐的晕增强结合能、降低不稳定性临界质量并抑制黑洞炸弹（black hole bomb）的生长速率。在散射端，相同的晕属性在增强结合效应的同时趋向于收窄超辐射窗口。

Conclusion: 准束缚态与超辐射散射是统一谱结构的互补表现，Dehnen晕作为环境调节器（environmental tuner）将其结构属性直接印刻在旋转黑洞的共振谱和能量提取通道上。

Abstract: We investigate the spectral dynamics of a rotating black hole embedded in a Dehnen $(1,4,γ)$ dark matter halo, where quasibound states and superradiant scattering jointly characterize the physical response of the system. Starting from an exact Schwarzschild--Dehnen solution, we construct its rotating counterpart via the Newman--Janis algorithm, yielding a consistent axisymmetric geometry that incorporates the influence of a structured halo. The Dehnen profile, through its inner slope parameter $γ$, introduces a controlled deformation of both the near-horizon and asymptotic regions of the spacetime. Using the analytical asymptotic matching method, we derive the quasibound-state spectrum and show that the real part of the frequency retains a hydrogen-like structure, but is systematically shifted by the halo through the effective mass scale $ρ_0 r_0^3/(γ-3)$. In particular, denser, more extended, and more cuspy halos enhance the binding energy, lower the critical mass required for the onset of instability, and typically suppress the growth rate of the black hole bomb. In the scattering sector, we obtain an analytic expression for the superradiant amplification factor and find that the same halo properties that strengthen binding effects also tend to narrow the superradiant window. These results demonstrate that quasibound states and superradiant scattering are complementary manifestations of a unified spectral structure, with the Dehnen halo acting as an environmental tuner that imprints its properties directly onto both the resonance spectrum and the energy-extraction channels of the rotating black hole.

### [47] [Hawking-Page phase transition for pure Lovelock black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10647)
*Nitesh K. Dubey,Sanved Kolekar*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了静态球对称反德西特（AdS）黑洞在纯Lovelock引力中的热力学性质，重点分析了特征温度（极小温度与Hawking-Page相变温度）之间的关系，以及Ruppeiner标量曲率在Hawking-Page相变处的普适性。研究表明，在Einstein引力中极小温度与Hawking-Page温度存在简单关系，而在高阶Lovelock理论中这一关系被维度与阶数依赖的因子修正；归一化Ruppeiner标量曲率在特定条件下呈现普适常数行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了深入理解反德西特（AdS）黑洞热力学中特征温度（极小温度与Hawking-Page相变温度）之间的内在联系，并探索Ruppeiner标量曲率在Hawking-Page相变处的普适性行为，从而揭示纯Lovelock引力下黑洞热力学的普适结构。

Method: 通过理论分析静态球对称AdS黑洞在纯Lovelock引力中的热力学性质，分别考察电磁中性情形与带电荷情形（巨正则系综）下的极小温度与Hawking-Page相变温度关系，并计算归一化Ruppeiner标量曲率在相变点的取值。

Result: 在Einstein引力中，中性AdS黑洞的极小温度与$d$维Hawking-Page温度相同；在高阶Lovelock理论中，关系被维度与阶数依赖的因子修正。带电荷情形下，Einstein引力中两温度相差简单维度依赖因子，而纯Lovelock理论中无普适关系。归一化Ruppeiner标量曲率在中性AdS黑洞中是仅依赖维度的普适常数；在Einstein理论下带电荷情形仍保持常数，但在一般Lovelock理论中依赖压力与静电势等热力学参数。

Conclusion: 纯Lovelock引力下AdS黑洞特征温度间的普适关系仅在Einstein极限下恢复，高阶曲率修正引入了额外的维度与阶数依赖。Ruppeiner标量曲率在Hawking-Page相变处的普适常数行为仅在Einstein引力和中性Lovelock黑洞中严格成立，在一般情形下表现为渐近普适性。

Abstract: We investigate the thermodynamic properties of static, spherically symmetric Anti-de Sitter (AdS) black holes, focusing on the interplay between characteristic temperatures, as well as on the universality of Ruppeiner scalar curvature at the Hawking-Page (HP) phase transition. In particular, we study the relation between the minimum temperature and the HP phase transition temperature for static, spherically symmetric AdS black holes in pure Lovelock gravity. For the electromagnetically neutral case in Einstein gravity, the minimum temperature in $(d+1)$ dimensions coincides with the HP transition temperature in $d$ dimensions, while in higher pure Lovelock theories this relation is modified by a dimension- and order-dependent factor, reducing to the Einstein result in appropriate limits. For charged AdS black holes, in the grand canonical ensemble, in general relativity, the two temperatures differ by a simple dimension-dependent factor, whereas no universal relation persists in higher curvature pure Lovelock theories. We further analyze the normalized Ruppeiner scalar curvature at the HP transition and show that it is a universal constant depending only on the spacetime dimension for electromagnetically neutral black holes in pure Lovelock theories. The normalized scalar curvature remains a constant, under appropriate conditions, even for the charged static spherically symmetric black holes in the grand canonical ensemble for the Einstein theory case, whereas in general pure Lovelock theories it depends on thermodynamic parameters such as pressure and electrostatic potential, asymptotically approaching a constant in the large-pressure or simultaneous large-potential and large-pressure limits.

### [48] [Gravitational superfluorescence from superradiant axion clouds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10776)

Method: 通过理论分析广义相对论中带标量场的刘维尔解（Liouville solution），研究其对称性、时间依赖性及在特定势能条件下的几何性质；并与施瓦西解（Schwarzschild solution）进行对比以提取质函数（mass function）。

Result: 该解在指数型无下界标量场势能条件下描述球对称黑洞形成：事件视界（event horizon）从有限时刻的无穷小半径出现并以光速膨胀。远处观测者可测量到类似单极子或时空球面位错的几何缺陷。质函数（mass function）与时间平方成正比。

Conclusion: 刘维尔解（Liouville solution）在给定条件下可描述黑洞形成，其事件视界（event horizon）的动态演化特征及可观测几何缺陷为相关研究提供了新的理论视角。

Abstract: The Liouville solution in General Relativity with a scalar field is discussed. This solution is invariant with respect to global Lorentz transformations, and dependence on time cannot be removed. If the scalar field potential is exponential and unbounded from below, the Liouville solution describes the formation of spherically symmetric black hole. The event horizon is a sphere, which appears with infinitesimal radius at a finite moment of time and afterwards expands with the velocity of light to infinity. A distant observer can measure the geometric defect at the point where the horizon appears. It is similar to the defect produced by the monopole or spherical dislocation of space-time. Comparison with the Schwarzschild solution yields the mass function which is proportional to the time squared.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 低维紧致 trapped 子流形（如 trapped loops）可以被视为黑洞的稳定信号（signature），拓展了传统 trapped surface 作为黑洞标志的概念。

Abstract: The conjecture that compact trapped submanifolds (CTMs) of any codimension greater than one cannot intersect the domain of outer communications of a black hole is tested in symmetrically collapsing spacetimes of $n+1$ dimensions, $n \geq 2$, and on the entire Kerr-Newman sub-extreme family. The results provide evidence to the idea that CTMs of lower dimension, such as trapped loops, should be ragarded as black hole signatures.

### [51] [A Friendly Phantom: Late-time AdS-to-dS transition and cosmological tensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11062)

Method: 引入一个具有“错误符号”动能项（即负动能，ghost kinetic term）的鬼标量场（phantom scalar），该场在一个有界双曲正切势（bounded hyperbolic-tangent potential）上演化，从而在晚期平滑诱导出从 AdS 负能量真空态到 dS 正能量真空态的跃迁。

Result: 该构造表明：鬼场的斥力行为可以在其能量密度仍为负值时出现；但整体总能量保持正定；晚期吸引子为 de Sitter 宇宙，不会演化为大撕裂奇点（Big Rip）；整个动力学在红外区是安全的。

Conclusion: Ph-Λ_sCDM 提供了一个具体的晚期动力学机制，具有缓解多种宇宙学张力的潜力。

Abstract: We present Ph-$Λ_{\rm s}$CDM, a phantom-scalar realization within General Relativity of the sign-switching cosmological-constant idea, $Λ_{\rm s}$CDM, in which a phantom scalar evolving on a bounded hyperbolic-tangent potential induces a smooth mirror AdS-to-dS transition in the late-time dark-energy density. The wrong-sign kinetic term, usually viewed as pathological, becomes the mechanism lifting the field from a negative- to a positive-energy vacuum-like regime. The construction also shows that the field can become repulsive while its energy density is still negative. The cosmology nevertheless remains controlled: total energy stays positive, the late-time attractor is de Sitter rather than a Big Rip, and the dynamics remain safely infrared. Ph-$Λ_{\rm s}$CDM thus offers a concrete late-time mechanism with the potential to address multiple cosmological tensions.

### [52] [Jittery Quantum Boomerang Effect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10067)
*Pedro Dornelas,Gerson J. Ferreira*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文研究无序Rashba二维电子气中自旋极化波包的动力学，发现一种“抖动量子回旋镖效应”（jittery quantum boomerang effect）：纵向与横向运动通过根本不同的机制返回原点。在弱散射区域，杂质散射充当黏性阻尼抑制瞬态Zitterbewegung并驱动横向位移归零，而纵向位移呈Drude类饱和。随无序增强，纵向运动出现部分回返，标志着从弱反局域化到二维安德森局域化的转变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究无序Rashba二维电子气中自旋极化波包的动力学行为，特别是纵向与横向运动是否以及如何返回原点，并揭示无序对自旋霍尔效应（spin Hall effect）和局域化（localization）的影响。

Method: 采用Chebyshev展开（Chebyshev expansion）计算时间演化算符，结合无序系综平均，对初始沿x方向具有有限动量、沿z方向自旋极化的态进行时间演化。在弱散射区域，利用量子动力学方程（quantum kinetic equation）推导运动方程并与数值结果对比。

Result: 发现了抖动量子回旋镖效应：纵向与横向运动通过不同机制返回原点。杂质散射作为黏性阻尼，抑制瞬态Zitterbewegung并驱动横向位移在长时间下回归y=0；纵向位移在弱无序下呈Drude类饱和。随无序增强，纵向运动出现部分回返。

Conclusion: 结果与无序Rashba模型中固有自旋霍尔电导（intrinsic spin Hall conductivity）消失的结论一致，也与瞬态固有自旋霍尔效应的时域实验观测相符。纵向动力学的部分回返信号了从弱反局域化（weak antilocalization）到二维安德森局域化（Anderson localization）的转变。

Abstract: We study the dynamics of a spin-polarized wave packet in a disordered Rashba two-dimensional electron gas and identify a jittery quantum boomerang effect in which longitudinal and transverse motion return to the origin through fundamentally distinct mechanisms. Starting from an initial state with finite momentum along $x$ and spin polarized along $z$, we calculate the time evolution by combining a Chebyshev expansion of the time-evolution operator with a disorder ensemble average. In the weak-scattering regime, equations of motion derived from the quantum kinetic equation reproduce the numerical trends and show that impurity scattering acts as a viscous damping mechanism that suppresses the transient Zitterbewegung and drives the transverse displacement back to $y=0$ at long times. In contrast, the longitudinal dynamics show a Drude-like saturation at weak disorder. These results are consistent with the vanishing intrinsic spin Hall conductivity in the disordered Rashba model and with experimental observations of a transient intrinsic spin Hall effect in the time-domain. As disorder increases, the longitudinal dynamics evolve to a partial return toward the origin, which signals a transition from weak antilocalization to Anderson localization in 2D.

### [53] [Magnetic HIP-NN for spin dynamics in disordered itinerant magnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10349)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在层级相互作用粒子神经网络（HIP-NN）的基础上引入磁性扩展，将旋转不变的自旋关联直接集成到层级消息传递层中，使得网络能够在保持自旋旋转对称性的同时，从耦合的几何-自旋环境中学习涌现的磁能量景观和有效局域场。

Result: mHIP-NN准确再现了控制Landau-Lifshitz-Gilbert动力学的局域力矩，并忠实捕捉了热淬火后空间自旋关联的非平衡演化。

Abstract: We present a magnetic extension of the Hierarchically Interacting Particle Neural Network (HIP-NN) that enables large-scale simulations of electron-mediated spin dynamics in disordered itinerant magnets. The resulting magnetic HIP-NN (mHIP-NN) incorporates rotationally invariant spin correlations directly into hierarchical message-passing layers, enabling the network to learn emergent magnetic energy landscapes and effective local fields from coupled geometric-spin environments while preserving spin-rotation symmetry. As a benchmark application, we consider structurally disordered itinerant $s$-$d$ exchange models in which the effective magnetic forces arise dynamically from the instantaneous electronic structure and are computationally prohibitive to evaluate using conventional exact-diagonalization-based approaches. We show that mHIP-NN accurately reproduces the local torques governing Landau-Lifshitz-Gilbert dynamics and faithfully captures the nonequilibrium evolution of spatial spin correlations following thermal quenches. Our results establish symmetry-aware hierarchical message-passing networks as an efficient and scalable framework for large-scale simulations of frustrated itinerant spin systems and nonequilibrium magnetic dynamics. More broadly, because the learned energy functional remains fully differentiable with respect to both atomic coordinates and spin variables, the framework also provides a natural foundation for spin-dependent interatomic potentials and coupled atom-spin dynamics.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用空穴法（cavity method）近似计算完整的LDoS分布，并结合非线性西格玛模型（non-linear sigma model）的对称性进行验证。

Result: 扩展相中LDoS分布的幂律尾（power-law tail）标度指数为3；连续谱本征向量为扩展但弱多重分形（weakly multifractal），其逆参与率（inverse participation ratio, IPR）呈现对数随系统尺寸标度，而非传统定义下的完全扩展或局域化行为。

Abstract: We study the local density of states (LDoS) distribution of a general class of weighted Erdős-Rényi graphs. Using the cavity method, we obtain a good approximation to the full LDoS distribution and compact expressions for its power-law tails, which we show to have exponent $3$ in the extended phase. We deduce that the eigenvectors in the continuous part of the spectrum are extended but (weakly) multifractal, and we extract expressions for the associated fractal dimensions and the singularity spectrum. We also demonstrate that the inverse participation ratio in this multifractal phase exhibits an unusual logarithmic scaling with system size, which is neither fully-extended nor localised by the usual definitions. Finally, we verify that some symmetry properties (derived from the non-linear sigma model), which have been shown to hold for many systems exhibiting multifractality, also hold in our case, both for the LDoS distribution and the singularity spectrum.

### [55] [Beyond the Markovian limit: Exact solutions for active motion in a power-law viscoelastic bath](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10145)
*Mintu Karmakar,Jure Dobnikar,Ignacio Pagonabarraga*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过求解平动和转动自由度耦合的非马尔可夫广义朗之万方程（generalized Langevin equations），为幂律黏弹性介质中的活性粒子发展了一套解析理论。

Result: 黏弹性记忆导致分数阶短时输运（fractional short-time transport）、增强的长时持久性（enhanced long-time persistence），以及瞬时力与游泳体取向（swimmer orientation）的去关联。记忆核（memory kernel）控制反常标度指数（anomalous scaling exponents），而活性决定亚扩散（sub-diffusive）、弹道（ballistic）与扩散（diffusive）等不同输运区间之间的交叉行为。

Conclusion: 该工作为描述复杂生物环境和高分子环境中的生物及合成微游泳体提供了理论框架。

Abstract: Active particles from bacteria to synthetic microswimmers often navigate viscoelastic media with complex relaxation dynamics. The classical active Brownian model that assumes instantaneous friction is clearly not applicable to describe such motility, while the non-Markovian processes combined with viscoelasticity are relatively unexplored. Here, we develop an analytical theory for an active particle in a power-law viscoelastic medium by solving coupled non-Markovian generalized Langevin equations for translational and rotational degrees of freedom. The viscoelastic memory results in novel phenomena such as fractional short-time transport, enhanced long-time persistence, and de-correlation of the instantaneous force and the swimmer orientation. We demonstrate that the memory kernel controls the anomalous scaling exponents, while the activity determines the crossover between sub-diffusive, ballistic and diffusive regimes. Our work provides a framework for theoretical description of biological and synthetic micro swimmers in complex biological and polymeric environments.

### [56] [Edge slip stabilizes confined active vortices by suppressing localized instabilities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10424)
*Zhihan Ye,Tianyu Ren,Hao Luo,Yanan Liu,Guangyin Jing*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过连续介质模型和线性稳定性分析，研究了滑移边界条件（slip boundary condition）如何调控圆形受限主动向列系统（active nematic system）中稳态涡旋（steady vortex state）的动力学稳定性，发现增大滑移速度可以抑制局域不稳定性，从而稳定宏观相干结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受限主动系统能够维持持久的涡旋流（vortical flows），其稳定性受边界条件的强烈影响，但边界滑移（boundary slip）如何定量决定动力学稳定性尚缺乏理解。

Method: 采用流主导（flow-dominated）区域的连续介质模型（continuum model），对圆形受限主动向列系统中的稳态涡旋态进行线性稳定性分析（linear stability analysis），推导出包含滑移速度（slip velocity）与流动-取向耦合（flow-alignment coupling）的显式稳定性判据。

Result: 增大滑移速度会抑制局域线性不稳定性（localized linear instabilities），从而促进稳态涡旋态的持续存在；换言之，放松边界摩擦（boundary friction）通过抑制通常破坏单涡旋态的流动诱导重新取向（flow induced reorientation），进而稳定了宏观相干结构。

Conclusion: 边界滑移可作为一种非平庸的流体动力学控制参数（hydrodynamic control parameter），用于工程化设计稳定的主动流（active flows）。

Abstract: Confined active systems can sustain persistent vortical flows whose stability is strongly influenced by boundary conditions. At the individual level, active units generate internal stresses that drive spontaneous flows, which in turn advect and reorient the particles. This nonlinear coupling between active flow and orientational order is significantly mediated by the system's boundaries, where the specific slip condition governs how these internal stresses generate active flow then rearrange the local orientations. However, a quantitative understanding of how boundary slip dictates their dynamical stability remains lacking. Here, we study how the slip boundary condition controls the stability of a steady vortex state in a circularly confined active nematic system. Using a continuum model in a flow-dominated regime, we perform a linear stability analysis and derive an explicit criterion incorporating the slip velocity and flow-alignment coupling. We find that increasing slip velocity suppresses localized linear instabilities, thereby promoting the persistence of the steady vortex state. This reveals a relaxing the boundary friction actually stabilizes the macroscopic coherent structure by depressing flow induced reorientation that typically destroys single-vortex states. Our findings establish boundary slip as a nontrivial hydrodynamic control parameter for engineering stable active flows.

### [57] [Energetics of Nucleation in Finitely Deformed, Phase-Transforming Soft Solids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10427)
*Mrityunjay Kothari*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文推导了超弹性体在有限变形下小转变区域的平衡弹性势能变化渐近展开式，将弹性贡献纳入经典成核理论，得到应力作用下的转变温度、临界半径和成核势垒，并通过可压缩neo-Hookean固体的算例展示了有限变形效应与线性弹性结果的显著差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典成核理论（classical nucleation theory）中，预存应力通过体驱动力中的弹性贡献改变成核势垒。该贡献在线弹性材料中已有充分表征，但在软固体有限变形下的结果尚不完善；在模拟中直接评估每个候选核的弹性自由能变化需求解非线性弹性边值问题，计算代价极高。

Method: 推导超弹性体在形成小转变区域前后平衡弹性势能变化的渐近展开式，展开参数为各向同性转变应变（transformation strain）的幅值，预存变形和应力可为有限大。利用该展开式将弹性贡献纳入经典成核理论，获得应力修正的转变温度、临界半径和成核势垒。

Result: 在可压缩neo-Hookean固体（compressible neo-Hookean solid）的静水压、单轴和等双轴加载条件下，拉伸应力促进成核，压缩应力抑制成核（当转变应变为膨胀性时）。与线性弹性结果对比表明，有限变形效应在中等拉伸下可显著改变预测的能垒。

Conclusion: 所提出的渐近展开方法避免了为每个候选核求解非线性弹性边值问题的计算负担，同时保留了有限变形下成核弹性贡献的关键特征，为软材料中的应力诱导成核分析提供了有效工具。

Abstract: Classical nucleation theory describes the rate at which stable nuclei form within a metastable parent phase by crossing a free-energy barrier set by competing bulk and interfacial energies. In an elastic material, a pre-existing stress state modifies this barrier through an elastic contribution to the bulk driving force. This contribution is well characterized for linear elastic materials, but the corresponding finite-deformation result for soft solids remains less developed. The gap is computationally significant: in simulations that sample candidate nuclei throughout a stressed body, direct evaluation of the elastic contribution to free-energy change would require solving a new nonlinear elasticity boundary-value problem for each possible nucleus. Here, we derive an asymptotic expansion of the equilibrium elastic potential energy change for a hyperelastic body before and after formation of a small transformed region. The expansion is with respect to the amplitude of an isotropic transformation strain, while the pre-existing deformation and stress may be finite. At leading order, the elastic contribution to the formation energy is determined entirely by the known untransformed equilibrium fields, with additional terms accounting for stiffness contrast between the parent and transformed phases. Incorporating this into classical nucleation theory yields the stress-shifted transformation temperature, critical radius, and nucleation barrier. Representative results are shown for a compressible neo-Hookean solid under hydrostatic, uniaxial, and equibiaxial loading; tensile stresses promote nucleation and compressive stresses suppress it when transformation strain is expansive. Comparison with the corresponding linear-elastic result shows that finite-deformation effects can substantially change the predicted energy barrier at moderate stretches.

</details>


### [58] [One-Step Self-Organized Multifunctional Micromotors via Evaporative Liquid-Liquid Phase Separation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10444)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多功能活性微载体（active microcarriers）在生物医学应用中需求迫切，但其传统制备工艺通常涉及复杂的多步流程，限制了可及性与实用性。因此，亟需一种简单、高效且生物相容性好的单步构建方法。

Method: 利用蒸发诱导的全水相液-液相分离现象，在聚合物与蛋白质混合液滴蒸发过程中，自发形成微米级凝聚体，同时封装功能组分（酶、纳米颗粒、药物）。借助蒸发引发的马兰戈尼流（Marangoni flow）与界面吸附作用，实现纳米颗粒的不对称内部自组织，从而产生Janus状结构与自发形状各向异性。

Result: 成功制备出具有内部磁各向异性的双功能微马达，其同时具备催化推进与磁矩转向能力，即使在均匀环境中也能实现定向运动。该方法一步实现了多功能、生物相容性微马达的构建。

Conclusion: 该工作提供了一种通用的单步平台技术，用于构建具有内禀不对称结构的生物相容性多功能微马达，有望简化微载体制备流程并拓展其在复杂生物环境中的应用。

Abstract: Active microcarriers capable of transporting multiple functional components and navigating complex environments are highly desirable for biomedical applications, yet their fabrication typically requires complex multistep processes. Here we show that evaporation-induced liquid-liquid phase separation in all aqueous polymer and protein mixtures provides a simple one-step route to multifunctional micromotors. During droplet evaporation, micron-sized condensates spontaneously form and encapsulate enzymes, nanoparticles, and drugs. Evaporation-induced Marangoni flows and interfacial adsorption generate asymmetric internal self-organization of nanoparticles, producing Janus-like architectures and spontaneously emergent shape anisotropy without the need for patterned fabrication. Dual functionality with internal magnetic anisotropy allowed catalytic propulsion steered by magnetic torque, enabling directional motion even in homogeneous environments. Thus, we present a versatile platform for the one-step construction of biocompatible, multifunctional micromotors with internally asymmetric architectures.

### [59] [Finite-Time Orientational Relaxation Restructures Collective Motion in Polar Active Matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10474)
*Rajneesh Kumar,Subhransu Sekhar Mishra,Debasish Chaudhuri*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该论文通过引入有限弛豫速率的朗之万（Langevin）公式化描述Vicsek类活性粒子，结合Vicsek局部共识与XY模型取向动力学，数值模拟揭示了随对齐速率增加而出现的丰富非平衡相图，包括各向同性态、极性带、交叉海相、均匀极性和微团簇态等，并发现各向同性-极性转变为强一级相变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将Vicsek模型中的瞬时排序机制推广为有限速率取向弛豫（finite-rate orientational relaxation），以更真实地描述活性物质（active matter）中粒子取向的动力学演化，并系统探讨对齐速率如何调控集体行为。

Method: 采用朗之万公式描述Vicsek类活性粒子，取向通过有限速率弛豫向局部平均方向演化，受对齐强度$J$和旋转扩散系数$D_r$控制，并利用大规模数值模拟确定非平衡相图。

Result: 增大对齐速率驱动系统依次经历各向同性态、极性带、交叉海相、均匀极性态和微团簇态；各向同性-极性转变为强一级相变，表现为Binder累积量和局部极化/密度分布的双峰特征；极性带尺寸随活性增加而增大，但对对齐速率的依赖呈非单调关系。

Conclusion: 有限时间取向弛豫作为控制参数（control parameter）能够定性重构极性活性物质的集体行为，揭示了比标准Vicsek模型更为丰富的非平衡相结构。

Abstract: We introduce a Langevin formulation of Vicsek-like active particles in which orientations evolve through finite-rate relaxation toward the local mean direction, with alignment strength $J$ and rotational diffusivity $D_r$, thereby combining Vicsek-type local consensus with XY-like orientational dynamics. Using large-scale numerical simulations, we determine the nonequilibrium phase diagram as a function of activity and alignment rate. Increasing the alignment rate drives a sequence of transitions from a homogeneous isotropic state to polar bands, a cross-sea phase of intersecting bands, a homogeneous polar state, and ultimately a micro-clustered regime. The isotropic-to-polar transition is strongly first order, as evidenced by Binder cumulants and bimodal distributions of local polarization and density, indicating coexistence of gas-like and liquid-like regions. Near the onset of collective motion, band size increases with activity but depends non-monotonically on alignment rate. Further increasing the alignment rate drives the system through the cross-sea and homogeneous polar phases before enhanced density fluctuations lead to micro-clustering. Our results demonstrate that finite-time orientational relaxation acts as a control parameter that qualitatively restructures collective behavior in polar active matter.

### [60] [Virial stress in systems of active Brownian particles in the presence of translational and rotational inertia](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10486)
*Chandranshu Tiwari,Sunil P. Singh,Roland G. Winkler*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该论文推导了具有平动和转动惯性的活性布朗粒子（ABP+TRI）系统的应力张量，研究了周期系统和受限系统的应力性质，发现泳动应力（swim stress）并不包含在局部应力张量中，因此不能代表ABP+TRI系统的实际应力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解活性物质（active matter）中惯性和边界条件对应力张量的影响，尤其是转动惯性（rotational inertia）如何改变近壁区域的极化行为和密度分布，以及状态方程（equation of state）的有效性。

Method: 采用第一类拉格朗日运动方程（Lagrange's equations of motion of the first kind）推导转动运动的应力张量；利用二维理想活性气体的朗之万模拟（Langevin simulations）验证周期系统状态方程，并分析受限系统的局部应力。

Result: 周期系统中存在依赖于平动和转动惯性的状态方程；受限系统在壁附近出现推进方向（propulsion direction）的强极化和密度增强，且随转动惯性增大而加剧；受限系统体相（bulk）的局部应力与周期系统相同；泳动应力（swim stress）不包含在局部应力张量中。

Conclusion: 转动惯性会破坏受限系统的状态方程，但体相局部应力与周期系统一致；泳动应力并非ABP+TRI系统应力的代表性量。

Abstract: We elucidate the stress in a system of active Brownian particles augmented with translational and rotational inertia (ABP+TRI). Stress tensors are derived for periodic systems as well as systems confined between walls by employing Lagrange's equations of motion of the first kind for the rotational motion. Using Langevin simulations of an ideal active gas in two dimensions, we confirm the existence of an equation of state for periodic systems that depends on translational and rotational inertia in general. Confinement implies a strong polarization of the propulsion direction near a wall and an enhanced density, both of which increase with increasing rotational inertia. This affects the local stress tensor normal to the confining walls, leading to a breakdown of the equation of state. Yet the local stress in the bulk part of the confined systems is identical with that of the periodic system. Importantly, for both kinds of boundary conditions, the so-called swim stress is not included in the local stress tensor; thus, in general, the swim stress is not representative of the stress in systems of ABP+TRIs.

### [61] [Moving backward to go faster: Diatom-inspired sliding reveals efficient modes of locomotion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10513)
*Julien le Dreff,Blaise Delmotte*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文基于硅藻群体启发，发现一种不同于经典波状摆动（undulatory swimming）的滑动推进（sliding-based propulsion）机制：链状多细胞结构通过相邻细胞间的相对滑动产生内部剪切力，从而驱动向前运动。该机制在速度与能量效率上均优于传统波动推进，且最优性能对应远大于链长的波长和与现实硅藻群体一致的细胞长宽比，提示流体动力学效率可能是硅藻链的演化选择压力之一。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典理论认为微生物在黏性环境中的运动主要依赖细长鞭毛（flagella）的波状弯曲，最优化推进要求形变波长接近身体长度。然而，自然界中存在如硅藻群体（diatom colonies）这样的链状多细胞结构，其运动机制尚不清楚。本文旨在探索滑动作为一种全新的运动模式是否能在多细胞链中驱动高效推进。

Method: 研究者受硅藻群体启发，提出一种基于相邻链状元素之间相对滑动（sliding）的推进模型，通过理论分析比较滑动推进与经典波状推进（undulatory swimming）的动力学特性，包括推进速度、能量效率以及最优波长和细胞长宽比（aspect ratio）的标度关系。

Result: 滑动推进产生的推力方向与经典波动推进相反，但能实现更高的运动速度和更大的能量效率。最优推进发生在波长远大于链长（wavelengths much larger than the chain length）的条件下，且最优细胞长宽比与自然界中硅藻群体的实际观测值一致。

Conclusion: 滑动机制是多细胞集合中一种此前被忽视的运动模式，该发现为流体动力学效率作为硅藻链演化选择压力（evolutionary selective pressure）提供了证据，并为高效仿生微型游泳器（bio-inspired microswimmers）和群体机器人系统（swarm robotic systems）的设计提供了新原理。

Abstract: Across biological scales, from sperm cells to whales, locomotion commonly relies on undulatory gaits, in which traveling deformation waves interact with the surrounding fluid to generate thrust opposite to the direction of wave propagation. In viscous environments, microorganism locomotion is classically understood in terms of undulatory bending of slender filaments such as flagella, with optimal propulsion achieved when the deformation wavelength is comparable to the swimmer length. Inspired by diatom colonies, we identify a fundamentally different swimming mechanism based on sliding between neighboring elements within a chain. We show that sliding between stacked elongated cells generates internal shear that drives propulsion opposite to classical undulatory swimming, while achieving higher speeds and greater energetic efficiency. Remarkably, optimal performance occurs at wavelengths much larger than the chain length and at cell aspect ratios consistent with those observed in natural diatom colonies, suggesting that hydrodynamic efficiency may constitute an evolutionary selective pressure in diatom chains. Together, these results identify sliding as a previously overlooked mode of locomotion in multicellular assemblies and suggest new design principles for efficient bio-inspired microswimmers and swarm robotic systems.

### [62] [Spontaneous translation of charged droplets during evaporation on dry surfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10755)
*Riming Xu,Yanbo Li,Jiawen Zhang,Jin Wang,Yikai Li*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本研究通过法拉第杯电荷测量与光学成像相结合的方法，揭示了在干燥聚合物基底上蒸发的水滴所携带的电荷演化行为：电荷在蒸发早期保持恒定，当液滴进入小体积状态后发生突然崩坍，伴随自发横向平移，而非射流或破碎。研究确认了一种干燥基底上的蒸发驱动静电弛豫模式，与润滑表面上的库仑裂变不同。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 蒸发中的 sessile droplets 通常被视为毛细物体（capillary objects），但日常操作产生的液滴可携带数十至数百皮库仑（picocoulombs）的电荷，其演化行为尚不明确。本文旨在探究这类电荷在干燥聚合物基底上随蒸发如何变化。

Method: 采用法拉第杯（Faraday cup）电荷测量与光学成像（optical imaging）相结合的方法；引入零时间协议（zero-time protocol）测定初始电荷；基于集成分辨测量（ensemble-resolved measurements）分析电荷演化；结合瑞利归一化分析（Rayleigh-normalized analysis）、球冠应力修正（spherical-cap stress correction）及接触角保持标度（contact-angle retention scale）进行力学解释；使用高速成像（high-speed imaging）与运动学分析（kinematic analysis）表征液滴运动。

Result: 在聚甲基戊烯（PMP）基底上，初始电荷可被保留；在PDMS、SOCAL涂层表面及聚苯乙烯上，电荷会发生交换、耗散或注入。在PMP上，电荷在蒸发早期几乎恒定，液滴达到小体积状态后突然减少。电荷崩坍伴随自发横向平移，而非射流或破碎。后续运动由接触线反复脱钉与再钉扎（contact-line depinning and re-pinning）控制；总移动距离受干燥表面钉扎影响显著，而峰值平移速度（peak translational velocity）是放电强度的更稳健指标。

Conclusion: 本研究识别出一种干燥基底上的蒸发驱动静电弛豫（evaporation-driven electrostatic relaxation）模式，区别于润滑表面上的库仑裂变（Coulomb fission）。该模式中，基底的静电被动性（electrostatic passivity）使电荷得以保留，液滴几何形状决定了不稳定性起始条件，而整体液滴平移提供了电荷释放路径。

Abstract: Evaporating sessile droplets are usually treated as capillary objects, but droplets generated by routine handling can carry tens to hundreds of picocoulombs of electric charge. Here we combine Faraday-cup charge measurements with optical imaging to determine how such charge evolves as water droplets evaporate on dry polymer substrates. A zero-time protocol shows that a reproducible initial charge is preserved on poly(methylpentene) (PMP), whereas PDMS, SOCAL-coated surfaces, and polystyrene either exchange, dissipate, or inject charge on contact. On PMP, ensemble-resolved measurements reveal two regimes: the charge remains nearly constant during early evaporation and then decreases abruptly once the droplet reaches a small-volume state. This charge collapse coincides with spontaneous lateral translation rather than jetting or breakup. A Rayleigh-normalized analysis, including a spherical-cap stress correction and measured contact-angle retention scale, shows that motion occurs only after evaporation drives the droplet into a high electro-pinning state. High-speed imaging and kinematic analysis support a picture in which the subsequent motion is governed by repeated contact-line depinning and re-pinning: the total distance traveled is strongly affected by dry-surface pinning, whereas the peak translational velocity serves as a more robust indicator of the discharge strength. These results identify a dry-substrate mode of evaporation-driven electrostatic relaxation, distinct from Coulomb fission on lubricated surfaces, in which substrate electrostatic passivity enables charge retention, droplet geometry selects the instability onset, and whole-droplet translation provides the charge-release pathway.

### [63] [NANOG assembles into self-limiting aging micelles that drive a sol-gel transition and modulate DNA dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10779)
*Amandine Hong-Minh,Yair Augusto Gutierrez Fosado,Abbie Guild,Nicholas Mullin,Laura Spagnolo,Ian Chambers,Davide Michieletto*

TL;DR: 该研究发现转录因子NANOG在高浓度下形成依赖于其内在无序结构域的宏观老化凝胶（aging gels），并通过分子动力学模拟、质量光度法和冷冻电镜观察到NANOG形成具有暴露DNA结合域的自限制胶束（self-limiting micelles），这些胶束能稳定DNA缠结并调控DNA动力学，暗示NANOG可能通过创建局部凝胶环境调节基因表达并赋予基因调控网络机械记忆。

Method: 首先通过实验观察NANOG在高浓度下的凝胶化行为；然后结合分子动力学模拟（molecular dynamics simulations）、质量光度法（mass photometry）和冷冻电镜（Cryo-EM）分析其结构组装形式；最后研究这些组装体对DNA动力学的影响。

Abstract: Proteins and nucleic acids form non-Newtonian liquids with complex rheological properties that contribute to their function in vivo. Here we investigate the rheology of the transcription factor NANOG, a key protein to maintain embryonic stem cell pluripotency. We find that at high concentrations, NANOG forms macroscopic aging gels that are dependent on its intrinsically disordered domain. By combining molecular dynamics simulations, mass photometry and Cryo-EM, we also discover that -- in contrast with unbounded condensates formed by other intrinsically disordered proteins -- NANOG forms self-limiting micelles with exposed DNA-binding domains. We show that these micelles can stabilize DNA entanglements and in turn modulate DNA dynamics. Based on our findings, we conjecture that NANOG may contribute to regulate gene expression by creating local gel-like environments that restrict genome dynamics and that its aging may ingrain mechanical memory in gene regulatory networks.

### [64] [How to grow a straight filament](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11080)
*Ludwig A. Hoffmann,L. Mahadevan*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过建立噪声驱动下弹性丝状物（elastic filament）的生长模型，研究局部与非局部反馈（local/nonlocal feedback）如何维持直向生长的稳定性。结果表明：局部反馈需依赖方向感知（orientation sensing）抑制长波不稳定性，而非局部反馈仅凭本体感知（proprioceptive sensing）即可实现稳定；弹性基底（elastic substrate）进一步抑制大尺度涨落。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生物体中丝状结构（filamentary structures）能在随机涨落（stochastic fluctuations）环境下可重复地保持直向生长，其背后的控制机制尚不明确。本文旨在揭示何种反馈策略能保障丝状物在噪声中维持直线形态。

Method: 构建一个受噪声驱动的生长弹性丝状物的最小模型（minimal model），其中生长响应依赖于应变（strain）、曲率（curvature）和方向（orientation），通过局部或非局部时空反馈律（spatiotemporal feedback laws）进行调控。采用线性稳定性分析（linear stability analysis）研究反馈机制稳定直构型的条件。

Result: 纯粹局部反馈需要方向感知来抑制长波不稳定性（long-wavelength instabilities），而非局部反馈仅凭曲率（本体）感知即可实现稳定。弹性基底的存在进一步抑制大尺度波动。

Conclusion: 本研究确立了保障丝状物稳健直向生长的最小控制策略（minimal control strategies），并为通过实验识别形态发生（morphogenesis）背后的反馈机制提供了可检验的特征信号。

Abstract: How can a growing biological filament remain straight despite stochastic fluctuations in growth? Motivated by filamentary structures that develop reproducibly across biological systems, we study the stability of a noisy, growing elastic filament regulated by feedback. We formulate a minimal model in which growth responds to the filament's strain, curvature, and orientation through local or nonlocal spatiotemporal feedback laws. Linear stability analysis identifies the conditions under which these feedback mechanisms stabilize a straight configuration. In the presence of noise, we show that purely local feedback requires orientation sensing to suppress long-wavelength instabilities, whereas nonlocal feedback allows stabilization through proprioceptive (curvature) sensing alone. Coupling to an elastic substrate further suppresses large-scale fluctuations. Our results establish minimal control strategies that ensure robust straight growth and suggest experimental signatures for identifying the feedback mechanisms underlying morphogenesis.

</details>

### [65] [Ternary public-key cryptosystem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07832)
*Steven Duplij,Qiang Guo,Na Fu*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 本文将公钥密码体制推广到三元代数结构，以ElGamal为代表家族，构建了三元ElGamal协议（密钥生成、临时加密、利用拟元解密），并通过数值实例验证了其可行性。三元框架提供了更丰富的代数结构（拟元替代二进制逆元）和更高的信息密度（矩阵三元化传递配对/明文向量），增强了攻击者的代数复杂度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统公钥密码体制基于二元代数结构。本文将公钥密码体制（public-key cryptosystems）推广到三元代数结构（ternary algebraic structures），以ElGamal为代表家族，探索更高维度的代数基础是否能为加密提供更丰富的代数结构和更高的信息密度。

Method: 首先引入非派生三元结构（nonderived ternary structures）的代数背景，包括特殊元素、三元群环（ternary group rings）以及矩阵三元化程序（matrix ternarization procedure），该程序将二元环和群环映射到在三元乘法下封闭的反对角线符号矩阵。在此基础上，构建三元ElGamal三步骤协议（密钥生成、临时加密、利用拟元解密），并推导显式的三元幂和拟元（querelement）公式以确保正确解密。

Result: 通过在三个具体代数结构上的数值实例验证了三元ElGamal构造的可行性：三元分式域、矩阵三元化有限群环、有限(6,3)-环（域）。实例验证了可接受的字长量化（word-length quantization）以及三元幂的循环行为（cycle behaviour）。

Conclusion: 三元框架突显了两个实用优势：更丰富的代数结构（拟元替代二元逆元）增加了攻击者的代数复杂度；更高的信息密度（矩阵三元化传递配对/明文向量）。正式的安全性假设、优化参数选择以及全面的安全性和性能分析仍需作为未来工作。

Abstract: Public-key cryptosystems eliminate the requirement for pre-shared secret keys by enabling encryption with a publicly disclosed key and decryption with a corresponding private key. In this article we generalize the public-key cryptosystems to ternary algebraic structures, with particular attention to ElGamal as a representative family. We introduce the necessary algebraic background for nonderived ternary structures, including special elements, ternary group rings, and a matrix ternarization procedure that maps binary rings and group rings to antidiagonal symbolic matrices closed under ternary multiplication. Building on these foundations, we formulate a ternary analogue of the ElGamal three-step protocol (key generation, ephemeral encryption, and decryption via querelements) and derive explicit ternary power and querelement formulas that enable correct decryption. Concrete instantiations and numerical examples over a ternary fraction field, a matrix-ternarized finite group ring, and a finite \((6,3)\)-ring (field) validate the construction and illustrate admissible word-length quantization and cycle behaviour of ternary powers. The ternary framework highlights two practical advantages: richer algebraic structure (querelements replace binary inverses) that increases algebraic complexity for attackers, and higher information density (matrix ternarization transfers paired/plaintext vectors). Formal hardness assumptions, optimized parameter choices, and comprehensive security and performance analyses remain necessary future work.

### [66] [A kinetic model of shear-induced rupture of short dsDNA](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10955)
*Ayman Hussein,Ralf Bundschuh*

Main category: q-bio.BM

TL;DR: 本文建立了基于力依赖成核-拉链路径的主方程框架，用于计算有限长度双链DNA在剪切力作用下的解离速率和过渡态距离，并通过实验数据验证了该框架的有效性，指出了双链DNA的三维螺旋几何结构在定义剪切下末端距中的关键作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 力诱导的短双链DNA（double-stranded DNA, dsDNA）解离是单分子生物物理学和DNA纳米技术的核心问题，但现有理论缺乏对有限长度DNA在剪切力作用下断裂的物理动力学描述。

Method: 构建了基于力依赖的成核-拉链路径的主方程框架，包含单碱基过渡，可直接计算宽力范围内的解离速率和过渡态距离。采用DNA-金纳米颗粒-DNA构型在恒定剪切力下进行实验验证。

Result: 模型准确复现了室温实验数据，统一解释了此前所有力区间内类似剪切双链体的测量结果。发现dsDNA的三维螺旋几何结构对于在短dsDNA的棒状聚合物模型中正确定义剪切下的末端距至关重要。提取的过渡态距离在实验相关参数范围内对单链DNA聚合物参数变化具有稳健性。

Conclusion: 该框架为解释力致断裂实验以及设计力与温度驱动的DNA纳米结构提供了预测性的动力学基础。

Abstract: Force-induced dissociation of short double-stranded DNA (dsDNA) is central to single-molecule biophysics and DNA nanotechnology, yet a physically grounded kinetic description of shear-induced rupture for finite-length constructs remains lacking. Here we develop a master equation framework built on a force-dependent nucleation-zipper pathway with single-base transitions, enabling direct calculation of dissociation rates and transition state distances over a broad force range. Applied to a DNA-gold nanoparticle-DNA construct under constant shear force, the model accurately reproduces the experimental room-temperature data in the covered force regime and provides a unified interpretation of prior measurements on similarly sheared duplexes across all force regimes. A central result is that the three-dimensional helical geometry of dsDNA is essential for correctly defining the end to end distance under shear in the rod-like polymer model of short dsDNA. We further show that the extracted transition state distances are robust to variations in ssDNA polymer parameters within the experimentally relevant regime. Finally, we analyze the temperature dependence of the transition state distance and discuss how our framework captures globally-heated rupture while identifying the additional complications introduced by localized plasmonic heating in gold nanoparticle-coupled constructs. These results provide a predictive kinetic foundation for interpreting force-rupture experiments and for designing force- and temperature-actuated DNA nanostructures.

### [67] [Anatomy of fast current-induced skyrmion motion in synthetic antiferromagnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09948)
*W. C. Chen,H. X. Yang,X. F. Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文揭示了合成反铁磁体（SAF）中斯格明子（skyrmion）的高迁移率不仅源于斯格明子霍尔效应（skyrmion Hall effect）的宏观抑制，还源于Gilbert阻尼参数α的微观降低；后者由反铁磁层间RKKY交换耦合增大斯格明子集体模式的磁振子（magnon）能隙、抑制阻尼主导的磁振子-电子散射率所致。该工作建立了一个双重机制框架，完整解释了SAF斯格明子的优异动力学特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有观点认为合成反铁磁体（synthetic antiferromagnets, SAFs）中电流驱动斯格明子的高迁移率主要归因于回转力（gyrotropic force）补偿导致斯格明子霍尔效应（skyrmion Hall effect）的宏观抑制。然而，这一解释忽略了Thiele方程中另一个关键参数——Gilbert阻尼参数α（Gilbert damping parameter）的显著降低，因此需要建立更完整的理论框架。

Method: 采用微观s-d模型（s-d model）进行分析，研究合成反铁磁体中强反铁磁层间Ruderman-Kittel-Kasuya-Yosida（RKKY）交换耦合对斯格明子集体模式磁振子能隙（magnonic gap）的影响，以及该机制对热磁振子布居（thermal magnon population）和磁振子-电子散射率（magnon-electron scattering rate）的调制作用。

Result: 强反铁磁层间RKKY交换耦合增大了SAF中斯格明子集体模式的磁振子能隙，从而抑制了热磁振子的布居，进而降低了在金属铁磁体中主导阻尼的磁振子-电子散射率，导致Gilbert阻尼参数α的衰减。

Conclusion: SAF斯格明子的优越动力学特性由双重机制共同决定：宏观拓扑效应（topological effect）修正运动方向，微观耗散机制（dissipation mechanism）减小运动阻力。两者的协同作用实现了高速、高效的运动，为Pham等人[Science 384, 307-312 (2024)]等近期实验报道的增强迁移率提供了基础性解释。

Abstract: The high mobility of current-driven skyrmions in synthetic antiferromagnets (SAFs) is widely explained by the macroscopic suppression of the skyrmion Hall effect through gyrotropic force compensation. This established view, however, overlooks a concurrent and significant reduction in the Gilbert damping parameter α, a key factor in the Thiele equation governing skyrmion velocity. Here, we show that this damping attenuation originates from a reconfigured magnon-electron scattering landscape. Using a microscopic s-d model, we demonstrate that the strong antiferromagnetic interlayer Ruderman-Kittel-Kasuya-Yosida (RKKY) exchange coupling in SAFs increases the magnonic gap of skyrmion collective modes, thereby suppressing the thermal magnon population and, consequently, the magnon-electron scattering rate that dominates damping in metallic ferromagnets. Our work establishes a dual-mechanism framework to fully explain the superior kinetics of SAF skyrmions: the macroscopic topological effect rectifies the motion direction, while the microscopic dissipation mechanism reduces the drag. This synergy enables high-speed and efficient motion, providing a fundamental elucidation of the enhanced mobility reported in recent studies such as the work by Pham et al. [Science 384, 307-312 (2024)].

</details>


### [68] [Dominant in-plane anomalous Hall effect in a monoclinic room-temperature ferromagnet](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10063)
*Guoxin Zheng,Arjyama Bordoloi,Mingjun Fan,Shunsuke Kitou,Hiraku Saito,Taro Nakajima,Sobhit Singh,Takashi Kurumaji,Linda Ye*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过在单斜Cr₃Te₄中工程化特定晶体学镜面对称性破缺，实现了室温铁磁状态下增强的面内反常霍尔效应，其面内霍尔信号比面外响应强五倍，并基于此展示了独特的面内场与电流传感功能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统反常霍尔效应（anomalous Hall effect）中，霍尔电流被限制在垂直于磁化强度（或外加磁场）的平面内。虽然某些对称性允许面内反常霍尔效应（in-plane anomalous Hall effect），但其信号通常远弱于传统霍尔响应。本研究旨在通过对称性工程大幅增强面内反常霍尔响应，实现室温下的强信号与新型传感功能。

Method: 通过工程化特定晶体学镜面对称性（crystallographic mirror symmetry）破缺，在具有室温铁磁性的单斜Cr₃Te₄中实现面内反常霍尔效应；结合密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）计算分析其电子结构。

Result: 在Cr₃Te₄中观测到强增强的面内反常霍尔响应，其面内信号超出面外响应五倍。基于该效应，实验演示了独特的面内场与电流传感功能。

Conclusion: 低晶体对称性铁磁体（low-crystalline-symmetry ferromagnets）且其费米面附近存在外尔点（Weyl points），可作为对称性工程化霍尔响应的实用平台，并为实现室温、几何灵活的传感器件提供了可行路径。

Abstract: Ferromagnetic metals are characterized by enhanced dissipationless transverse transport responses via the anomalous Hall effect, offering a route towards magnetic sensing and spintronic readout functionalities. In most ferromagnets, the anomalous Hall current is constrained to lie in the plane perpendicular to the magnetization (or applied magnetic field). Recently, it has been recognized that selected symmetries can also permit a Hall response in a traditionally forbidden configuration, where the Hall current lies in the same plane as the magnetization, realizing an in-plane anomalous Hall effect. Reported realizations of this effect, however, are typically much weaker than the conventional Hall response in the same material. Here, through engineering specific crystallographic mirror symmetry-breaking, we realize a strongly enhanced in-plane anomalous Hall response in monoclinic Cr3Te4 with room-temperature ferromagnetism. Remarkably, the in-plane anomalous Hall signal exceeds the out-of-plane response by a factor of five, with which we demonstrate a unique in-plane field and current sensing functionality. Combined with density functional theory calculations, our results establish low-crystalline-symmetry ferromagnets with near-Fermi-level Weyl points as a practical platform for symmetry-engineered Hall responses, and point to a route towards room-temperature, geometry-flexible sensing devices.

</details>


### [69] [Predicting Defect States: A Quick Screening Protocol for Substitutional Point Defect Engineering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10139)
*Hyosik Kang,Lukas Muechler*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 提出一种基于原胞（unit cell）的紧束缚（tight-binding）协议，通过从完整弛豫的小型原胞中提取Wannier紧束缚哈密顿量，快速预筛选晶体材料中的替代性点缺陷（substitutional defects），并在三种不同体系中验证了其有效性，尽管在绝对能量位置、高电负性原子空位及自洽电荷重分布效应方面存在局限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 晶体材料中的点缺陷（point defects）对电子、光学和磁性质至关重要，但系统地探索缺陷构型在计算上成本高昂，因为需要在周期性边界条件（periodic boundary conditions）下采用大型超胞（supercell）计算来近似孤立缺陷。

Method: 该协议从小型且完全弛豫的主晶格原胞和类缺陷原胞中提取Wannier紧束缚哈密顿量（Wannier tight-binding Hamiltonians），通过复制主晶格哈密顿量构建超胞模型，并仅修改替代位点的在位能（on-site energies）而保持跳迁参数（hopping parameters）不变，从而引入缺陷。

Result: 在过渡金属二硫属化物（transition-metal dichalcogenides）中的等结构替代缺陷、六方氮化硼（hexagonal boron nitride）中的对称性破缺碳替代缺陷以及金刚石中的氮空位（nitrogen-vacancy, NV⁻）中心三种体系中，协议成功捕获了带隙内态（in-gap states）的数量、简并度（degeneracies）及相对于宿主带边的浅层或深层特征，但在绝对能量位置上存在定量偏差。

Conclusion: 该协议能够快速预筛选替代性点缺陷，但仍无法处理高电负性原子空位以及涉及自洽电荷再分布（self-consistent charge redistribution）的电荷态或自旋极化（spin-polarization）效应。

Abstract: Point defects in crystalline materials play a central role in determining electronic, optical, and magnetic properties. However, systematic exploration of defect configurations remains computationally expensive because large supercell calculations are required to approximate isolated defects under periodic boundary conditions. We present a unit-cell-based tight-binding protocol that enables rapid pre-screening of substitutional defects. The protocol extracts Wannier tight-binding Hamiltonians from small, fully relaxed unit cells of the host and defect-like systems, replicates the host Hamiltonian to construct a supercell model, and introduces the defect by modifying only the on-site energies at the substitution site while leaving the hopping parameters unchanged. We validate the protocol across three diverse systems: isostructural substitutional defects in transition-metal dichalcogenides (M$_\mathrm{Mo}$ MoS$_2$, M = Ce, Zr, Nb, Tc, and Ru), symmetry-breaking carbon substitutions in hexagonal boron nitride (C$_\mathrm{B}$C$_\mathrm{N}$ h-BN), and nitrogen-vacancy (NV$^-$) centers in diamond. These case studies span two-dimensional and three-dimensional hosts, simple substitutions, and substitution-vacancy complexes. In all cases, the protocol successfully captures the number of in-gap states, their degeneracies, and their shallow or deep character relative to host band edges, despite some quantitative deviations in absolute energy positions. We further identify limitations for vacancies of highly electronegative atoms and for charge-state or spin-polarization effects, both of which involve self-consistent charge redistribution not captured by the protocol.

</details>


### [70] [Synthesis and Characterization of Atomically-Sharp Superconductor-Dielectric Interface](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10144)
*Nathan Sitaraman,Zhaslan Baraissov,Alexis Grassl,Hongbin Yang,Daniel Tong,David Muller,Matthias Liepe*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文从化学角度解释了氧化锆（ZrO₂）覆盖层为何能在铌（niobium）表面形成结晶态、保持尖锐界面并阻止铌氧化物再生，进而降低超导量子器件的介电损耗；同时提出了一种生长更高质量氧化锆层的新方法，并首次对其微观特性进行了全面分析。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超导体-介电体界面的性质已知会强烈影响超导量子器件的退相干时间（coherence times），这种影响被认为源于无序介电体和界面中“二能级系统”（two-level system, TLS）缺陷的浓度差异。氧化锆覆盖层虽被证明能降低损耗，但其优异的界面特性背后的化学机制尚不明确，且缺乏对ZrO₂覆盖层微观结构的系统分析。

Method: 基于ZrO₂的化学性质以及Nb-Zr-O三元相图（ternary system），从化学角度解释氧化锆层能形成结晶、保持尖锐界面并阻止铌氧化物再生的原因；同时提出一种新的生长方法，用于在铌上制备空气稳定性更高、结晶度更好且界面更尖锐的氧化锆覆盖层。

Result: 证明了氧化锆层之所以能形成结晶态、维持与金属铌的尖锐界面并阻止铌氧化物再生，源于ZrO₂的化学性质及Nb-Zr-O三元体系的特性；展示了一种新方法，所生长的氧化锆层在结晶度和界面尖锐度上均优于此前报道的结果。首次提供了对ZrO₂覆盖层微观特性的全面分析。

Conclusion: 该工作为理解氧化锆覆盖层降低超导量子器件介电损耗的化学根源提供了依据，所发展的高质量ZrO₂生长方法与微观分析结果为提升超导量子器件的性能奠定了重要基础。

Abstract: Modification of superconductor-dielectric interfaces is known to strongly impact coherence times of superconducting quantum devices. This relationship is thought to arise from differences in the concentration of "two-level system" defects in the disordered dielectrics and superconductor-dielectric interfaces; these defects couple to electromagnetic modes in the device and cause dissipation. Zirconium oxide barrier layers on niobium have emerged as a promising pathway to low-loss interfaces in recent years, evidently due to the crystalline nature of these layers in comparison to the amorphous niobium native oxide. We explain the unique ability of zirconium oxide to form a crystalline layer, to maintain a sharp interface with metallic niobium, and to prevent niobium oxide re-growth in terms of the chemical properties of ZrO$_2$ and the Nb-Zr-O ternary system. We demonstrate a new method to grow air-stable zirconium oxide layers on niobium with a higher level of crystallinity and a sharper oxide-metal interface than previously shown, and provide the first comprehensive microscopic analysis of ZrO$_2$ capping layer properties. These developments pave the way toward vital performance advances in superconducting quantum devices.

</details>


### [71] [Pressure-Driven Structural Phase Competition and Functional Response in Layered LiInP2S6](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10178)
*Xiaochi Xie,Pegah Mohammadi,Sobhit Singh*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过第一性原理密度泛函理论计算，研究了静水压力下LiInP2S6三种竞争性多晶型物（单斜C2/c相与三角P-31c相的层内和层间构型）的结构、力学、电子和光学性质。发现约0.38 GPa处存在由单斜C2/c基态相到三角P-31c层内相的压力诱导结构相变，并揭示了压力对相稳定性、力学特性及电子光学性质的差异化影响。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解静水压力如何调控层状量子材料中的层间相互作用（interlayer interactions）和竞争性离子构型（competing ionic configurations），对于控制其涌现功能特性至关重要。

Method: 采用第一性原理密度泛函理论（first-principles density-functional theory）计算，系统研究了压力下LiInP2S6的三种竞争性多晶型物——单斜C2/c相和三角P-31c相的层内（in-layer）与层间（in-gap）构型。

Result: 发现约0.38 GPa处存在从单斜C2/c基态相到三角P-31c层内相的压力诱导结构相变（pressure-induced structural phase transition），由增强的层间耦合和晶格各向异性压缩驱动。三角P-31c层间相因更强的层间离子相互作用和较低的可压缩性而始终能量不利。所有相在0-26 GPa压力范围内保持力学稳定，且力学刚性、弹性波速和德拜温度随压力增加而提高。各相内部的电子和光学性质在压力下高度鲁棒，仅带隙和光吸收边（紫外-可见光范围）发生适度变化，但跨结构相变时出现显著改变。

Conclusion: LiInP2S6是一种压力敏感的离子-范德华材料（ionic-vdW material），其中层间相互作用的细微变化主导着结构稳定性和功能性质。

Abstract: Understanding how hydrostatic pressure modifies interlayer interactions and competing ionic configurations is essential for controlling the emergent functional properties of layered quantum materials. Here, using first-principles density-functional theory calculations, we investigate the pressure-dependent structural, mechanical, electronic, and optical properties of three competing LiInP2S6 polymorphs: the monoclinic C2/c phase and the trigonal P-31c phase in both in-layer and in-gap configurations. Our results reveal a pressure-induced structural phase transition from the monoclinic ground-state C2/c phase to a trigonal P-31c in-layer phase at ~0.38 GPa, driven by enhanced interlayer coupling and anisotropic lattice compression. In contrast, the trigonal P-31c in-gap phase remains energetically unfavorable due to its stronger interlayer ionic interactions and reduced compressibility. All phases remain mechanically stable under compression (0-26 GPa) and exhibit enhanced mechanical rigidity, elastic wave velocities, and Debye temperatures with increasing pressure. Remarkably, the electronic and optical properties within each phase remain highly robust under pressure, with only moderate changes in the band gap and optical absorption edge (UV-Visible range) under pressure; however, substantial modifications emerge across the pressure-induced structural phase transition. These findings establish LiInP2S6 as a pressure sensitive ionic-vdW material in which subtle changes in interlayer interactions govern structural stability and functional properties.

</details>


### [72] [Graphlet Histogram Representation Database of Inorganic Crystals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10195)
*Aaditya Panigrahi,Yanjun Liu,Omri Lesser,Krishnanand Mallayya,Eun-Ah Kim*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出了 Graphlet-MP，一个基于图元（graphlet）直方图表示的无机晶体材料表征数据库，涵盖 149,082 种晶体，提供原子位点、成键对和键角三元组三个层次的结构描述，并配套开源工具，旨在为材料性质预测提供数据高效且可解释的替代方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有材料性质预测的机器学习模型大多依赖从大型密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）数据库中端到端学习到的表示，当实验数据稀缺时适用性受限。基于领域知识的预计算表示虽具数据高效性和可解释性，但现有方法最多只捕捉成分或键连接性，丢失了局部结构几何信息。

Method: Graphlet-MP 为 Materials Project 中的 149,082 种无机晶体预计算了图元直方图表示。每种材料通过三个层次图元阶次（graphlet order）的 79 种分布来描述：原子位点（atomic sites）、成键对（bonded pairs）和键角三元组（bond-angle triplets）。这些特征从晶体学信息文件（crystallographic information file, CIF）中经筛选的 Voronoi 镶嵌（screened Voronoi tessellation）提取。

Result: 研究提供了该表示的完整技术规范、用于在该空间中比较材料的推土机距离（Earth Mover's Distance, EMD）度量，以及完整的预计算数据库。同时发布了开源代码库，使用户能够为任意晶体结构（包括实验测定结构）生成图元直方图，并可将数据库扩展至新材料或目标性质。

Conclusion: Graphlet-MP 作为一种数据高效、可解释且开源的材料表征工具，弥补了现有领域知识驱动表示在局部结构几何信息上的缺失，为实验数据稀缺场景下的材料性质预测提供了可行方案。

Abstract: Machine learning models for materials property prediction increasingly rely on representations learned end-to-end from large density-functional-theory databases, limiting their applicability when only scarce experimental data are available. Domain-knowledge-driven representations precomputed from crystal structures alone offer a data-efficient, interpretable alternative, but existing approaches capture at most composition or bonding connectivity and discard local structural geometry. Here, we present Graphlet-MP, a database of graphlet histogram representations for 149,082 inorganic crystals from the Materials Project (MP). Seventy-nine distributions describe each material over three hierarchical graphlet orders: atomic sites, bonded pairs, and bond-angle triplets, extracted via screened Voronoi tessellation from the crystallographic information file. We provide a complete technical specification of the representation, an Earth Mover's Distance metric for comparing materials in this space, and the full precomputed database. An accompanying open-source codebase enables users to generate graphlet histograms for arbitrary crystal structures, including experimentally determined ones, and to extend the database to new materials or target properties.

</details>


### [73] [Finite-temperature Fe K-edge X-ray absorption simulations reveal local structural dynamics of an iron(II) photosensitizer in solution and the crystalline phase](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10221)
*Patrick Müller,Lorena Fritsch,Matthias Bauer,Thomas D. Kühne*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过结合Fe K边X射线吸收测量、第二代Car-Parrinello从头算分子动力学以及全电子高斯增强平面波模拟，对溶液相和晶相中的铁(II) N-杂环卡宾光敏剂进行系综平均谱计算，成功再现了近边特征，并揭示了柔性光敏剂中电子特征与热运动、溶剂无序及晶体堆积效应之间的结构-动力学关联。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解释柔性光敏剂的金属K边谱（metal K-edge spectra）需要一种能够将电子特征（electronic signatures）与热运动（thermal motion）、溶剂无序（solvent disorder）和晶体堆积效应（crystal-packing effects）分离开的结构模型。当前缺乏能够同时处理上述多种因素的理论-实验联合框架。

Method: 将Fe K边X射线吸收测量（X-ray absorption measurements）与第二代Car-Parrinello从头算分子动力学（Car-Parrinello ab initio molecular dynamics）以及全电子高斯增强平面波模拟（all-electron Gaussian and augmented-plane-wave simulations）相结合，对乙腈溶液和晶相中的铁(II) N-杂环卡宾（iron(II) N-heterocyclic carbene）光敏剂进行系综平均（ensemble-averaged）谱计算。

Result: 系综平均谱成功再现了两种环境下的主要近边特征（near-edge features），并保持了实验观察到的溶解后第一Fe配位壳层（first Fe coordination shell）的相似性。与扩展精细结构测量（extended fine-structure measurements）提取的径向分布对比验证了轨迹采样的Fe-N和Fe-C配位壳层，而元素分辨对分布（element-resolved pair distributions）解释了高阶壳层实验对比度迅速丧失的原因。动力学系综还揭示了三联吡啶氮原子存在宽的面外分布（broad out-of-plane distribution）以及Fe中心配位面呈现近八面体分布（nearly octahedral distribution）。

Conclusion: 有限温度X射线吸收模拟（finite-temperature X-ray absorption simulations）能够通过单一路径描述（trajectory-based description）将局域谱、溶剂相配体运动和中等范围结构无序（medium-range structural disorder）联系起来，为分子过渡金属光敏剂提供紧凑的结构-动力学图像（structural-dynamics picture）。

Abstract: Interpreting metal K-edge spectra of flexible photosensitizers requires a structural model that separates electronic signatures from thermal motion, solvent disorder, and crystal-packing effects. We combine Fe K-edge X-ray absorption measurements with second-generation Car--Parrinello ab initio molecular dynamics and all-electron Gaussian and augmented-plane-wave simulations for an iron(II) N-heterocyclic carbene photosensitizer in acetonitrile solution and in the crystalline phase. Ensemble-averaged spectra reproduce the main near-edge features in both environments and preserve the experimentally observed similarity of the first Fe coordination shell upon dissolution. Comparison with radial distributions extracted from extended fine-structure measurements validates the Fe--N and Fe--C coordination shells sampled by the trajectories, while element-resolved pair distributions explain why higher-shell experimental contrast is rapidly lost. The same dynamical ensembles reveal a broad out-of-plane distribution of the terpyridine nitrogen atom and a nearly octahedral distribution of the Fe-centered coordination planes. The results show that finite-temperature X-ray absorption simulations can provide a compact structural-dynamics picture of molecular transition metal photosensitizers by linking local spectra, solvent-phase ligand motion, and medium-range structural disorder within one trajectory-based description.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 该工作流包含三个核心步骤：首先，利用基于ICSD的Wyckoff位点替换（Wyckoff-site substitution）和MatterGen的条件结构生成（conditional structure generation）两种策略扩展候选材料空间；其次，使用领域微调（domain-finetuned）的DPA3机器学习原子间势对热力学和动力学稳定性进行高效预筛选；最后，对预筛选通过的候选结构执行高精度的DFT计算验证。

Result: 工作流识别出3,574种此前未见报道的稳定磷化物结构，其中包含196种HSE06带隙在0–3.0 eV范围内的半导体。进一步筛选发现30种有前景的光电子候选材料和26种热电候选材料，其中7种为全新发现的光电子材料，8种为全新发现的热电材料。

Conclusion: 所发现的材料为实验合成提供了候选材料池，并表明将生成式AI与机器学习原子间势相结合能够加速功能半导体材料的发现过程。

Abstract: Metal phosphides have diverse bonding motifs and coordination environments, making them promising for optoelectronic and thermoelectric applications, but their chemical space remains underexplored. Here we report an AI-driven high-throughput discovery workflow that combines generative materials design, machine-learning interatomic potentials, and targeted density functional theory (DFT) calculations. ICSD-derived Wyckoff-site substitution and MatterGen-based conditional structure generation are used to expand the candidate space beyond existing phosphide databases. A domain-finetuned DPA3 machine-learning potential then enables efficient prescreening of thermodynamic and dynamical stability before DFT validation. This workflow identifies 3,574 previously unreported stable phosphide structures, including 196 semiconductors with HSE06 band gaps of 0-3.0 eV. By screening these new semiconductors together with experimentally known phosphide semiconductors, we identify 30 promising optoelectronic candidates and 26 promising thermoelectric candidates, including seven newly discovered optoelectronic materials and eight newly discovered thermoelectric materials. These results provide a candidate pool for experimental synthesis and show that combining generative AI with machine-learning interatomic potentials can accelerate the discovery of functional semiconductor materials.

### [75] [Neural electron backscatter diffraction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10352)
*I-Tzu Huang,Marat I. Latypov*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出神经EBSD（neural EBSD）方法，将电子背散射衍射（EBSD）扫描视为连续的、可微的四维菊池衍射强度场，并通过基于坐标的神经网络表示，实现了高精度重建、超分辨率、连续空间查询以及大幅数据压缩（700倍）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统EBSD技术将连续的多晶显微组织离散化到网格上进行记录与分析，这种离散化限制了后续处理的精度与灵活性，无法实现亚网格尺度的连续查询和空间导数计算。

Method: 将EBSD扫描建模为连续可微的四维强度场（样品-探测器域），采用基于坐标的神经网络（coordinate-based neural network）表示。提出了联合映射（joint formulation）和分解映射（factorized formulation）两种方案，后者将连续样品域系数场与学习的探测器域基函数（basis patterns）相结合。

Result: 在再结晶和增材制造的Inconel 718合金上的实验表明，分解映射方案重建菊池图案的平均误差低于最大强度的1%。该方法实现了样品帧内的全图案超分辨率（full-pattern super-resolution）、任意离网格路径的连续查询，以及通过解析空间导数实现空间连续的边界和异质性定位。存储网络权重和基函数替代原始图案可实现700倍压缩。

Conclusion: 神经EBSD通过连续可微表示突破了传统EBSD离散网格的限制，在重建精度、超分辨率、空间连续分析和大规模数据压缩方面展现出显著优势，为EBSD数据的后续分析提供了新的范式。

Abstract: In a polycrystalline microstructure, orientation and dislocation content vary smoothly within grains, and the grain boundaries between them are continuous curves. Electron backscatter diffraction (EBSD) records this continuum on a discrete grid with every subsequent analysis (from indexing to advanced pattern processing) confined to that grid. We introduce neural EBSD, which treats an EBSD scan as a continuous, differentiable four-dimensional field of Kikuchi diffraction intensity (in specimen--detector domain) and then represents it with a coordinate-based neural network. We develop and compare two formulations: a joint formulation that maps all four coordinates to intensity, and a factorized formulation that combines continuous specimen-domain coefficient fields with learned detector-domain basis patterns. Tested on recrystallized and additively manufactured Inconel 718, the factorized formulation shows better accuracy in reconstructing Kikuchi patterns that have map-averaged errors below 1% of the maximum intensity. Beyond reconstruction, it provides full-pattern super-resolution in the specimen frame, continuous querying along arbitrary off-grid paths, as well as spatially continuous boundary and heterogeneity localization from analytical spatial derivatives. Storing the network weights and learned bases in place of the raw patterns in a large dataset offers a 700-fold compression while preserving on-demand access to the full patterns for downstream analyses.

### [77] [Optical-like interference control polar-phonons dispersions in 2D materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10549)
*Benoit Van Troeye,Geoffrey Pourtois*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过经典电动力学中的镜像电荷框架（mirror-charge framework）重新审视二维材料的极性声子模（polar phonon modes），指出在完美反射介电边界条件下，二维材料仍可恢复LO-TO分裂（LO-TO splitting）或等效的面外模现象，挑战了此前认为二维材料极性声子色散在布里渊区中心呈线性且LO-TO分裂消失的论断。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有理论认为，由于二维材料相比三维晶体降低了维度，其极性声子模在布里渊区（Brillouin zone）中心附近应呈线性色散，从而导致纵向光学-横向光学分裂（LO-TO splitting）消失。作者希望重新检验这一结论是否正确。

Method: 采用源自经典电动力学（classical electrostatics）的镜像电荷框架（mirror-charge framework）进行分析，考察介电边界条件对二维材料极性声子模色散的影响。

Result: 在完美反射介电界面（perfectly-reflective dielectric interfaces）条件下，二维材料可以恢复LO-TO分裂，或对于面外模（out-of-plane modes）产生等效现象。极性声子模的色散实际上由源势（source potential）及其在介电界面处的反射所产生的类光学（optical-like）相长干涉与相消干涉共同决定。

Conclusion: 介电边界条件（dielectric boundary conditions）对理解二维材料中与声子相关的性质具有关键作用，此前关于二维材料极性声子模行为的简化论断并不总是成立。

Abstract: It has been argued that the polar phonon modes of two-dimensional (2D) materials should show a linear dependence close to the Brillouin zone center due to the reduced problem dimensionality compared to a three-dimensional crystal, leading to a vanishing LO-TO splitting. Revisiting this question using a mirror-charge framework derived from classical electrostatics, we show that it is not always true: with perfectly-reflective dielectric interfaces, it is possible to recover a LO-TO splitting, or an equivalent phenomenon for the out-of-plane modes. Effectively, the dispersion of polar phonon modes is governed by optical-like constructive and destructive interferences of the source potential with its reflection at the dielectric interfaces. This work highlights the critical role of dielectric boundary conditions to understand phonon-related properties in 2D materials.

### [78] [Extending Field Limits in Nanoscale Magnetic Imaging with Metamaterial-inspired Magnetic Flux Concentrators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10570)

Conclusion: 通过调节MFC的几何形状和材料参数可优化其性能以适应样品和实验约束，该策略具有可调性和广泛适用性，能够扩展多种纳米尺度磁成像技术的可访问磁场范围。

Abstract: Many nanoscale magnetic imaging techniques are constrained by the maximum magnetic field that can be applied during measurements, due to geometrical limitations or interactions with the probe or the detected signal (e.g., electrons). Here, it is demonstrated that sample-integrated metamaterial-inspired magnetic flux concentrators (MFCs) locally amplify magnetic fields, allowing observation of magnetization processes beyond instrumental limits. Micrometer-sized MFCs fabricated directly on the samples are tested in photoemission electron microscopy experiments employing X-ray magnetic circular dichroism as magnetic contrast mechanism. At low applied fields, substantial amplification factors enable observation of magnetization reversal in a chain of magnetite nanoparticles synthesized by magnetotactic bacteria at an applied field of 8 mT, substantially smaller than the 50 mT predicted by simulations in absence of MFCs. At higher fields, the field enhancement extends the accessible field range by a factor of five, enabling for the first time, imaging of the field-dependent magnetic domain structure evolution of an isolated giant magnetofossil. Finally, we show how MFC geometry and material parameters can be tuned to optimize performance considering sample and experimental constraints, providing a tunable and broadly applicable strategy for extending the accessible field range in a wide variety of nanoscale magnetic imaging techniques.

</details>

Abstract: High-entropy materials are complex, multifunctional materials that have reshaped the design of advanced functional materials. Abstract: Strongly correlated two-dimensional systems provide compelling platforms for investigating exotic quantum phenomena. ### [81] [Efficient analytic continuation approach to Bethe-Salpeter excitation spectra in selected energy windows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10849)
*Ivan Duchemin,Xavier Blase*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出利用解析延拓（analytic continuation）技术在复频率平面上构建Bethe-Salpeter吸收谱，通过迭代计算少量极化率张量并建立连分式（continued-fraction）表示，从而高效获取目标能量范围内的吸收光谱，并展示了在分子和团簇体系中的应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统Bethe-Salpeter方程（BSE）在实频率轴上直接计算吸收谱计算成本高昂，尤其是在宽能量范围或高能区。本文旨在探索利用解析延拓技术，通过复平面采样来降低计算开销，同时保持光谱精度。

Method: 在复频率平面上选取一组较稀疏的采样点$(z_k)$，迭代计算对应的极化率张量$\bar{\barα}(z_k)$；利用这些数据构建$\bar{\barα}(z)$的连分式表示，进而计算实轴附近目标能量范围内的吸收谱。连分式的系数为矩阵值（matrix-valued coefficients），以完整描述极化率张量。还展示了如何从连分式中提取极点（poles）以辅助光谱分析。

Result: 以二肽（dipeptide）的价激发（valence excitations）、C$_{60}$富勒烯及其PCBM衍生物、Ag$_{20}$银团簇的表面等离激元共振（surface plasmon resonance）为案例验证了方法的有效性，并进一步探索了C$_{60}$的高能X射线吸收谱（X-ray absorption spectrum）。

Conclusion: 基于解析延拓的连分式方法能够高效、准确地构建Bethe-Salpeter吸收谱，矩阵值系数的引入确保了极化率张量的完整描述，极点提取功能为光谱解析提供了额外工具，适用于从低能价激发到高能X射线吸收的广泛能量范围。

Abstract: We explore the merits of building the Bethe-Salpeter absorption spectrum in a specific energy range using analytic continuation techniques. Specifically, we calculate iteratively a few $\bar{\bar α}(z_k)$ polarizability tensors for a coarse set of $(z_k)$ frequencies in the complex-plane. These data allow constructing a continued-fraction representation for $\bar{\barα}(z)$ that is used to calculate the absorption spectrum close to the real energy axis in the desired energy range. The number and location of these sampling complex frequencies are discussed. The importance of building a continued-fraction representation of the full polarizability tensor with matrix-valued coefficients is emphasized. We show how to extract the poles of the continued fraction as a tool for analyzing the resulting spectra. We study as examples the valence excitations of a paradigmatic dipeptide, the C$_{60}$ fullerene and its PCBM derivative, together with the description of the surface plasmon resonance of the Ag$_{20}$ silver cluster. Further, the high-energy C$_{60}$ X-ray absorption spectrum is explored.

Abstract: We investigate optically excited spin dynamics in a uniaxial ferrimagnet near the magnetization compensation point under a magnetic field applied along the magnetic anisotropy axis. Experiment and numerical modeling reveal an unusual regime where the frequencies of two spin eigenmodes approach each other and become highly field sensitive. The modes, corresponding to opposite rotations of the Neel vector, simultaneously reverse their handedness at a critical field where their frequencies become degenerate. Employing state-of-the-art $ab~initio$ techniques, this work systematically investigates the influence of various experimentally reported defects on the magnetic properties of bulk and monolayer MBT at different concentrations. Mn-vacancy and Mn-rich defects are found to enhance the ferromagnetism of bulk MBT.
