### [84] [Direction-Dependent Quantum Transport Properties of MoS$_2$ Integrated into Biphenylene Configuration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11027)
*Gözde Özbal Sargın*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

Abstract: Motivated by the experimental realization of the two-dimensional (2D) carbon biphenylene network (BPN), the theoretical extension of the BPN topology to various groups of elements was successfully implemented. The current-voltage ($I-V$) characteristics demonstrate an exceptionally strong transport anisotropy, characterized by a substantial current ratio of $I_{\text{armchair}}/I_{\text{zigzag}} \approx 7 \times 10^4$. Furthermore, while the current along the armchair direction increases steadily with the applied bias, transport along the zigzag direction is characterized by a pronounced intrinsic negative differential conductance (NDC). This contrast highlights fundamentally distinct charge transport mechanisms along the two orthogonal axes. Consequently, different directions of this BPN phase of MoS$_2$ can be tailored for distinct nanoelectronic applications, where the armchair and zigzag axes serve as a reliable current switch and an active NDC device, respectively.

### [86] [Synthetic pre-training of graph-network models for predicting solid-state NMR parameters](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11038)
*Chiheb Ben Mahmoud,Carlos Bornes,Christopher J. Heard,Lukáš Grajciar,Jonathan R. Yates,Volker L. Deringer*

TL;DR: 本文提出一种合成预训练与微调协议，用于固态核磁共振（NMR）参数的图神经网络（graph-based ML）建模，通过先在合成张量数据上预训练、再在真实数据上微调，显著提升数据效率，并初步探索了化学可迁移性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 核磁共振（NMR）是探测原子结构的强有力手段，但精确的量子力学预测张量NMR参数计算成本高昂，既阻碍了直接的量子力学研究，也限制了为机器学习（ML）模型收集高质量训练数据的能力。

Method: 引入一种合成预训练与微调（pre-training and fine-tuning）协议：先在从已有ML模型获得的合成张量数据上预训练图基ML模型，再在新标注的真实数据（ground-truth data）上进行微调。

Result: 当预训练与微调覆盖相同的组分与构型空间（compositional and configurational space）时，数据效率（data efficiency）显著提升；此外，初步实验探索了化学可迁移性（chemical transferability）。

Conclusion: 该工作为固态NMR张量ML模型的数据高效训练流程提供了路线：将廉价的合成监督信号与有针对性的第一性原理（first-principles）精修相结合。

Abstract: Nuclear magnetic resonance (NMR) is a powerful probe of atomic structure, but accurate quantum-mechanical predictions of tensorial NMR parameters are computationally demanding. This creates a bottleneck both for direct quantum-mechanical studies and for collecting high-quality training data for machine-learning (ML) models. Here, we introduce a synthetic pre-training and fine-tuning protocol for graph-based ML models of solid-state NMR parameters. We first pre-train models on synthetic tensorial data, as obtained using an existing ML model, and subsequently fine-tune those models on new ground-truth data. We observe a pronounced improvement in data efficiency when pre-training and fine-tuning span the same compositional and configurational space, and we carry out initial experiments regarding chemical transferability. Our work outlines a route toward future data-efficient training workflows for tensorial ML models for solid-state NMR, combining inexpensive synthetic supervision with targeted first-principles refinement.

</details>


### [87] [In-situ total scattering investigation of crystalline ordering in amorphous ion-beam sputtered thin films for interferometric gravitational wave detectors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11059)

Method: 采用同步辐射散射实验（synchrotron radiation scattering experiment）进行原位测量；利用X射线衍射（X-Ray Diffraction）和Rietveld分析研究退火过程中的结晶行为；通过原子对分布函数（Pair Distribution Function, PDF）分析考察非晶到晶体转变期间的结构变化。

Result: 多种结构重排同时发生：首先阳离子亚结构在约100 Å范围内快速形成骨架（backbone structure），随后氧原子环境逐渐重排，材料的结晶度（crystallinity）逐步提高。

Conclusion: 非晶氧化钽在退火中的结构演化包含两个并行的过程：阳离子骨架的快速建立和氧原子环境的渐进式重排，后者主导了从非晶到晶态的转变。

Abstract: Amorphous tantala is an important optical material used in a number of high-precision optical applications, including gravitational wave interferometry. In this paper, we study in-situ the structural changes that occur in amorphous ion-beam sputtered coatings during an annealing treatment by means of a synchrotron radiation scattering experiment. The scattering signal is measured as a function of time on a large range of the Q-space. X-Ray diffraction and Rietveld analysis are used to study crystallization during the annealing treatment, whereas pair distribution function analysis allows to inspect the structural changes occurring during the amorphous to crystalline transition. Our findings indicate that several structural rearrangements occur in parallel, namely a first quick establishment of a backbone structure in the cationic substructure appearing on a rather extended range (up to 100 Angstrom), followed by a progressive rearrangement of the oxygen atoms environment which gradually increases the crystallinity of the structure.

### [88] [Approaching the Limit of Intrinsic Crystalline Thermal Insulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11072)
*Ruihuan Cheng,Zhiqiang Cui,Mani Jayaraman,Lincong Ji,Chen Wang,Zesheng Zeng,Petr Levinsky,Jiri Hejtmanek,Christophe Candolfi,Emmanuel Guilmeau,Xingchen Shen,Yue Chen*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 提出了一种集成通用机器学习原子间势（universal machine learning interatomic potentials）与高保真声子输运理论（high-fidelity phonon transport theories）的高通量工作流，用于加速超低热导率晶体材料的发现。通过该方法识别出数十种室温热导率低于0.2 W m⁻¹ K⁻¹的晶体，其中CsTlI₄以0.14 W m⁻¹ K⁻¹创下纪录，并建立了与超低热导率强相关的物理可解释描述符。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超低热导率晶体材料是潜在的热障涂层或热电材料，但传统的试错法（trial-and-error）发现效率低下，亟需更高效的筛选策略。

Method: 开发了一套高通量工作流（high-throughput workflow），将通用机器学习原子间势（universal machine learning interatomic potentials）与高保真声子输运理论（high-fidelity phonon transport theories）相结合，实现热绝缘体的快速探索。

Result: 识别出数十种室温本征热导率低于0.2 W m⁻¹ K⁻¹的晶体，并实验验证了CsTlI₄在300 K下具有0.14 W m⁻¹ K⁻¹的超低热导率。基于原子间力常数（interatomic force constants）建立了与超低热导率强相关的物理可解释描述符。

Conclusion: 这项工作展示了加速热绝缘体发现的数据驱动策略（data-driven strategy），并揭示了层级键合（hierarchical bonding）与强非简谐性（strong anharmonicity）协同抑制热载振动（heat-carrying vibrations）的微观机制。

Abstract: Crystalline materials with ultralow thermal conductivity ($κ$) are potential thermal barrier coatings or thermoelectrics, yet the discovery of ultralow-$κ$ materials remains inefficient due to the limitations of trial-and-error approaches. Herein, we propose a state-of-the-art high-throughput workflow that integrates universal machine learning interatomic potentials with high-fidelity phonon transport theories to accelerate the exploration of thermal insulators. Applying this approach, we identify dozens of crystalline materials with intrinsic room-temperature $κ$ values below 0.2 $\rm W m^{-1} K^{-1}$. Among them, we report and experimentally validate CsTlI$_4$, a record-breaking material with an ultralow $κ$ of 0.14 $\rm W m^{-1} K^{-1}$ at 300 K. Structural and bond analyses reveal that a hierarchical bonding framework, consisting of multi-coordinated Cs-I and antibonding Tl-I interactions, leads to weak chemical bonding and a soft lattice. These features reduce phonon group velocities, enhance phonon scattering, and induce strong vibrational mismatch between sublattices, collectively suppressing both particle-like phonon propagation and wave-like tunneling. Beyond this specific system, we establish physically interpretable descriptors based on interatomic force constants that correlate strongly with ultralow $κ$ and capture the role of bonding hierarchy and coordination environments in governing thermal transport. This work demonstrates a robust data-driven strategy for accelerating the discovery of thermal insulators and provides microscopic insight into how hierarchical bonding and strong anharmonicity cooperate to impede heat-carrying vibrations.

### [89] [Flower-like WO3-modified Vulcan carbon GDEs for photoelectro-Fenton process: Efficient ciprofloxacin degradation and mechanistic insights](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11114)
*João Paulo C. Moura,Vanessa S. Antonin,Caio Machado Fernandes,Aline B. Trench,Erica S. Conrado,Michell O. Almeida,Kathia M. Honorio,Renata Colombo,Rafael Sotana,Ana M. P. Neto,Mauro C. Santos*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文研究了基于3% WO3/C气体扩散电极（GDE）的电化学H2O2合成，该电极表现出优于纯碳载体的性能，并进一步应用于电芬顿（electro Fenton, EF）和光电芬顿（photoelectro Fenton, PEF）体系中降解环丙沙星（ciprofloxacin, CIP）。WO3/C的协同效应促进了H2O2生成和污染物矿化，经理论分析验证降解产物的环境毒性显著降低，为废水 remediation 提供高效策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用3% WO3/C气体扩散电极（GDE）作为阴极，对比裸露Vulcan碳载体，在50、75、100 mA cm⁻²电流密度下测定H2O2产量和电流效率。将WO3/C GDE应用于电芬顿（EF）降解环丙沙星（CIP），并引入紫外光构建光电芬顿（PEF）体系，结合硼掺杂金刚石（boron doped diamond, BDD）阳极提升矿化率。通过理论分析评估降解产物的环境毒性。

Result: 在50、75、100 mA cm⁻²下，H2O2浓度分别达到423、586、916 mg L⁻¹，电流效率约70%。WO3/C GDE在电芬顿（EF）体系中30分钟内实现约70%的环丙沙星（CIP）初始降解，但后期受限于Fe²⁺再生缓慢。引入紫外光的光电芬顿（PEF）体系在90分钟内实现CIP完全去除，结合BDD阳极后总有机碳（total organic carbon, TOC）矿化率达66%。降解机制涉及羟基自由基攻击哌嗪环、脱氟及喹诺酮环氧化。

Conclusion: WO3/C气体扩散电极（GDE）凭借WO3与碳的协同效应，在H2O2合成和废水处理中表现出高效低能耗的优势，光电芬顿（PEF）与BDD阳极的组合进一步克服了传统电芬顿（EF）的局限性，为有机污染物彻底矿化提供了可行途径。

Abstract: Electrochemical H2O2 synthesis was investigated using a 3 percent WO3 C gas diffusion electrode GDE. The catalyst outperformed bare Vulcan carbon, generating H2O2 concentrations of 423, 586, and 916 mg L at 50, 75, and 100 mA cm2, respectively, maintaining around 70 percent current efficiency. This performance and lower energy consumption are attributed to the WO3 carbon synergistic effect. In electro Fenton EF applications, the WO3 C GDE achieved rapid initial ciprofloxacin CIP degradation of around 70 percent in 30 min, though limited later by slow Fe2 regeneration. Incorporating UV light photoelectro Fenton overcame this constraint, yielding complete CIP removal within 90 min, while a boron doped diamond BDD anode enhanced total organic carbon TOC mineralization to 66 percent. The proposed degradation mechanism proceeds via hydroxyl radical attack on the piperazine ring with or without defluorination and quinolone ring oxidation, with theoretical analysis confirming reduced environmental toxicity of the transformation products. Overall, WO3 C GDEs represent a highly efficient strategy for H2O2 generation and wastewater remediation.

### [90] [Roughness-robust surface altermagnetism in $PT$ antiferromagnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11128)
*K. D. Belashchenko*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文研究了粗糙表面下交变磁体（altermagnet）的宏观自旋-动量关联对称性，提出粗糙表面交变磁性由表面反对称劳厄点群（surface antisymmetry Laue point group）决定，并在PT对称反铁磁体中为自旋电子学功能提供了新路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有分类仅适用于原子级平整表面平台的局域对称性（local symmetry），而实际表面往往粗糙不平，自旋分裂（spin splitting）如何在宏观平均后仍存在尚不清楚。论文旨在解决粗糙表面上交变磁性（surface altermagnetism）的对称性约束与分类问题。

Method: 通过对称性分析，引入表面反对称劳厄点群来表征粗糙表面宏观自旋-动量关联（spin-momentum correlations）的对称性。基于反对称空间群（antisymmetry space group）中是否包含反平移操作（antitranslations）来判断粗糙表面交变磁性的存在性。

Result: 粗糙表面交变磁性在任何反对称空间群包含反平移的磁体中是被禁止的，因此分类简化为PT对称反铁磁体（$PT$-symmetric antiferromagnets）。粗糙化可以从未补偿的平整终端产生补偿表面交变磁体（compensated surface altermagnets），提高表面对称性，或抑制自旋分裂。

Conclusion: 粗糙表面交变磁性在PT对称反铁磁体中兼具体可切换性（bulk switchability）与表面输运特性，为自旋电子学功能（spintronic functionality）提供了可行途径。

Abstract: Surface altermagnetism extends spin splitting beyond bulk altermagnets through symmetry reduction at surfaces and interfaces. An existing classification applies to the local symmetry of atomically flat surface terraces. The present paper addresses the symmetry of macroscopic spin-momentum correlations that survive averaging over compensated rough surfaces. These correlations are governed by the surface antisymmetry Laue point group. Rough-surface altermagnetism is forbidden at any surface of a magnet whose antisymmetry space group contains antitranslations, and the classification therefore reduces to $PT$-symmetric antiferromagnets. By restoring all symmetries leaving the surface normal invariant, roughness can generate compensated surface altermagnets from uncompensated flat terminations, increase the surface symmetry, or suppress spin splitting. By combining bulk switchability with altermagnetic surface transport properties, roughness-robust surface altermagnetism in $PT$-symmetric antiferromagnets provides a route toward spintronic functionality.

</details>

### [91] [Fabry-Perot Interference, g-factor Anisotropy, and Gate-Tunable Quantum dot in Chiral Tellurium Nanowires](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10001)
*Suresh Ghimire,Mohammad Hafijur Rahaman,Nathan Tanner Sawyers,Madan Mohan Bhandari,Gokul Acharya,Syed Zulfiqar Hussain Shah,Iris Nandhakumar,Pawan Kumar,Zainul Aabdin Khan,Hugh O. H. Churchill,Dharmraj Kotekar-Patil*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文展示了水热法生长的碲（tellurium，Te）纳米线中的相位相干准弹道输运、各向异性塞曼光谱（Zeeman spectroscopy）和栅极可调量子点行为，揭示了由两端电阻驱动的准弹道与强局域化输运之间的转变，并测得了高度各向异性的朗德g因子（Lande g-factor）和自旋轨道能隙（spin-orbit energy gap），确立了手性碲纳米线作为栅极定义自旋量子比特（spin qubit）和混合碲-超导体马约拉纳零模（Majorana zero modes）平台的潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 具有强自旋轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）的手性材料为探索拓扑（topology）、手性（chirality）与量子输运之间的相互作用提供了独特平台，但元素碲（elemental tellurium）纳米结构中的量子相干（quantum coherent）区域此前尚未得到充分研究。

Method: 采用水热法生长碲纳米线，制备单根纳米线场效应晶体管（field-effect transistor, FET），通过电输运测量和塞曼光谱分析表征其量子输运特性，并利用栅极电压调控量子点（quantum dot）形成。

Result: 器件呈p型输运，空穴迁移率从210 K时的约80 cm² V⁻¹ s⁻¹升至1 K时的约190 cm² V⁻¹ s⁻¹，约50 K处存在由声子限制（phonon-limited）散射到库仑散射（Coulomb scattering）主导的转变；低电阻器件（<30 kΩ）表现出法布里-珀罗干涉（Fabry-Perot interference），高电阻器件（>30 kΩ）呈现库仑阻塞（Coulomb-blockade）行为；面内g因子g∥=1.18，面外g因子g⊥=18.41，自旋轨道能隙ΔSO=0.864 meV。

Conclusion: 手性碲纳米线可作为栅极定义自旋量子比特和混合碲-超导体马约拉纳零模架构的多功能平台，利用其大且可调的g因子在元素范德华（van der Waals, vdW）体系中实现量子相干操控。

Abstract: Chiral materials with strong spin-orbit coupling offer a unique platform for exploring the interplay between topology, chirality, and quantum transport yet the quantum coherent regime in elemental tellurium nanostructures remains largely unexplored. Here we demonstrate phase-coherent quasi-ballistic transport, anisotropic Zeeman spectroscopy, and gate-tunable quantum dot formation in hydrothermally grown t-tellurium nanowires. Single nanowire field-effect transistors exhibit p-type transport with hole mobilities rising from approx. 80 cm2 V-1 s-1 at 210 K to approx. 190 cm2 V-1 s-1 at 1 K, consistent with a crossover from phonon-limited to Coulomb scattering dominated regimes near 50 K. Notably, devices segregate into two distinct regimes based on their room temperature two-terminal resistance : low-resistance devices (< 30 kOhm) exhibit Fabry-Perot interference, whereas high resistance devices (> 30 kOhm) display Coulomb-blockade behavior revealing a two-terminal resistance-driven transition between quasi-ballistic and strongly localized transport regimes. Zeeman spectroscopy in in-plane and out-of-plane magnetic fields yields highly anisotropic Lande g-factors (an in-plane gparallel = 1.18 and an out-of-plane gperp = 18.41) and directly resolves a spin-orbit energy gap DeltaSO = 0.864 meV from an avoided crossing. These results establish chiral tellurium nanowires as a versatile platform for gate-defined spin qubits exploiting large, tunable g-factors and for hybrid tellurium-superconductor architectures targeting Majorana zero modes in an elemental vdW system.

### [92] [Higher-winding phases in one-dimensional non-Hermitian topological superconductors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10418)
*Yung-Yeh Chang,Xiang-Yu Li,Ken Shiozaki,Chen-Hsuan Hsu*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于系数（coefficient-based）的方法，用于计算一维非厄米拓扑超导体（non-Hermitian topological superconductors）的绕数（winding numbers）并解析推导相边界，应用于包含高阶跳跃项的晶格模型，揭示了更高绕数拓扑相，并阐明了弱扰动对非厄米趋肤效应（non-Hermitian skin effect）的抑制及其与马约拉纳零模（Majorana zero modes）的关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非厄米拓扑超导体中，点隙拓扑（point-gap topology）、非厄米趋肤效应与马约拉纳零模三者紧密交织，现有方法难以系统处理包含高阶跳跃项的更大参数空间及更高绕数的拓扑相，亟需一种系统高效的计算和相图构建方法。

Method: 采用基于系数的方法计算绕数并解析推导具有ℤ不变量的点隙拓扑一维非厄米拓扑超导体的相边界；将该方法应用于两个晶格模型（含或不含子晶格自由度），并引入更长程跳跃项以生成高阶多项式；通过开放边界谱验证绕数，并利用逆参与率（inverse participation ratio）检验零模对无序的稳定性。

Result: 该方法成功解析了扩展参数空间中的相边界，支持产生更高绕数的拓扑相；弱扰动可抑制非厄米趋肤效应，同时保持子晶格对称性保护的马约拉纳零模对应的不变量；开放边界谱中观察到与体态不变量一致的一对或多对零能边界模。

Conclusion: 该系数化方法为构建更高绕数非厄米拓扑超导体的拓扑相图提供了系统高效的途径。

Abstract: Non-Hermitian topological superconductors provide a setting in which point-gap topology, non-Hermitian skin effects, and Majorana zero modes are strongly intertwined. In this work, we adopt a coefficient-based approach for computing winding numbers and deriving analytical expressions for phase boundaries in one-dimensional non-Hermitian topological superconductors characterized by point-gap topology with $\mathbb{Z}$ invariants. We apply this approach to two non-Hermitian topological superconducting lattice models, with and without sublattice degrees of freedom, including longer-range hoppings, thereby accessing a much broader parameter space. These extensions generate higher-order polynomials and support phases with higher winding numbers, reflecting the underlying $\mathbb{Z}$ topology. We further clarify how a weak perturbation suppresses the non-Hermitian skin effect while preserving the sublattice-symmetry-protected invariant associated with Majorana zero modes. The predicted winding numbers are verified by open-boundary spectra, where one or multiple pairs of zero-energy boundary modes appear consistently with the bulk invariant. We also examine the stability of these modes against onsite disorder through the inverse participation ratio. Our results provide a systematic and efficient route to constructing topological phase diagrams for higher-winding non-Hermitian topological superconductors.

### [93] [Electrical Spectroscopy of Intervalley Relaxation in WSe$_2$ Transistors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10470)
*Katsunori Wakabayashi*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出多层WSe₂场效应晶体管的跨导可作为谷间弛豫时间τ_iv的直接电学谱仪，通过扩展平衡谷热力学框架与单一弛豫方程，预测了三种可由标准射频和直流仪器测量的电学特征，从而替代以往仅能通过超快光学技术获得的谷间弛豫时间测量方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 谷间弛豫时间τ_iv是描述多层过渡金属二硫族化物（如WSe₂）中载流子在Γ谷与K谷之间散射动力学的重要参数，以往仅能通过超快光学技术（ultrafast optical techniques）测量，缺乏便捷的电学测量手段。本研究旨在建立一种纯电学方法，利用场效应晶体管的跨导直接谱学测量τ_iv。

Method: 扩展平衡谷热力学框架（equilibrium valley-thermodynamics framework），引入Γ谷载流子分数f_Γ(t)的单一弛豫方程（single relaxation equation），推导出跨导g_m(ω)的频率依赖关系，并预测三种电学特征信号。

Result: 预测了三种可定量提取τ_iv的电学特征：(i) 洛伦兹型跨导g_m(ω)=g_{m,0}+g_{m,v}^0/(1+iωτ_iv)，虚部在ω_c=τ_iv^{-1}处出现峰值，且双层与三层具有相反符号；(ii) 栅阶跃后的两阶段电流瞬态，双层呈现过冲（overshoot）而三层呈现欠冲（undershoot）；(iii) 与扫描速率成比例的磁滞回线，其栅压分布和层数依赖的符号反转可将谷动力学与陷阱诱导的动力学区分开。

Conclusion: 这三种电学特征均可通过标准射频（rf）和直流（dc）仪器实现对τ_iv的定量电学测量，为谷间弛豫时间提供了一种便捷的全电学谱学方案。

Abstract: We show that the transconductance of multilayer WSe$_2$ field-effect transistors serves as a direct electrical spectrometer of the intervalley relaxation time $τ_{\rm iv}$, previously accessible only by ultrafast optical techniques. Extending an equilibrium valley-thermodynamics framework with a single relaxation equation for the $Γ$-valley carrier fraction $f_Γ(t)$, we predict three signatures: (i)~a Lorentzian transconductance $g_m(ω)=g_{m,0}+g_{m,v}^0/(1+iωτ_{\rm iv})$, whose imaginary part peaks at $ω_c=τ_{\rm iv}^{-1}$ with opposite signs for bilayer and trilayer; (ii)~a two-stage current transient after a gate step, exhibiting bilayer overshoot or trilayer undershoot; and (iii)~sweep-rate-proportional hysteresis whose gate-voltage profile and layer-number sign reversal distinguish valley from trap-induced dynamics. All three signatures provide quantitative electrical access to $τ_{\rm iv}$ with standard rf and dc instrumentation.

</details>

In this work, we show that strain significantly alters the geometry of moiré superlattices by breaking the C3 rotational symmetry. Furthermore, interlayer exciton diffusion was preferentially guided along the stretched moiré superlattice orientations over a wide spatial range, reflecting the strain-modified moiré potentials. ### [95] [Spin polarisation signatures of Fractionally Charged Skyrmions in Fractional Quantum Hall states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10754)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用腔-极化子光谱学（cavity-polariton spectroscopy）技术，测量高迁移率GaAs量子阱中填充因子 $1/3 \le \nu \le 1$ 范围内带间朗道能级激发的光学耦合强度，进而提取电子系统的自旋极化（spin polarisation）随填充因子的变化关系。

Result: 首次在该体系中报告了完全极化系统中最低能量激发的振子强度完全抑制现象，这是单重态三子（singlet trion）形成的特征；在强磁场下，完全极化的FQH态在偏离量子化填充因子时表现出对称去极化行为，类似于 $ν=1$ 附近斯格明子（Skyrmion）的行为，且去极化服从经验规律 $S=ν^*$。

Conclusion: 所观测到的去极化行为可作为最小分数电荷斯格明子（Minimal Fractionally Charged Skyrmions, MFCS）存在的证据，该类激发由束缚的自旋翻转（spin-flip）和准粒子（quasiparticle）激发构成。

Abstract: We investigate spin polarisation and low-energy excitations in fractional quantum Hall (FQH) states using cavity-polariton spectroscopy of high-mobility GaAs quantum wells. By measuring the optical coupling strength of interband Landau-level excitations over the range $1/3 \le ν\le 1$, we extract the spin polarisation of the electron system as a function of filling factor.
  Complete suppression of the oscillator strength of the lowest energy excitation, characteristic of singlet trion formation in fully polarised systems, is reported for the first time in this regime.

The depolarisation follows an empirical law $S=ν^*$, where $S$ is the number of spin flips per added magnetic flux quantum and $ν^*$ the effective Composite Fermion filling factor. We interpret this behaviour as evidence for Minimal Fractionally Charged Skyrmions (MFCS) formed from bound spin-flip and quasiparticle excitations.

### [96] [Interplay between Aharonov-Bohm and Altshuler-Aronov-Spivak oscillations in phase-pure GaAs/InAs core/shell nanowires of different lengths](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10788)
*Farah Basarić,Kaiwen Wang,Tudor-Gabriel Dumitru,Andrei Manolescu,Francisco Alvarado Cesar,Ana M. Sanchez,Christoph Krause,Detlev Grützmacher,Alexander Pawlis,Thomas Schäpers*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过实验与紧束缚（tight-binding）模拟，系统研究了GaAs/InAs核壳纳米线中随接触间距和栅压变化的Aharonov–Bohm型与Altshuler–Aronov–Spivak型磁通周期振荡，揭示了平均效应对不同谐波振幅和相位刚性（phase rigidity）的影响，并指出准弹道输运（quasi-ballistic transport）的存在。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Aharonov–Bohm（AB）型和Altshuler–Aronov–Spivak（AAS）型电导振荡在超导量子器件中具有重要应用前景，但二者在相位刚性（phase rigidity）上本质不同，且其出现受平均效应（averaging effects）强烈影响。目前尚缺乏针对样品尺寸和输运区间如何调控这些振荡的系统研究。

Method: 对纯闪锌矿结构（zinc-blende）GaAs/InAs核壳纳米线进行不同接触间距样品的栅压（gate voltage）依赖测量，同时开展仅含少数散射中心的紧束缚（tight-binding）输运模拟，对比不同长度纳米线的谐波行为。

Result: 随着接触间距增大，平均效应导致h/e周期的AB型振荡逐渐减弱，而h/2e周期的AAS振荡及其h/4e高次谐波得到增强。观测到h/3e周期振荡及其相位刚性，归因于相邻低次谐波的相位刚性传播。模拟结果与实验在多谐波及其相位刚性上一致。

Conclusion: 实验与模拟共同表明，尽管存在少量散射中心，纳米线中仍存在准弹道输运（quasi-ballistic transport），并伴随持久的AB型振荡和相位刚性的AAS型振荡。

Abstract: In GaAs/InAs core/shell nanowires, comprising a tubular conducting shell, interference phenomena observed under an axial field and originating from closed-loop states encircling the insulating core, provide an ideal platform for superconducting quantum devices that utilize effects such as Aharonov--Bohm or Altshuler--Aronov--Spivak-type conductance oscillations. Both effects are different in nature with respect to phase rigidity because of interference of non-time-reversed or time-reversed paths, respectively. Since their occurrence is largely governed by averaging effects, which depend on sample dimensions and the transport regime, we present a systematic study of flux-periodic oscillations of phase-pure zinc-blende GaAs/InAs core/shell nanowires as a function of gate voltage for samples with different contact separation lengths. Our analysis shows that with increasing contact separation length, averaging effects result in gradual reduction of $h/e$-periodic Aharonov--Bohm-type oscillations, while the $h/2e$-periodic Altshuler--Aronov--Spivak oscillations and its $h/4e$-periodic higher harmonics are enhanced. The additional phase rigidity seen in the $h/3e$-periodic oscillations is attributed to phase rigidity propagating from the neighbouring lower harmonics. Our tight-binding transport simulations on nanowires of different lengths which contain only a few scattering centers confirm the experimental observations regarding the different harmonics and their phase rigidity. Together, our experimental and simulation findings indicate quasi-ballistic transport with persistent Aharonov--Bohm-, and phase-rigid Altshuler--Aronov--Spivak-type oscillations despite few scattering centers.

### [97] [Magnetism and Topology from Circularly Polarized Phonon Floquet Engineering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10854)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索圆极化声子作为一种有效磁场（effective magnetic field）来工程化调控材料中的磁性和拓扑性质，为声子Floquet方法提供新的可能性。

Method: 采用理论分析，在蜂窝状晶格上考虑圆极化声子对电子态的调制，通过声子Floquet工程构建有效电子模型，分析其诱导的次近邻跳跃、Haldane质量项以及时间反演对称性破缺效应。

Result: 圆极化声子打破了时间反演对称性，在谷点处打开能隙，驱动系统从平凡绝缘体到陈绝缘体的拓扑相变；同时，由于TRS破缺，系统产生了轨道磁化和自旋磁化。

Conclusion: 圆极化声子可作为有效磁场用于工程化调控材料的磁性和拓扑性质，为声子Floquet方法在量子材料研究中的应用开辟了新途径。

Abstract: We theoretically show that circularly polarized phonons induce electronic magnetization and drive a topological phase transition via phonon Floquet engineering. Considering the electronic states modulated by circularly polarized phonons on a honeycomb lattice, we show that such lattice dynamics generates an effective next-nearest-neighbor electron hopping, leading to a Haldane-type mass term. Circularly polarized phonon breaks time-reversal symmetry (TRS) and opens a gap at valley points, undergoing phase transition from a trivial insulator to a Chern insulator. Moreover, the orbital and spin magnetizations emerge due to the breaking of TRS. Our results show that circularly polarized phonons serve as an effective magnetic field to engineer magnetism and topology, offering new opportunities for phonon Floquet approaches.

### [98] [Optical fingerprints across the strain-driven semi-Dirac transition in Kekulé-O graphene](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10996)
*Yawar Mohammadi*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文研究了Kekulé-O石墨烯中应变驱动的半狄拉克相变（semi-Dirac transition）所产生的各向异性光学指纹（optical fingerprints），揭示了伴随能带重构的光谱权重转移和光学各向异性增强，并识别了三种低能指纹特征：有隙吸收峰（gapped absorption peaks）、半狄拉克临界标度（semi-Dirac critical scaling）和范霍夫光学共振（van Hove optical resonance）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索Kekulé-O石墨烯在应变驱动下半狄拉克相变过程中的光学响应行为，揭示能带重构如何影响低能光学特性，并为实验观测提供可识别的光学指纹。

Method: 采用数值四带计算（numerical four-band calculations）与解析低能结果相结合的方法，分析了随应变增加而涌现的三类低能光学指纹，并考虑了中等无序展宽（moderate disorder broadening）和有限温度效应（finite-temperature effects）的影响。

Result: 在半狄拉克临界点，Kekulé能隙在Γ点闭合，低能光电导表现为σ_xx(Ω)∝Ω^{1/2}和σ_yy(Ω)∝Ω^{-1/2}的各向异性标度行为；相变后半狄拉克点分裂为两个各向异性狄拉克锥（anisotropic Dirac cones），并在Γ点附近出现鞍点（saddle points），引发远低于石墨烯能量的显著范霍夫光学共振。

Conclusion: 应变驱动的能带重构通过主导光学跃迁通道的连续演化产生上述低能光学指纹，且这些指纹在中等无序和有限温度下仍保持可识别性，表明在实验现实条件下具有潜在的可观测性。

Abstract: We show that the strain-driven semi-Dirac transition in Kekulé-O graphene gives rise to a sequence of anisotropic optical fingerprints associated with band structure reconstruction. Across the transition, optical spectral weight is continuously redistributed among the dominant interband transitions, leading to a pronounced enhancement of the optical anisotropy. Combining numerical four-band calculations with analytical low-energy results, we identify three low-energy fingerprints that emerge with increasing strain: gapped absorption peaks, semi-Dirac critical scaling, and a pronounced van Hove optical resonance. At the semi-Dirac critical point, where the Kekulé gap closes at the $Γ$ point, the low-energy optical conductivity is characterized by $σ_{xx}(Ω)\proptoΩ^{1/2}$ and $σ_{yy}(Ω)\proptoΩ^{-1/2}$. Beyond the transition, the semi-Dirac point splits into two anisotropic Dirac cones, accompanied by the emergence of saddle points near the $Γ$ point. The resulting saddle-point excitations produce a pronounced van Hove optical resonance at energies well below those of graphene, while the split Dirac cones give rise to an anisotropic constant optical conductivity. We further show that the low-energy optical fingerprints can be traced to the continuous evolution of a dominant optical transition channel driven by strain-induced band reconstruction. Moreover, the fingerprints remain identifiable in the presence of moderate disorder broadening and finite-temperature effects, indicating their potential observability under experimentally realistic conditions.

### [99] [Interplay between photon condensation and electron-electron interactions in molecular systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11060)
*Matteo Parisi,Elisabetta Paladino,Giuseppe A. Falci,Gian Marcello Andolina,Salvatore Savasta,Marco Polini,Francesco M. D. Pellegrino*

TL;DR: 本文研究了一个由方形平面板块（square planar plaquettes）和多个电子组成的极小分子模型，通过将系统耦合到空间非均匀的腔模（cavity mode），分析了源自顺磁范弗莱克机制（paramagnetic Van Vleck mechanism）的光子凝聚（photon condensation）这一静磁不稳定性。研究发现，除半填充（half-filling）和单电子特殊情况外，由于电子-电子相互作用，系统可能经历从二级相变到一级相变的转变，并给出了对应的极化激元（polaritonic）激发能谱特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在分子尺度模型中，通过空间非均匀腔模耦合诱导的静磁不稳定性（即光子凝聚）的物理机制，并系统分析电子填充因子（filling factor）对相变行为的影响。

Method: 采用紧束缚哈密顿量（tight-binding Hamiltonian）加上局域哈伯德排斥项（on-site Hubbard repulsion）描述电子动力学；将系统耦合到空间非均匀的腔模，利用顺磁范弗莱克机制分析光子凝聚的起源；对不同电子填充因子下的全局行为进行计算分析。

Result: 半填充和单电子情况下，若发生相变则必为二级相变（second order phase transition）；而在其他填充因子下，由于电子-电子相互作用（electron-electron interaction）的影响，系统可能发生一级相变（first order transition）。极化激元激发能（polaritonic excitation energies）的分析提供了该静磁不稳定性及其相变阶数的清晰光谱特征。

Conclusion: 该极小分子模型在腔量子电动力学（cavity quantum electrodynamics）框架下能够展现丰富的光子凝聚相变现象，且相变阶数受电子填充和相互作用调控，对应的极化激元光谱可作为实验探测的明确指征。

Abstract: We investigate a minimal molecular model consisting of square planar plaquettes hosting multiple electrons, whose dynamics is governed by a tight-binding Hamiltonian supplemented by on-site Hubbard repulsion. By coupling this system to a spatially nonuniform cavity mode, we analyze the emergence of a magnetostatic instability, namely photon condensation, originating from the paramagnetic Van Vleck mechanism. The global behavior of the system is analyzed for different electronic filling factors, and we find that, except for the special cases of half-filling and single electron, where the transition, if it occurs, is necessarily a second order phase transition, the global system may also undergo a first order transition because of the action of the electron-electron interaction. The polaritonic excitation energies are analyzed, providing clear spectroscopic signatures of the magnetostatic instability and of its order.

### [100] [Quantum statistics in an extended collider coupled to a qubit](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11147)
*Rishav Chaudhuri,Sai Satyam Samal*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文研究了在介观对撞机（mesoscopic collider）中，将点状对撞器扩展为扩展对撞器（extended collider）后，对费米子和玻色子波包散射的统计分析。通过后选择（post-selection）杂质态，系统分析了用于表征聚束效应（bunching）和推断互统计（mutual statistics）的基准指标，发现只有特定基准能准确反映粒子的互统计，其他选择可能产生虚假的统计信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 介观对撞机是探测量子粒子互统计的有效平台，实验已成功提取费米子（fermions）及任意子（anyons）的互统计。然而，现有研究多集中于点状对撞器（如量子点接触，quantum point contact），将其耦合至二能级杂质（two-level impurity）或量子比特（qubit）可诱导费米子的统计嬗变（statistical transmutation），使其表现出类似玻色子的聚束倾向。作者旨在将对撞器扩展至扩展情形，系统评估不同基准指标在表征聚束和推断互统计时的有效性。

Method: 作者研究了费米子和玻色子波包在扩展对撞器中的散射过程，并在对杂质态进行后选择的条件下进行分析。他们系统比较了多种用于表征聚束效应的基准指标（benchmarks），考察各指标能否忠实反映碰撞粒子间潜在的互统计。

Result: 只有一种特定的基准指标能够真实反映碰撞粒子的互统计，而其他可选的基准指标可能产生虚假的统计信号（spurious statistical signatures）。

Conclusion: 用于探测量子统计的正确基准依赖于介观对撞器的精细细节（intricate details），因此在实际实验中需要谨慎选择基准指标，以避免对互统计的误判。

Abstract: Mesoscopic colliders provide an effective platform for probing the mutual statistics of quantum particles. Recent experiments have successfully extracted the mutual statistics of fermions, and more exotic anyons using quantum point contacts (QPCs). Coupling a point-like collider, such as a quantum point contact, to a two-level impurity or qubit can induce statistical transmutation of fermions, causing them to display boson-like bunching tendencies. Here, we extend the analysis to an extended collider. We investigate the scattering of two incoming fermionic and bosonic wave packets in the presence of post-selection on the impurity state, and systematically analyze the possible benchmarks used to characterize bunching and infer the underlying mutual statistics. We show that only a specific benchmark faithfully captures the mutual statistics of the colliding particles, while alternative choices can produce spurious statistical signatures. Hence, the correct benchmark for probing the quantum statistics depends on the intricate details of the mesoscopic collider.

</details>

### [101] [Exceptional Points as Manifestations of Analyticity Breakdown in the 't Hooft Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10141)
*Kejun Liu*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文利用1+1维大N_c QCD的t Hooft模型，通过PT对称变形驱动介子两點函數在例外点（exceptional point）发生解析性破缺，首次在禁闭规范理论中实现了例外点解析性破缺的精确解析控制与可观测时间域签名。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在量子场论与统计力学（statistical mechanics）中，因果响应函数的解析性（analyticity）破缺是基础但难以严格研究的问题。本文旨在利用精确可解的t Hooft模型，提供一个严格的实验室来研究这一现象，特别是在禁闭规范理论（confining gauge theory）中。

Method: 在1+1维大N_c QCD的t Hooft模型中，对光锥介子算符施加PT对称形变（PT-symmetric deformation） i γ (x-1/2)，这等价于引入虚化学势（imaginary chemical potential）。将预解式（resolvent）重新表示为雅可比连分数（Jacobi continued fraction），从而以闭合形式给出例外点（exceptional point, EP）阈值γ_c。通过2×2 Jordan标准型确定平方根指数ν=1/2，并用N=1999的有限尺寸标度（finite-size scaling）加以确认。

Result: 在双极点近似下，例外点阈值γ_c = 2π g² N_c，到深度五时收敛至7.966 g² N_c，这是一个解析而非数值的阈值。时间域传播子模（propagator norm）在γ < γ_c时有界，在γ_c时线性增长（Jordan secular law），在γ > γ_c时指数增长。阈值与禁闭（confinement）锁定，γ_c ∝ g² N_c，并呈现均匀的例外点级联（EP cascade）。另一非互易变形（non-reciprocal deformation）产生精确指数的非厄米趋肤效应（non-Hermitian skin effect）。

Conclusion: 这是首次在禁闭规范理论中实现例外点解析性破缺的精确解析控制实例。其时间域签名在光量子与拓扑电路类比中可观测，为研究非厄米量子场论中的解析性破缺提供了严格的范例。

Abstract: We use the exactly-solvable t Hooft model of 1+1D large-N_c QCD as a rigorous laboratory for the breakdown of analyticity of a causal response function, the meson two-point function. A PT-symmetric deformation i gamma(x-1/2) of the light-cone meson operator, the analogue of an imaginary chemical potential, drives the lowest two mesons to an exceptional point (EP) at gamma_c. Recasting the resolvent as a Jacobi continued fraction yields gamma_c in closed form: 2 pi g^2 N_c at the two-pole level, converging to 7.966 g^2 N_c by depth five -- an analytic, not numerical, threshold. The square-root exponent nu=1/2 is fixed by the 2x2 Jordan form and confirmed by finite-size scaling to N=1999. The breakdown has an unambiguous time-domain signature: the propagator norm is bounded for gamma < gamma_c, grows linearly at gamma_c (the Jordan secular law), and exponentially beyond -- observable, since the deformed operator is a non-Hermitian Wannier-Stark ladder, in photonic and topolectrical analogues. The threshold is locked to confinement, gamma_c propto g^2 N_c, and recurs as a uniform EP cascade; a second, non-reciprocal deformation yields an exactly-exponential non-Hermitian skin effect. This is the first analytically-controlled instance of exceptional-point analyticity breakdown in a confining gauge theory.

</details>


### [102] [Contact Tulczyjew Geometry for Continuous and Discrete Dissipative Dynamics on Skew Algebroids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10515)
*Leonardo Colombo,Manuel de León*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文在斜代数胚（skew algebroid）上建立了接触Tulczyjew形式体系，用于描述耗散动力学（dissipative dynamics），并给出了其连续与离散两种版本。连续版本通过引入Euler向量场（Euler vector field）贡献得到接触Tulczyjew态射（contact Tulczyjew morphism），从而导出Euler-Lagrange-Herglotz方程（Euler-Lagrange-Herglotz equations）与接触Hamilton方程（contact Hamiltonian equations）；离散版本通过接触Tulczyjew关系（contact Tulczyjew relation）与匹配条件恢复离散Herglotz极值（discrete Herglotz extremals），并在正则切丛情形还原为标准接触变分积分器（contact variational integrators）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将Tulczyjew形式体系（Tulczyjew formalism）从辛几何（symplectic geometry）推广到接触几何（contact geometry），以在斜代数胚的广义框架下统一描述耗散动力学，并填补该领域连续与离散理论之间的空白。

Method: 从斜代数胚的Tulczyjew态射出发，通过局部线丛平凡化（local line-bundle trivialization）构造其接触扩展，即在普通Tulczyjew态射基础上增加E^*上的Euler向量场贡献。离散版本则基于离散容许关系（discrete admissibility relation）定义离散接触Tulczyjew关系，并通过匹配连续接触动量来得到离散Herglotz极值。

Result: 连续构造给出了接触生成对象（contact generating object）隐含的耗散动力学，局部坐标下的匹配条件导出斜代数胚上的Euler-Lagrange-Herglotz方程；超正则情形下通过Legendre变换（Legendre transformation）得到接触Hamilton方程。离散构造在正则切丛情形恢复标准接触变分积分器，在奇异或斜代数胚情形则作为隐式离散关系（implicit discrete relation）而非先验更新映射（a priori update map）保持有意义。

Conclusion: 所提出的接触Tulczyjew形式体系为斜代数胚上的耗散系统提供了一种内在几何框架，其离散版本在广义设置下具有比传统变分积分器更广的适用性，尤其适用于奇异约束或非标准切丛结构的情形。

Abstract: We develop a contact Tulczyjew formalism for dissipative dynamics on skew algebroids. Starting from the Tulczyjew morphism of an skew algebroid, we identify its contact extension in a local line-bundle trivialization. The local representative is obtained by adding to the ordinary Tulczyjew morphism the Euler vector field contribution on $E^*$. This gives an intrinsic explanation of the contact term appearing in the local contact Tulczyjew morphism.
  For a contact generating object, the construction produces an implicit dissipative dynamics on the contact phase side. In local coordinates, the matching condition gives the Euler-Lagrange-Herglotz equations on the skew algebroid. In the hyperregular case, the corresponding contact Hamiltonian equations are recovered by Legendre transformation.
  We also develop the discrete counterpart of the construction. After fixing a discrete admissibility relation, a discrete contact generating object defines a discrete contact Tulczyjew relation on the contact phase space. Discrete Herglotz extremals are obtained by matching consecutive contact momenta, with the usual conormal interpretation in the constrained case. In the regular tangent-bundle case, this recovers standard contact variational integrators, while in the singular or skew algebroid setting the same construction remains meaningful as an implicit discrete relation rather than an a priori update map.

</details>


### [103] [Weighted least action principle for Maxwell equations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10745)
*Jacob Rubinstein,Gershon Wolansky*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文针对传统费马最小时间原理仅适用于单条光线（非可测物理对象）的局限，提出了基于两个平面上波强度测量的升级变分原理，用于任意介质中麦克斯韦方程几何光学极限下的完整菲涅尔光线束（Fresnel rays bundle）描述，并利用菲涅尔光线与相位法线（phase normals）的互易性，实现通过两次强度测量确定电磁波相位。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统费马最小时间原理（Fermat principle of least time）仅能确定单条光线的路径，但单条光线并非可测量的物理对象，因此需要一种基于可测量量（波强度）的升级变分原理。

Method: 基于在两个平面上测量波强度，推导了适用于任意介质中麦克斯韦方程（Maxwell equations）几何光学极限（geometric optics limit）的升级变分原理，该原理提供了连接两个平面上关联点的完整菲涅尔光线束。

Result: 该理论的一个应用是利用菲涅尔光线与相位法线之间的互易性（reciprocity），通过两次强度测量确定电磁波的相位。

Conclusion: 所提出的变分原理将费马原理从不可测的单条光线推广到可测量的波强度层面，为从强度测量反演相位提供了新的理论框架。

Abstract: The Fermat principle of least time determines the path of a single ray of light given its initial and final positions and the medium electromagnetic properties. However, a single ray is not a measurable physical object. We derive here an upgraded variational principle for the geometric optics limit of Maxwell equations in an arbitrary medium, based on measuring the intensity of the wave on two planes. The principle provides the complete Fresnel rays bundle connecting associated points at the first and second planes. One of the applications of the present theory is to use the reciprocity between Fresnel rays and phase normals to determine the phase of an electromagnetic wave from two intensity measurements.

</details>


### [104] [Nonlinear Anisotropic Visco-Anelasticity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10801)
*Souhayl Sadik,Arash Yavari*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一套统一的非线性几何理论框架，将粘弹性（viscoelastic）与滞弹性（anelastic）响应整合到同一热力学体系中。通过将变形梯度乘法分解为弹性、粘性和滞弹性三部分，推广了Bilby-Kröner-Lee分解，并利用材料度量（material metric）、结构张量（structural tensors）等几何工具系统构建了本构方程、平衡律、热力学势和动力学方程。该框架统一了非线性粘弹性与滞弹性，澄清了现有理论中中间构型（intermediate configuration）的几何混淆。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有非线性粘弹性与粘塑性理论在中间构型的定义和分解方式上存在歧义，缺乏一个能统一描述时间相关（time-dependent）响应与特征应变驱动（eigenstrain-driven）效应的几何框架。本文旨在通过引入材料度量与结构张量的几何语言，消除这些模糊性，建立一个自洽的粘滞弹性几何理论。

Method: 将变形梯度（deformation gradient）乘法分解为弹性（elastic）、粘性（viscous）与滞弹性（anelastic）三部分，推广了经典的Bilby-Kröner-Lee分解。引入材料度量（material metric）刻画固体演化中的自然构型（natural configuration），利用变换后的结构张量（transformed structural tensors）处理各向异性。系统应用热力学第一和第二定律推导本构方程和演化方程，无需依赖观察者不变性（observer invariance）假设。

Result: 将通用框架特例化为各向同性（isotropic）和横观各向同性（transversely isotropic）粘滞弹性固体。通过两类普适变形（universal deformations）示例，展示了该框架如何建模具有分布特征应变（distributed eigenstrains）及相关残余应力（residual stresses）的不可压缩各向异性固体的耦合粘性与滞弹性响应。

Conclusion: 该几何框架通过将时间相关效应与特征应变驱动效应耦合在一个完全自洽的几何表述中，统一了非线性粘弹性与滞弹性。明确揭示了弹、粘、滞弹性变形的几何结构，解决了现有非线性粘弹性和粘塑性理论中关于中间构型的歧义问题。

Abstract: We formulate a nonlinear geometric theory of visco-anelasticity that unifies viscoelastic and anelastic responses within a single thermodynamic framework. At each material point, the total deformation gradient is multiplicatively decomposed into elastic, viscous, and anelastic distortions, thereby generalizing the Bilby-Kröner-Lee decomposition to visco-anelasticity. The theory explicitly incorporates the material metric, which encodes the evolving natural configuration of the solid, the transformed structural tensors, and provides a consistent formulation of the constitutive equations, the balance laws, the thermodynamic potentials, and the kinetic equations. The first and second laws of thermodynamics are systematically applied to derive the constitutive and evolution equations without invoking observer invariance. Anisotropy is treated in full generality through structural tensors. As illustrative examples, we specialize the general framework to isotropic and transversely isotropic visco-anelastic solids. Two examples within the class of universal deformations, which admit closed or partially closed form solutions, show how the proposed framework can be used to model the coupled viscous and anelastic response of incompressible anisotropic solids with distributed eigenstrains and the associated residual stresses. This geometric framework unifies nonlinear viscoelasticity and anelasticity by coupling time-dependent and eigenstrain-driven effects within a single, fully consistent geometric formulation. In particular, the proposed framework clarifies the geometric structure of the elastic, viscous, and anelastic distortions and resolves ambiguities associated with intermediate configurations in existing formulations of nonlinear viscoelasticity and viscoplasticity.

</details>


### [105] [The Yang-Baxter Equation for the Chiral Potts Model and Integrable Parafermions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11146)
*Zhao Zhang*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该论文基于手性波茨模型（chiral Potts model）的星-三角关系（star-triangle relation）与星-星关系（star-star relation），构造了一类新型的三谱参量（three spectral parameters）杨-巴克斯特方程（Yang-Baxter equation, YBE），并揭示了其与可解边模型（edge model）与顶点模型（vertex model）统一框架之间的联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了将可解边模型与顶点模型进一步统一，作者试图构造一类新的、参数化于三个谱参数（spectral parameters）的杨-巴克斯特方程，从而更深入地理解奥恩萨格（Onsager）星-三角关系在YBE框架中的本质角色。

Method: 从手性波茨模型的星-三角关系与星-星关系出发，推导出适用于R-矩阵的新型三谱参量杨-巴克斯特方程。该构造利用了边模型（如伊辛模型）的量子哈密顿量同时包含最近邻相互作用项与在位势项这一特性，由此自然引入了R-算符中的额外谱参数。

Result: 成功构造了一类由三个谱参数参数化的新YBE，其R-矩阵来源于手性波茨模型的玻尔兹曼权重（Boltzmann weights）。该结果将近期关于可解边模型与顶点模型的统一工作向前推进，并将奥恩萨格的星-三角关系从YBE的简单替代形式提升为其基础构成要素。

Conclusion: 该构造统一了边模型与顶点模型的可解结构，表明三谱参量YBE是手性波茨模型对称性（Z_N对称性）与曲线亏格（genus）大于一的几何结构在代数层面的自然表达。

Abstract: A new type of Yang-Baxter equation (YBE) for $R$-matrices parameterized by three spectral parameters is constructed from the star-triangle and star-star relations for the chiral Potts model. As the $Z_N$ symmetric generalization to the Ising model, its Boltzmann weights are known to depend on two variables describing a curve with genus larger than one for $N>2$, except for the self-dual point corresponding to the Fateev-Zamolodchikov chain. This combined with the fact that the quantum Hamiltonians of edge models like Ising contain both nearest neighbor interaction and onsite potential terms results in the extra spectral parameter of the $R$-operator. My construction extends the recent unification of solvable edge and vertex models which recasts Onsager's star-triangle relation from a mere alternative form of the YBE for edge models to its underlying ingredient.

</details>

### [106] [Noncommutative NLS systems: Darboux--Bäcklund transformations and integrable discretisations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10037)
*Sotiris Konstantinou-Rizos*

Main category: nlin.SI

TL;DR: 本文研究了与约化群相关联的非线性薛定谔（NLS）型系统的非交换类比和可积离散化，包括AKNS系统、Kaup–Newell导数NLS系统及其Mikhailov–Shabat–Yamilov形变，构造了非交换变形并导出了相应的Darboux–Bäcklund变换和晶格方程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索非线性薛定谔（NLS）型系统在非交换框架和可积离散化下的推广，特别是针对与约化群（reduction groups）相关联的AKNS、Kaup–Newell导数NLS及其Mikhailov–Shabat–Yamilov形变系统，以揭示其结构性质与解的性质。

Method: 通过取先前构造的可积晶格系统的连续极限（continuum limits）恢复相应的NLS型偏微分方程；构造Mikhailov–Shabat–Yamilov系统的非交换形变，并分析其Lax表示（Lax representation）是否需要引入非局域变量（nonlocal variables）；导出非交换导数NLS及其形变系统的Darboux–Bäcklund变换和以顶点–键晶格方程（vertex–bond lattice equations）形式呈现的可积离散化。

Result: 在AKNS和Kaup–Newell情形中，非交换变形不引入非局域变量，而Mikhailov–Shabat–Yamilov系统的非交换形变则需要非局域变量；成功构造了非交换导数NLS及其形变系统的可积离散化；为六点导数NLS型晶格方程及其非交换类比构造了显式解。

Conclusion: 非交换性和可积离散化在NLS型系统中的推广呈现出不同的结构特征，尤其是在Lax表示中是否引入非局域变量方面因系统而异；所构造的显式解和晶格方程为进一步研究非交换可积系统提供了基础。

Abstract: We study noncommutative analogues and integrable discretisations of nonlinear Schrödinger (NLS)-type systems associated with reduction groups. In particular, we consider the Ablowitz--Kaup--Newell--Segur (AKNS) system, the Kaup--Newell derivative NLS system, and the Mikhailov--Shabat--Yamilov deformation of the derivative NLS system together with their Darboux--Bäcklund transformations and associated lattice equations.
  We derive the continuum limits of previously constructed integrable lattice systems and recover the corresponding NLS-type partial differential equations. We then construct a noncommutative deformation of the Mikhailov--Shabat--Yamilov system and show that, unlike the AKNS and Kaup--Newell cases, its Lax representation requires the introduction of nonlocal variables.
  Furthermore, we derive Darboux--Bäcklund transformations and integrable discretisations for the noncommutative derivative NLS and deformation derivative NLS systems in the form of vertex--bond lattice equations. We also construct explicit solutions for a six-point derivative NLS-type lattice equation and for its noncommutative analogue.

</details>

### [107] [A Recrossing-Free Dividing Surface in Quantum Mechanics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10266)
*Pouya Khazaei*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明，在量子力学中构造无反复穿越的划分面（recrossing-free dividing surface）并非不可能，通过量子流（quantum flow）中稳定与不稳定不变流形（invariant manifolds）的交线，可以定义一个唯一有界轨迹，从而构建移动划分面（moving dividing surface），使反应性量子特征（reactive quantum characteristics）恰好穿越一次，实现标准量子概率流（quantum probability current）的单向通量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近一个世纪以来，量子力学中一直被认为不可能存在无反复穿越的划分面，因为单向反应通量（one-way reactive flux）似乎需要同时知道轨迹层面的位置与动量，这与不确定性原理（uncertainty principle）存在明显冲突。本文旨在证明这一障碍并非根本性的。

Method: 通过分析精确量子流（exact quantum flow），证明该流可容纳稳定与不稳定不变流形，二者的交线定义了一条唯一有界轨迹，该轨迹锚定了一个移动划分面。

Result: 该移动划分面使反应性量子特征恰好穿越一次，产生标准量子概率流的单向通量。

Conclusion: 经典反应动力学（classical reaction dynamics）背后的几何框架可以以根本性的量子形式推广到精确量子流中。

Abstract: For nearly a century, a recrossing-free dividing surface in quantum mechanics has been thought impossible. One-way reactive flux seems to require simultaneous trajectory-level knowledge of position and momentum -- an apparent conflict with the uncertainty principle. We show that this obstruction is not fundamental. The exact quantum flow can admit stable and unstable invariant manifolds whose intersection defines a unique bounded trajectory. This trajectory anchors a moving dividing surface that reactive quantum characteristics cross exactly once, producing a one-way flux of the standard quantum probability current. The geometric framework underlying classical reaction dynamics therefore carries over to the exact quantum flow, in a fundamentally quantum form.

</details>


### [108] [Towards the implementation of a quantum classifier](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10150)
*Lorenzo Confalonieri,Adrián Pérez Salinas,Stefano Carrazza*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究使用量子电路作为二元分类模型（binary quantum classifier），基于Qibo开源框架实现图像与高能碰撞事件数据的分类，并与经典小卷积神经网络进行性能对比。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索量子电路在量子机器学习（quantum machine learning）中作为二元分类模型的可行性，并评估其相对于经典方法的性能与局限性。

Method: 基于量子电路设计二元量子分类器，使用Qibo开源框架进行量子模拟；定义电路模型Ansatz（含可训练参数）与损失函数，实现多种最小化器（minimizer）；在MNIST手写数字数据集（归约为0和1）以及LHC（CERN）的高能碰撞图像（32×32）与六维特征变量数据集上进行实验，并处理有/无堆叠效应（pile-up）场景。

Result: 通过增加Ansatz层数与训练集规模，对比不同最小化器的表现；计算ROC曲线、AUC分数、混淆矩阵（confusion matrix）和测试集准确率（test set accuracy）；针对含堆叠效应的图像数据，将量子分类器结果与小卷积神经网络（small convolutional neural network）进行对比。

Conclusion: 能够基于量子电路构建二元量子分类器，但其性能与局限性需在与经典技术的比较中加以评估。

Abstract: In this work, we investigate the use of a quantum circuit as a binary classification model in the context of quantum machine learning. We call this model, binary quantum classifier.
  First, we describe fundamental concepts of quantum computing and introduce the computational tool used: Qibo, an open-source framework for efficient quantum simulations and quantum hardware control. Then, we describe how to design a binary quantum classifier for the classification of images and small arrays of variables by showing how to input data in the circuit, defining a quantum circuit model Ansatz with trainable parameters and a loss function, and implementing multiple minimizers. We test our quantum classifier with two data sets. The first one is the MNIST data set which is composed of handwritten digits (reduced to only handwritten zeros and handwritten ones for binary classification). We study the behavior of different minimizers by increasing the number of layers of the Ansatz. The second data set represents two different high energy collisions that can occur at colliders such as LHC (CERN). Due to in-time proton-proton interactions known as pile-up, we distinguish two different data sets: "without pile-up" and "with pile-up". These collisions can be represented by images of size 32x32 or by six high-level variables that we call features. By increasing the size of the training data set and the number of layers of the Ansatz, we search for the best minimizer. Splitting the data set in training set and test set, we compute: ROC curve, AUC score, confusion matrices and test set accuracy. For "with pile-up" images, we compare the results obtained with the quantum classifier with a small convolutional neural network.
  We conclude that is possible to build a binary quantum classifier with a quantum circuit and we highlight its performances and limitations in comparison with classical technologies.

</details>


### [109] [Revealing the topology of quantum states via Kirkwood-Dirac quasiprobabilities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11002)
*Stefano Gherardini,Luca Lepori*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于Kirkwood-Dirac准概率（KDQ）来区分多体量子系统拓扑态的理论方法，将奇异关联子（strange correlator）表示为KDQ的函数，并建立了奇异关联子与弱值（weak value）之间的联系，进而提出可通过瞬时淬火（sudden quench）实验实现的量子拓扑见证（quantum topology witness），同时讨论了基于干涉测量的拓扑区分协议及其实现挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多体量子系统中，如何判定两个量子态是否属于不同的拓扑（topology）类别是一个基础性问题。现有工具——奇异关联子（strange correlator）虽可用于拓扑区分，但其底层物理机制尚需进一步揭示。本文试图通过KDQ建立奇异关联子的第一性原理表示，从而为拓扑区分提供更清晰的理论基础和实验可行的方案。

Method: 本文的方法基于将奇异关联子表示为Kirkwood-Dirac准概率（Kirkwood-Dirac quasiprobability, KDQ）的函数。KDQ提供了两时量子关联子（two-time quantum correlator）的第一性原理表示。由此建立奇异关联子与弱值（weak value）之间的等价关系，即奇异关联子是将初始平庸态（trivial state）转化为非平庸拓扑态（topologically non-trivial state）的可观测量的弱值。在此基础上，提出一种可通过测量瞬时淬火（sudden quench）转变的前后效应来获取的量子拓扑见证（quantum topology witness），并进一步讨论了利用KDQ完全重构方案实现的干涉测量（interferometric）拓扑区分协议。

Result: 通过理论推导，本文建立了奇异关联子与KDQ之间的严格对应关系，并证明奇异关联子等价于一个特定的弱值。基于此提出了一个可在多体系统上通过瞬时淬火实验实现的量子拓扑见证。此外，给出了一个用于拓扑区分的干涉测量协议，并讨论了该协议实现的主要路线与面临的挑战。

Conclusion: 本文从理论上揭示了奇异关联子与Kirkwood-Dirac准概率及弱值之间的内在联系，为量子拓扑区分提供了一种新的理论视角。所提出的量子拓扑见证方案在实验上具有可行性，而基于干涉测量的协议则为未来实现拓扑态区分提供了潜在的技术路径。

Abstract: We discuss a theoretical approach to discriminate whether two states of a many-body quantum system belong or not to different topology classes. This approach is based on expressing a strange correlator - a recently established tool for quantum topology discrimination - between the states as a function of Kirkwood-Dirac quasiprobabilities (KDQs). KDQs provide a first-principles representation of two-time quantum correlators. The link between strange correlators and KDQs allows to establish that strange correlators are weak values of an observable converting an initial trivial state into a topologically non-trivial one. We thus propose a quantum topology witness that is achievable measuring the prior and subsequent effects on a many-body system of a sudden quench transformation that realizes the transition between trivial and topological phases. The witness is evaluated on a probe quantum state whose main features are detailed within the paper. Finally, directly exploiting schemes that allows for the complete reconstruction of KDQs, we address an interferometric protocol for topology discrimination, along with a general discussion of the main lines and challenges towards its implementation.

Method: 采用光机械系统（optomechanical system），以量子转子和光子为对象，通过引力子（graviton）的虚交换（virtual exchange）分析二者间的纠缠生成；将转子近似为高自旋经典角动量态，计算顺行与逆行运动光子的线性纠缠熵之差。

This paper explores the generation of entanglement due to the quantum gravitational interaction in an optomechanical setup with a quantum rotor and photon. The virtual exchange of a graviton provides entanglement between the photon degrees of freedom and the spatial position of the quantum rotor, with the rotational state affecting its magnitude. We analyze the case of a high spinning rotor, in an approximately classical state of angular momentum, and quantify its effect on the gravitationally induced entanglement between the photon and the position of the quantum rotor. ### [111] [Magic and entanglement in 1+1-dimensional SU(2) lattice gauge theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09971)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用规范不变的纠缠熵和稳定子Rényi熵作为度量，在满足高斯定律的dressed-site基下表述(1+1)维SU(2)格点规范理论；利用张量网络（tensor networks）对系统尺寸最大至L=100（300个量子比特）进行计算。

Result: 发现存在一个由 $g_{\star}$ 标记的交叉现象：基态从一个富含magic的区域过渡到一个magic较少的区域；该交叉同时伴随着纠缠熵和晶格粒子密度（lattice particle density）的最剧烈变化。

Conclusion: 在含有物质的非阿贝尔格点规范理论（non-Abelian lattice gauge theory）中对非稳定子资源性和纠缠熵的大规模研究，为理解规范理论中magic与纠缠的相互作用提供了新见解，这些性质对经典模拟和早期容错量子模拟均具有重要意义。

Abstract: Entanglement and non-stabilizerness (magic) quantify two distinct departures of quantum systems from classical description: the former measures non-local correlations, while the latter measures the deviation from stabilizer states that can be efficiently simulated classically. Understanding magic in physically relevant quantum field theories is essential for identifying where quantum advantage may be realized in the early fault-tolerant quantum computing era. We calculate the gauge-invariant entanglement entropy and stabilizer Rényi entropy of the ground state of the (1+1)-dimensional SU(2) lattice gauge theory formulated in a dressed-site basis that enforces Gauss's law exactly. Using tensor networks, we obtain results for system sizes up to $L=100$ (300 qubits). ### [112] [Wave packets from the spectrum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10004)
*ChunJun Cao,Oliver Friedrich,Marin Girard,Nicolas Loizeau,Ashmeet Singh*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文论证了在格子理论中，通过改变福克基（Fock basis）可以确保系统具备最小程度的局域性（locality）；具体而言，通过将高度非局域的随机矩阵模型转化为局域的1D晶格理论，并推广到任意哈密顿量，展示了该方法在量子分体学（quantum mereology）中的潜在应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在格子理论（lattice theories）中，动力学可能表现出高度非局域性（non-local dynamics）。作者试图证明，通过改变福克基（Fock basis），可以在不改变哈密顿量（Hamiltonian）谱的前提下，使动力学呈现出更局域的形式，从而确保系统具备最小程度的局域性。

Method: 从一个高度非局域的随机矩阵模型（random matrix model）出发，通过选择新的产生湮灭算符（creation and annihilation operators）集合，将其转化为一个局域的1D晶格理论，其中粒子能以局域化的波包（localized wave packets）传播。作者进一步证明，任意哈密顿量都可以通过类似操作被表示为这种局域格子理论的形式。

Result: 展示了非局域随机矩阵模型可以转化为局域1D晶格理论；证明了任意哈密顿量均可被重整为类似形式，且晶格色散关系（lattice dispersion relation）与理论的可积性（non-integrability）取决于原哈密顿量的谱（spectrum）。

Conclusion: 该工作为量子分体学（quantum mereology）在量子场论中的进一步研究提供了基础步骤；表明通过选择适当的福克基，可以在不改变物理内容的前提下揭示系统的局域结构。

Abstract: The freedom to change Fock basis seems to ensure a minimum amount of locality in lattice theories in the following sense: If $\lbrace (\hat a_i^\dagger\,,\,\hat a_i)\rbrace$ for $i=1,\dots,n$ is a lattice of creation and annihilation operators and if a given Hamiltonian $\hat H$ induces highly non-local dynamics on that lattice, then it will usually be possible to change to a new set of operators $\lbrace (\hat b_i^\dagger\,,\,\hat b_i)\rbrace$ in terms of which the dynamics appear less non-local. We demonstrate this by turning a highly non-local random matrix model into a local, 1D lattice theory where particles can propagate in localized wave packets. More generally, we show that any Hamiltonian can be made to look like such a theory, with the lattice dispersion relation and the non-integrability of the theory depending on the spectrum of $\hat H$. We argue that our results are a step towards quantum mereology for fields.

### [113] [Identical Bosons, large occupation numbers and classical field description](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10055)
*Gaurav Goswami*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文检验了“高占据数必然导致经典场描述有效”这一常见假设，发现仅高占据数不足以保证经典行为，只有状态足够接近大占据相干态（coherent state）时经典描述才成立。该结论对超轻暗物质（ultra-light dark matter）的经典场方程应用具有重要含义。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于检验学术界一个普遍但常缺乏论证的假设：当单粒子态的平均占据数（mean occupation number）足够大时，经典场描述（classical field description）必然适用。这一假设被广泛用于超轻暗物质等系统的动力学计算，但其有效性和鲁棒性（robustness）尚未被严格检验。

Method: 采用 $2\sigma_\varphi < |\langle \varphi \rangle|$ 作为经典场行为的判据（criterion），将其应用于任意量子态（arbitrary quantum state）以检验经典行为的成立条件。进一步通过分析量子态偏离相干态（coherent state）的程度，考察何种偏差会破坏经典行为。

Result: 任意具有大占据数的量子态并不必然表现出经典行为；只有对态矢量施加一定限制才能改善经典性。经典描述成立的关键因素是量子态与大占据相干态之间的接近程度（proximity），而非占据数本身的大小。

Conclusion: 高占据数本身不足以保证经典场描述的适用性，状态与相干态的接近程度才是决定性因素。该发现对超轻暗物质模型中经典场方程的使用边界提供了重要约束。

Abstract: For a system with a large number of identical Bosons, it is common to claim, often without any additional justifications, that, when the mean occupation number in a single particle state is sufficiently large, classical field description will be applicable. This is why e.g. for ultra-light dark matter, the classical field equations are used to compute its dynamics. In this work, we test the validity and robustness of this assumption based on the criterion $2 σ_\varphi < |\langle \varphi \rangle| $ for classical field behaviour and applying it to aribtrary quantum states. We find that an arbitrary state with large occupation number doesn't behave classically while imposing some restrictions on the state vectors can improve the classical behavior. Since coherent states are known to have quasi-classical behaviour, we also ask how much deviation from coherent state can spoil the classical behaviour. Based on this analysis, we find that it is the proximity of the state to a large occupation coherent state rather than large occupation number itself which ensures validity of classical description. Implications of this for ultra light dark matter are discussed.

### [114] [Absence of poor local minima in matrix product states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09988)
*Hao-Kai Zhang,Chenghong Zhu,Shuo Liu,Shi-Xin Zhang,Tao Xiang*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过证明矩阵乘积态（MPS）的能量景观不存在不良局部极小值，解释了顺序电路在实践中可训练而砖墙电路不可训练的表观悖论，揭示了有效局部过参数化（effective local overparametrization）在决定可训练性中的关键作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子电路普遍存在严重的可训练性问题，即使是浅层电路也会陷入大量不良局部极小值。然而，由顺序电路制备的矩阵乘积态（MPS）在实践中却表现出显著的可训练性，这构成了一个表观悖论。本文旨在解析这一矛盾。

Method: 本文通过理论证明和数值实验相结合的方式展开研究。理论上，证明MPS能量景观在正交中心（orthogonality center）移动下局部极小值分布具有不变性，并利用MPS的规范自由度（gauge freedom）产生的有效局部过参数化来解释局部极小值向全局极小值集中现象。数值上，对比了顺序电路与砖墙电路（brickwork circuits）在随机哈密顿量下的优化收敛效果。

Result: 理论证明表明，在同样设置下砖墙电路存在不良局部极小值的情况下，MPS的能量景观不存在不良局部极小值。数值实验证实，顺序电路的优化即使对随机哈密顿量也能收敛到接近最优的解，与砖墙电路形成鲜明对比。

Conclusion: MPS的有效局部过参数化是决定其可训练性的关键因素，这一机制类似于过参数化的经典神经网络。研究结果为克服变分量子算法（variational quantum algorithms）的可训练性瓶颈提供了有价值的指导。

Abstract: Quantum circuits suffer from severe trainability issues: even shallow circuits are swamped with poor local minima. Yet matrix product states (MPS), which can be prepared by sequential circuits, are remarkably trainable in practice -- as demonstrated by decades of successful density matrix renormalization group calculations. In this work, we resolve this apparent paradox by proving that the energy landscapes of MPS are free from poor local minima, under the same setting where brickwork circuits are not. The key insight is that the gauge freedom of MPS creates an effective local overparametrization that causes local minima to concentrate near the global minimum, analogous to overparametrized classical neural networks. We rigorously prove that the local minimum distribution of the MPS energy landscape is invariant under moves of the orthogonality center. Numerical experiments further confirm that the optimization of sequential circuits converges to near-optimal solutions even for random Hamiltonians, in stark contrast to brickwork circuits. Our findings highlight the pivotal role of effective local overparametrization in determining trainability, providing a valuable guide for overcoming the trainability bottleneck of variational quantum algorithms.

</details>


### [115] [Precision measurements at the interface between unitary and non-unitary encoding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10529)
*Peng Xu*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文利用线性响应理论和误差传播公式，在包括单粒子和集体退相位（dephasing）及衰减（decay）的广义噪声下，统一分析了酉（unitary）与非酉（non-unitary）编码界面的精度标度（precision scaling），揭示了纠缠在非酉估计中也能达到海森堡极限（Heisenberg limit）的条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在开放量子系统中，噪声对量子计量学（quantum metrology）精度的影响至关重要，但现有研究缺乏对酉与非酉编码界面在广义噪声下统一精度标度的理解。

Method: 采用线性响应理论（linear response theory）和误差传播公式（error propagation formula），推导酉参数 $Ω$ 和耗散强度（dissipation strength）$γ$ 的解析精度表达式。

Result: 对于酉编码，当可观测量（observable）与厄米噪声算符（Hermitian noise operator）对易时，最优编码时间与 $N$ 无关，精度达到海森堡极限 $ΔΩ\propto 1/N$；否则退化为标准量子极限（standard quantum limit）或不再随 $N$ 改善。对于非酉编码，当 $[\hat{A}, \hat{O}] = 0$ 时，精度与内禀动力学及编码时间无关，标度为 $Δγ\propto \sqrt{γ/ \expval*{\hat{L}^\dagger \hat{L}}}$；集体衰减下迪克态（Dicke state）达到海森堡极限 $Δγ\propto 1/N$。

Conclusion: 该工作为噪声环境下量子计量学协议的设计提供了统一的理论框架和实用指导。

Abstract: We investigate precision scaling at the interface between unitary and non-unitary encoding under generalized noise including single-particle and collective dephasing and decay. Using linear response theory and the error propagation formula, we derive analytic precision expressions for both the unitary parameter $Ω$ and the dissipation strength $γ$. For unitary encoding, when the observable commutes with a Hermitian noise operator, the optimal encoding time is independent of $N$, yielding the Heisenberg limit $ΔΩ\propto 1 / N$; otherwise the precision degrades to the standard quantum limit or ceases to improve with $N$. For non-unitary encoding, when $[\hat{A}, \hat{O}] = 0$, the precision is insensitive to intrinsic dynamics and encoding time, scaling as $Δγ\propto \sqrt{γ/ \expval*{\hat{L}^\dagger \hat{L}}}$. Notably, for collective decay, the Dicke state reaches the Heisenberg limit $Δγ\propto 1 / N$, demonstrating that entanglement can enhance non-unitary estimation. Our results provide a unified framework and practical guidance for designing quantum metrology protocols in noisy environments.

Motivation: 准周期系统中通过迁移率边（mobility edge）或局域化转变（localization transition）操控局域化具有重要的物理意义，但目前对耗散如何影响这类系统中的局域化行为尚缺乏深入理解。

Method: 通过分析量子束缚态（quantum bound state）的离散或连续嵌入性质，研究发射器局域化特性与束缚态类型的关联；利用广义对偶变换（generalized duality transformation）解析推导反常迁移率边和临界势强度。

Result: 离散束缚态导致有效激发跳跃呈指数衰减（exponentially decaying），形成局域态；连续谱嵌入束缚态导致正弦振荡（sinusoidally oscillating），形成临界态。腔的物理特性对激发局域化有显著影响，仅通过调节腔场即可操控激发局域化。

Conclusion: 耗散可诱导反常迁移率边和扩展-局域转变，建立了发射器-光子束缚物理与准周期临界性的统一机制，并提供了完整的相图，为通过调节腔场实现局域化操控提供了理论依据。

Abstract: The manipulation of localization in quasiperiodic systems by mobility edges or localization transition holds significant physical importance. In this letter, we demonstrated that the dissipation can induce the emergence of anomalous mobility edges and extended-localized transition in emitter-cavity arrays controlled by quasiperiodic potentials. Specifically, we observe that the localization properties of emitters is governed by the nature of quantum bound states, either discrete or embedded in continuum, providing a unified mechanism linking the emitter-photon bound physics to quasiperiodic criticality. Depending on the bound state discrete or continuumlike, the induced effective excitation hopping exhibits either exponentially decaying or sinusoidally oscillating, giving rise to the formation of localized or critical states, respectively. Through a generalized duality transformation, we analytically determine the anomalous mobility edges and the critical strength of potential, enabling the construction of a full phase diagram. The study reveals that the physical characteristics of cavity exert a significant influence on excitation localization. Therefore, the manipulation of excitation localization can be achieved solely by adjusting the cavity fields.

</details>


### [117] [Inherent flux crosstalk and coupler-driven single-qubit gates in superconducting circuits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10970)
*Balázs Gulácsi,Guido Burkard*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了超导量子比特中随时间变化的外部磁通量如何通过类似法拉第感应定律的机制，在电容耦合的量子比特间产生非平凡的交叉电压驱动（cross-voltage driving），并发现可利用这一效应通过耦合器实现快速单量子比特控制，从而可能消除独立的微波XY控制线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 串扰（crosstalk）——即非期望的量子比特寻址——在扩大量子信息系统规模时严重损害整体性能。超导量子比特通过可调耦合和频率可调性实现高保真纠缠门，但同时也因非期望的磁通耦合引入串扰。本研究旨在量化分析随时间变化的外部磁通量对超导量子比特耦合的影响。

Method: 研究采用量子化电路方法，分析时变外部磁通量对超导量子比特耦合的影响机制，类比法拉第感应定律（Faraday's law of induction）推导电容耦合量子比特间的交叉电压驱动效应。

Result: 当量子比特SQUID环（superconducting quantum interference device loop）中的磁通量随时间变化时，电容耦合的量子比特之间会产生非平凡的交叉电压驱动（cross-voltage driving）。该效应可在标准可调耦合器（tunable-coupler）架构中实现快速单量子比特控制。

Conclusion: 这一发现表明，利用磁通驱动的串扰效应可以替代独立的微波XY控制线（microwave XY control lines），为简化超导量子比特系统的控制架构提供了新途径，有助于量子信息系统的规模化扩展。

Abstract: Crosstalk refers to unwanted qubit addressing. This is particularly detrimental when scaling up quantum information systems because unintended interactions limit their overall performance. For superconducting qubits, tunable couplings and frequency tunability achieved through externally applied magnetic fluxes enable high-fidelity entangling gates; however, they also introduce crosstalk through unintended flux coupling. In this work, we investigate the impact of time-dependent external magnetic fluxes in quantized circuits on superconducting qubit couplings. We find that non-trivial cross-voltage driving emerges between capacitively linked qubits when the magnetic flux threading the SQUID loop of a qubit varies in time, in a manner analogous to Faraday's law of induction. Crucially, we show that this effect enables fast single qubit control through the coupler element in standard tunable-coupler architectures, potentially eliminating the need for individual microwave $XY$ control lines.

### [118] [Rank Collapse, Fixed Points, and the Renormalization Group Structure of MLP Residual Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10324)
*Parviz Haggi-Mani,Irina Rish*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文在多层感知机（MLP）残差网络中首次定量验证了深度神经网络前向传播与重整化群（renormalization group）流之间的类比关系。实验表明，训练后残差流的有效秩随深度单调下降，且该秩塌缩（rank collapse）对输入分布的谱结构具有选择性：短相关长度（~1）的马尔可夫链序列发生显著秩塌缩，而长相关长度（~7）的序列则保持秩稳定；层间核漂移集中在少数几个特定转变层，其余网络层接近不动点（fixed point）状态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管深度神经网络前向传播与重整化群流之间的类比在文献中已被反复提及，但现有讨论仅停留在定性层面：深度被描述为粗粒化尺度，注意力机制被比作配分函数（partition function），表示被说成流向不动点。此前没有任何工作定义过可测量的RG序参量（order parameter），在受控变化的输入分布下测试该类比，或做出可经验验证的定量预测。

Method: 作者研究了最便于处理该类比的最简架构：纯MLP残差堆叠（pure MLP residual stack），在合成马尔可夫链序列上进行掩码词元预测（masked token prediction）任务，该序列具有已知的谱性质。通过控制位置级别的均值池化（mean-pooling）伪影，测量残差流的有效秩随深度的变化，以及层间核漂移的分布模式。

Result: 三项核心发现：(i) 训练后残差流的有效秩随深度单调下降，与无关自由度逐步积分（progressive integration）的预期一致。(ii) 该秩塌缩具有选择性：仅在短相关长度（~1）的链中发生，而在长相关长度（~7）的链中不存在；网络恰好保留了与预测任务相关的自由度，对应重整化群相关性判据（RG relevance criterion）的内容。(iii) 层间核漂移集中在一到两个特定转变层，其余网络层接近不动点，与离散不动点平台（discrete fixed-point plateau）行为一致。

Conclusion: 这些发现构成了首个定量且位置级别的证据，表明MLP残差网络实现了一种由输入分布谱结构（spectral structure）控制的选择性粗粒化（selective coarse-graining）过程。

Abstract: The analogy between deep neural network forward passes and renormalization group (RG) flows has been repeatedly noted in the literature, but existing treatments remain qualitative: depth is described as a coarse-graining scale, attention is likened to a partition function, and representations are said to flow toward fixed points. No existing work has defined a measurable RG order parameter, tested it under controlled variation of the input distribution, or made quantitative predictions that are empirically verified. We study the simplest architecture for which the analogy is tractable: a pure MLP residual stack trained on masked token prediction over synthetic Markov chain sequences with known spectral properties. We report three findings. (i) The effective rank of the residual stream decreases monotonically with depth after training, consistent with progressive integration of irrelevant degrees of freedom. (ii) This rank collapse is selective: it occurs for chains with short correlation length approximately 1 but is absent for chains with long correlation length approximately 7, measured at the position level to control for mean-pooling artifacts. The network preserves exactly the degrees of freedom relevant to the prediction task, the content of the RG relevance criterion. (iii) Inter-layer kernel drift is concentrated at one or two specific transitions, with the remainder of the network near a fixed point, consistent with a discrete fixed-point plateau. Together these findings constitute the first quantitative, position-level evidence that MLP residual networks implement a selective coarse-graining procedure governed by the spectral structure of the input distribution.

</details>


### [119] [Algorithmic and Minimax Complexities in Kernel Bandits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11171)
*Yunbei Xu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文通过统一的信息论框架（MAIR）将 GP-UCB 与 DEC/MAMS 两种方法联系起来，在频率派再生核希尔伯特空间（RKHS）Bandits 中揭示了算法复杂度（algorithmic complexity）与类全局极小极大系数（class-wide minimax coefficient）之间的本质区别。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: GP-UCB 与 DEC/MAMS 方法表面上属于不同的理论体系，缺少统一的视角来理解两者之间的关系及其各自的优劣。

Method: 提出统一的 MAIR（Maximum Algorithmic Information Ratio）框架和异质半正定算法先验（heterogeneous positive-semidefinite algorithmic priors），将 GP-UCB 的算法高斯过程先验与 MAMS 的类全局 MAIR/DEC 包络线置于同一算法信息论语言下进行分析。

Result: 泛化了 GP-UCB 分析与 MAMS 算法；提出了一种结合两者优势的安全主算法（safeguarded master）；通过核Bandits构造证明，在过参数化模型中算法复杂度可以比类全局极小极大或 DEC 证书（certificates）提供更多信息。

Conclusion: 算法信息与类全局极小极大系数回答不同的问题，并可能导致不同的性能差距；核 Bandits 为这一区别提供了清晰的数学可观测环境。

Abstract: Gaussian-process upper confidence bound (GP-UCB) and decision-estimation-coefficient (DEC) methods may appear, at first sight, to belong to different theories. This paper places the two viewpoints in a common algorithmic-information language for frequentist RKHS bandits. GP-UCB fixes an algorithmic, rather than true, Gaussian-process prior and exploits realized-trajectory complexity together with computational tractability, whereas MAMS optimizes a robust class-wide MAIR/DEC envelope. Through the unified MAIR framework and heterogeneous positive-semidefinite algorithmic priors, we generalize both the GP-UCB analysis and the MAMS algorithm, propose a safeguarded master that combines their advantages, and provide a kernel-bandit construction showing that algorithmic complexity can be more informative than class-wide minimax or DEC certificates in overparameterized models. The resulting message is that algorithmic information and class-wide minimax coefficients answer different questions and can lead to different gaps; kernel bandits provide a clean setting in which this distinction becomes mathematically visible.

</details>

### [120] [Patch-Level DINOv2 Scoring for Gravitational-Wave Glitch Detection: Breaking the Signal Dilution Barrier via Vector-Quantized Local Feature Indexing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09933)
*Luca Cirfeta*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于图像块（patch）级别打分的无监督引力波毛刺（glitch）检测架构，通过替换全局CLS相似度指标为top-k块级顺序统计量，克服了DINOv2全局池化对小信号（<5%）的抑制问题，在LIGO O4a数据上展示了显著检测能力，并构建了拓扑显著性图谱用于毛刺定位。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有工作（Cirfeta, 2026b）发现DINOv2的CLS令牌（CLS token）对谱图网格中不足5%的小信号存在系统性抑制，限制了对引力波毛刺的无监督检测能力。本文旨在克服这一信号稀释（signal dilution）问题。

Method: 采用冻结的DINOv2（ViT-S/14），将全局CLS相似度指标替换为基于单个图像块（patch）的top-k顺序统计量（top-k order statistic）；对19类Gravity Spy O3b形态（morphologies）构建向量量化参考索引（Vector-Quantized reference index），每类64个质心（centroids），共1216个质心。

Result: 在LIGO O4a L1数据（session 20260524）的应变域注入（strain-domain injections）实验中，对空间扩展形态（SpiralBurst）实现了显著的分布分离（KS=0.963, 最优k=68）；同时确认了超短瞬变信号（AsymBlip）受到块级时间分辨率限制。构建的拓扑显著性图谱（topological saliency map）成功定位了Scattered_Light和注入SpiralBurst的毛刺特征。

Conclusion: 块级显著性（patch-level saliency）更适合作为拓扑可视化工具（topological visualizer）而非二元检测器，这与DINOv2在引力波谱图嵌入空间（embedding space）中的非各向同性几何（non-isotropic geometry）一致。

Abstract: We present a patch-level scoring architecture for unsupervised gravitational-wave glitch detection that mitigates the signal dilution limitation identified in Cirfeta (2026b). The CLS token of frozen DINOv2 (ViT-S/14) performs global average pooling over 37x37=1369 patches, systematically suppressing signals occupying less than 5% of the spectrogram grid. We replace the global CLS similarity metric with a top-$k$ order statistic over individual patch token similarities against a Vector-Quantized reference index ($K=64$ centroids per class, 19 Gravity Spy O3b morphologies, 1216 total centroids). Applied to strain-domain injections in LIGO O4a L1 data (session 20260524), we demonstrate a statistically significant distributional separation ($\text{KS}=0.963$ at optimal $k=68$) for spatially extended morphologies (SpiralBurst), while confirming the patch-size temporal resolution limit for ultra-short transients (AsymBlip). A topological saliency map constructed from spatial patch similarity against a background matrix (78 null segments) correctly localizes glitch signatures for Scattered_Light and injected SpiralBurst. The Max/Mean ratio analysis demonstrates that patch-level saliency functions as a topological visualizer rather than a binary detector, consistent with the non-isotropic geometry of DINOv2 embedding space on GW spectrograms.

</details>

Result: 基于LIGO、Virgo、KAGRA第三次观测运行（O3）四十天数据的测试表明：参数精度（parameter precision）平均提升5.38%；天图定位（sky localization）精度平均提升16.75%；且结果相比原始GstLAL输出具有更高的准确度（accuracy）。

Conclusion: 所提方法在无需大幅增加延迟的前提下有效改善了GstLAL管道的候选体参数和天图定位表现，并已被GstLAL正式采纳用于第四次观测运行（O4）。

Abstract: Modeled gravitational wave searches correlate the strain data with a bank of gravitational wave template waveforms to make detections of gravitational wave candidates, and these results are processed by downstream tools to calculate the likely sky location and distance of the source of the candidates. This is crucial for multi-messenger efforts, since it informs astronomers where to point their telescopes to facilitate electromagnetic follow-up of the gravitational wave candidates. We present a novel method to improve the low-latency results of the GstLAL gravitational wave search pipeline, and thus improving sky location estimates of low-latency candidates. This method involves ingesting the GstLAL low-latency results, and performing a small targeted hierarchical search to recover the candidates with more accurate parameters, in a medium-latency timescale (few seconds to five minutes). To test our method, we perform a GstLAL low-latency analysis on forty days of data from the third observing run of LIGO, Virgo, and KAGRA, and show that our method improves the GstLAL results by 5.38% and the subsequent sky location results by 16.75% on average. ### [122] [UnReal-B : Real-Space DFT Solver for Matter in Extreme Magnetic Fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10750)

Method: 基于实空间密度泛函理论（real-space Density Functional Theory），针对极端磁场（B ≈ 10¹²–10¹⁵ G）下的一维物质链建模。采用绝热近似（adiabatic approximation）简化计算，构建了一个流线化的数值框架以求解强磁化凝聚态物质的电子结构。

Result: Unreal-B 与多个天体物理相关元素的已发表基准结果进行了对比验证，显示出极好的一致性，同时保持了相对简单和透明的实现方式。

Conclusion: UnReal-B 已作为开源软件发布，能够促进中子星表面物质的可重复研究和社区驱动探索，并为响应未来观测约束的进一步开发提供了基础。

Abstract: As new observational technologies reveal increasingly detailed properties of neutron star surfaces, the demand for accessible and extensible theoretical modeling tools continues to grow. We present UnReal-B, a real-space Density Functional Theory solver for one-dimensional chains of matter in extreme magnetic fields $B \approx 10^{12} - 10^{15},\mathrm{G}$. By employing the adiabatic approximation, UnReal-B, provides a streamlined numerical framework for calculating the electronic structure of strongly magnetized condensed matter. The solver is benchmarked against published results for several astrophysically relevant elements, demonstrating excellent agreement while maintaining a comparatively simple and transparent implementation. Released as open-source software, UnReal-B facilitates reproducible and community-driven investigations of neutron-star surface matter and provides a foundation for future developments motivated by emerging observational constraints.

### [123] [Quantum-geometric origin of superfluid weight in quasicrystals with critical states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09989)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: A distinctive feature of many quasiperiodic systems is the presence of critical states that are neither extended nor exponentially localized. We investigate the geometric effect on the superfluid weight in quasiperiodic systems with critical states at zero temperature. We employ both real-space and momentum-space approaches to superfluid weight in quasicrystals, which allows us to separate the conventional and quantum geometric contributions. We find that the superfluid weight is dominated by the geometric contribution in quasiperiodic systems with critical states. This finding reveals a fundamental interplay between superconductivity and critical states in quasicrystals.

### [124] [Distribution of Majorana modes in the extended-range Kitaev chain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10043)
