<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在Kitaev链模型中，已有研究多集中于短程相互作用，而长程或扩展范围相互作用（extended-range interactions）下的拓扑性质尚未被充分理解。本文旨在探讨当配对项和跳跃项以代数方式衰减时，系统的拓扑相结构、拓扑不变量的解析表达以及边缘模的物理行为。

Method: 假设配对项和跳跃项在空间中以指数α和β呈代数衰减；在截断范围情形下分析拓扑相数量与耦合近邻站点数的关系；推导拓扑不变量（topological invariant）和相变的解析公式；引入马约拉纳平均位置（Majorana average position）来测量边缘模的空间分布；以次近邻Kitaev链为例，在有限尺寸团簇中进行数值计算，并定义有效宇称（effective parity）来描述边缘-边缘非局域费米子态的占据。

Result: 在截断范围情形下，拓扑相的数量等于所耦合近邻站点数；有效宇称展现出超越基态费米子宇称交换（energetic exchange from the ground-state fermion parity switches）的新特征，这些特征与各边缘模的分布相关；计算表明基态费米子宇称与边缘占据数之间存在直接关联，这一关联反映在马约拉纳平均位置的局域化与退局域化上。

Conclusion: 扩展范围相互作用的Kitaev链模型在保持拓扑缠绕数不变的前提下，其拓扑相结构可由截断范围的耦合近邻数决定；通过马约拉纳平均位置和有效宇称，可以更深入地理解边缘模的分布与基态费米子宇称之间的内在联系。

Abstract: The topological properties of the Kitaev chain model with extended-range interactions are investigated, focusing on cases where the topological winding number is preserved. We assume that the pairing and hopping terms decay algebraically in space with exponents $α$ and $β$, respectively. We show that in the truncated-range scenario, there are as many distinct topological phases as the number of coupled neighboring sites. In addition, an explicit analytical formulation is provided to evaluate the topological invariant and the phase transitions that emerge in these systems. Besides the analytical description, we introduce a new physical insight into the topological excitations of the ground-state by measuring the spatial distribution of the edge modes with the Majorana average position. Taking the next-nearest neighbor Kitaev chains as a probe, various numerical calculations of Majorana edge states were performed in finite-size clusters to determine the sensitivity of the topological zero energy modes to the parameters of interest. The occupation of edge-to-edge non-local fermion states is computed and defined as an effective parity. Such an effective parity exhibits new interesting features beyond the energetic exchange from the ground-state fermion parity switches, which are related to the distribution of the respective edge modes. Our calculations show a direct correlation between the ground-state fermion parity and the edge occupation numbers, which are translated into localization and delocalization of the Majorana average position.

</details>


### [125] [Microscopic Investigation of the Superconducting State in CuCo$_{2}$S$_{4}$: Evidence for an Intermediate-Coupling Fully Gapped Superconductor](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10162)
*K. Panda,A. Bhattacharyya,Liang-Wen Ji,Jing Li,R. Stewart,D. T. Adroja,Guang-Han Cao*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文通过μ子自旋旋转与弛豫（μSR）测量，结合磁化强度与热容实验，首次对过渡金属硫族化合物尖晶石CuCo₂S₄的超导态进行了微观研究。结果表明该材料具有完全能隙（fully gapped）的超导有序参量，间隙比2Δ(0)/(k_B T_SC)=3.95(2)超过BCS弱耦合值，处于中等电子-声子耦合区间；零场μSR未观察到时间反演对称性破缺（TRSB）的证据，但受铁磁杂质相影响，不能完全排除其存在。综合证据支持CuCo₂S₄展现出与常规s波超导一致的完全能隙中等耦合超导态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索过渡金属硫族化合物尖晶石（thiospinel）CuCo₂S₄中的超导现象，并提供微观层面的超导态实验证据。

Method: 采用μ子自旋旋转与弛豫（muon spin rotation and relaxation, μSR）测量，辅以磁化强度（magnetization）与热容（heat-capacity）实验。

Result: 横向场μSR显示出完全能隙的超导有序参量；间隙比2Δ(0)/(k_B T_SC)=3.95(2)超过BCS弱耦合值3.53，表明中等耦合强度；零场μSR未探测到时间反演对称性破缺（time-reversal symmetry breaking, TRSB）的自发内磁场，但铁磁杂质相降低了测量灵敏度，无法彻底排除TRSB。

Conclusion: CuCo₂S₄具有完全能隙（fully gapped）的超导态，耦合强度为中等，行为与常规s波超导（conventional s-wave superconductivity）一致。

Abstract: The thiospinel compound CuCo$_2$S$_4$ provides an attractive platform for exploring superconductivity in transition-metal chalcogenide spinels. Here, we report the first microscopic investigation of the superconducting state in CuCo$_2$S$_4$ using muon spin rotation and relaxation ($μ$SR) measurements, complemented by magnetization and heat-capacity experiments. The temperature dependence of the superconducting depolarization rate obtained from transverse-field $μ$SR measurements indicates a fully gapped superconducting order parameter. The extracted gap ratio $2Δ(0)/(k_{\mathrm{B}}T_\mathrm{SC}) = 3.95(2)$ exceeds the BCS weak-coupling value of 3.53, placing CuCo$_2$S$_4$ in the intermediate electron-phonon coupling regime. Zero-field $μ$SR measurements were performed to probe possible time-reversal symmetry breaking (TRSB) in the superconducting state. Within the experimental resolution, no additional spontaneous internal magnetic fields are observed below $T_c$. However, due to the presence of a ferromagnetic impurity phase and the associated fast-relaxing signal component, the sensitivity of the present measurements to weak spontaneous fields is reduced. Consequently, while no evidence for TRSB is detected, its existence cannot be definitively ruled out. Overall, our combined thermodynamic and $μ$SR results demonstrate that CuCo$_2$S$_4$ exhibits a fully gapped superconducting state with intermediate coupling strength, consistent with conventional $s$-wave superconductivity in this cobalt-based thiospinel system.

</details>


### [126] [Vortex pinning of Ba$_{0.62}$K$_{0.38}$BiO$_3$ investigated by magneto-optical Kerr-effect and magnetization measurements](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10300)
*Soichiro Yamane,Sota Nakamura,Atsutoshi Ikeda,Dayu Zhai,Siddarth Gorregattu,Xing He,Sudarshan Sharma,Yipeng Cai,Yasutomo J. Uemura,Martin Greven,Shingo Yonezawa*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文利用超高分辨率磁光克尔效应（MOKE）和磁化测量，研究了三维氧化物超导体Ba1-xKxBiO3中的涡旋钉扎（vortex pinning）行为，发现零场MOKE信号呈现显著的磁历史依赖，该行为可用Bean临界态模型（Bean's critical-state model）描述，并验证了MOKE作为光学介观探针在第二类超导体（type-II superconductors）混合态研究中的可行性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 涡旋钉扎（vortex pinning）是决定第二类超导体（type-II superconductors）不可逆磁响应和涡旋运动耗散的关键因素，但针对三维氧化物超导体中涡旋钉扎的光学探测手段尚不充分，需发展新的互补性实验方法。

Method: 实验采用超高分辨率磁光克尔效应（MOKE）结合精细磁化测量，系统采集Ba1-xKxBiO3在超导态下的零场MOKE信号，并分析其随训练场（training field）演化的磁历史依赖行为。

Result: 零场MOKE信号呈现显著的磁历史依赖，类似于俘获涡旋（trapped vortices）引起的剩余磁化（remanent magnetization）；该演化行为可被Bean临界态模型（Bean's critical-state model）准确描述。训练场依赖在零场附近呈线性关系，未发现自发时间反演对称性破缺（spontaneous time-reversal-symmetry breaking）的异常特征。

Conclusion: MOKE被确立为一种可行的光学介观探针，可用于第二类超导体（type-II superconductors）中涡旋钉扎（vortex pinning）的探测，并为区分涡旋诱导的MOKE响应与时间反演对称性破缺（time-reversal-symmetry broken）超导序参量贡献提供了清晰的实验协议。

Abstract: Vortex pinning plays a crucial role in determining properties of type-II superconductors. For example, it governs the irreversible magnetic response as well as dissipation caused by vortex motion. Here, we study vortex pinning in the three-dimensional oxide superconductor Ba1-xKxBiO3 using ultra-high-resolution magneto-optical Kerr effect (MOKE) and detailed magnetization measurements. We find that the zero-field MOKE signal in the superconducting state exhibits a pronounced magnetic-history dependence. This behavior closely resembles the remanent magnetization caused by trapped vortices. Furthermore, we demonstrate that the observed evolution of the MOKE signals is well described by Bean's critical-state model for trapped vortices. Our results establish MOKE as a viable optical and mesoscopic probe of vortex pinning in type-II superconductors, providing a new complementary approach to investigate mixed-state phenomena. We also find that the training-field dependence of the MOKE is linear near zero training field, without any anomalies indicative of spontaneous time-reversal-symmetry breaking in an unconventional superconducting state. Our study defines a clear protocol to distinguish vortex-induced MOKE responses from those associated with a time-reversal-symmetry broken superconducting order parameter.

</details>


### [127] [Superheating field of clean superconductors near the type-I--type-II boundary: the low-temperature Meissner stability limit of niobium](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10420)
*Takayuki Kubo*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文利用自洽非线性非局域 Eilenberger 理论，计算了位于第 I 类与第 II 类超导体边界附近的洁净超导体（特别是 Nb）的低温超热场 $B_{\rm sh}$，发现该值远高于从 Ginzburg-Landau 理论在 $T_c$ 附近简单外推至低温所得的结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超热场（superheating field）是超导腔等应用中的重要性能极限参数，但此前缺乏对低温下、位于 I 类与 II 类超导体边界附近（如 Nb，$\kappa_{\rm GL}=0.7$）的自洽、非线性、非局域计算。

Method: 基于自洽非线性非局域 Eilenberger 理论（self-consistent nonlinear nonlocal Eilenberger theory），结合 Meissner 态的线性稳定性分析（linear stability analysis）进行数值计算。

Result: 对于 Nb 类材料 ($\kappa_{\rm GL}=0.7$)，在 $T/T_c=0.2$ 且 $B_{c0}\simeq 200\,{\rm mT}$ 时，得到 $B_{\rm sh}\simeq 290\,{\rm mT}$。该值显著高于将 $T_c$ 附近的 Ginzburg-Landau 结果简单地外推到低温区所得的数值。对于 TESLA 形状的 Nb 加速腔，该结果对应约 $67\,{\rm MV/m}$ 的内禀 Meissner 稳定性极限。

Conclusion: 洁净 Nb 在低温下的超热场远高于传统 Ginzburg-Landau 外推预测，表明其在 TESLA 型加速腔中具有更高的内禀 Meissner 稳定性极限（约 $67\,{\rm MV/m}$），对超导腔设计和性能评估具有重要指导意义。

Abstract: We calculate the low-temperature superheating field $B_{\rm sh}$ of clean superconductors near the boundary between type-I and type-II superconductivity, with particular emphasis on Nb. The calculation is based on the self-consistent nonlinear nonlocal Eilenberger theory and the linear stability analysis of the Meissner state. For a Nb-like material with $κ_{\rm GL}=0.7$, we obtain $B_{\rm sh}\simeq 290\,{\rm mT}$ at $T/T_c=0.2$, using $B_{c0}\simeq 200\,{\rm mT}$. This value is substantially higher than the value obtained by naively extrapolating the Ginzburg--Landau result near $T_c$ to $T\ll T_c$. For a TESLA-shaped Nb accelerator cavity, it corresponds to an intrinsic Meissner-stability limit of about $67\,{\rm MV/m}$.

### [128] [Dichotomous electronic system in a bilayer Ni$^{1+}$ nickelate](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10564)
*Young-Joon Song,W. E. Pickett,K. -W. Lee*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文通过分析新报道的层状镍酸盐La₃Ni₂O₅F（具有理想二维特征），提出其超导电性来源于间隙电子密度（interstitial density）形成的独特能带结构：部分占据的E*能带（源自间隙态）与Ni d轨道耦合，导致非解析狄拉克点（non-analytic Dirac point）及空穴-电子准粒子二分性，从而引发非常规超导态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 无限层镍酸盐（Infinite layer nickelates, ILNs）在空穴掺杂后展现超导电性，但其电子结构机制尚未完全厘清，特别是间隙态（interstitial states）导致的次级费米面（secondary Fermi surface）和自掺杂（self-doping）效应。新发现的La₃Ni₂O₅F为理解这类材料中基于间隙密度的非常规超导机制提供了理想二维平台。

Method: 基于新报道的La₃Ni₂O₅F化合物（形式氧化态Ni¹⁺）的电子结构分析，结合其理想二维特征（essentially ideal two dimensional character），聚焦部分占据的E*能带（源于间隙密度）的强各向异性形状、圆柱形电子费米面以及E*与Ni d_{xz}, d_{yz}轨道之间的耦合。

Result: E*能带具有强各向异性，跨越三个“顶端（apical）”层，形成圆柱形电子费米面并导致自掺杂。该间隙密度与包括Ni d_{xz}, d_{yz}在内的价带网络（network of valence bands）相关联，与E*共同产生初始的非解析狄拉克点（incipient non-analytic Dirac point），形成一种非常规的间隙密度–d带耦合。

Conclusion: E*电子带与常规Ni dpσ带将表现出空穴和电子准粒子行为（quasiparticle behavior）在正常态输运和远红外性质中的二分性（dichotomy），并可能导致即使对于镍酸盐而言也属于非常规的超导态性质。

Abstract: ``Infinite layer'' nickelates (ILNs) ${\cal R}$NiO$_2$ (${\cal R}$=rare earth elements), having empty apical O sites, become superconducting upon hole doping. They display a secondary electron Fermi surface (FS), giving hole doping, arising not from atomic orbitals but from a band based on interstitial density. Newly reported La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_5$F, formally Ni$^{1+}$, provides an unexpected example of ILN with essentially ideal two dimensional character. A partially occupied single band $E^*$, based on interstitial density, has distinct properties, as its strongly anisotropic shape extends over the three ``apical'' layers and leads to a cylindrical electron FS giving self-doping. This interstitial density is associated with a {\it network of valence bands}, including a Ni $d_{xz},d_{yz}$ pair that partners with $E^*$ to provide an incipient non-analytic Dirac point, leading to an unusual type of interstitial density--$d$ band coupling. The $E^*$ electron band and the conventional Ni $dpσ$ band will display a dichotomy of hole and electron quasiparticle behavior in normal state transport and far-IR properties, and likely resulting in unconventional superconducting state properties even for nickelates.

</details>


### [129] [Majorana fermions at self-generated interfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10812)
*Nikola Prodanov,Sergio Ciuchi,Sergio Caprara*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文通过将Kitaev模型与经典弹性晶格场耦合，研究了在系统内部（而非仅端点）产生Majorana费米子的可能性。电子-晶格相互作用导致具有不同拓扑不变量的超导区域发生相分离，从而在内部界面处形成Majorana束缚态，最终在系统体态中实现稀薄的Majorana费米子气体。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准Kitaev模型仅在拓扑相参数条件下于系统端点产生局域的Majorana费米子；本文试图探索是否能在系统的体态（bulk）内部，而非仅物理边界处，实现Majorana费米子的涌现。

Method: 将Kitaev模型推广，引入电子密度与经典弹性晶格场（classical elastic lattice field）之间的局域耦合。该电子-晶格相互作用能够诱发具有不同拓扑不变量（topological invariants）的超导区域之间的相分离（phase separation），从而在系统内部生成可承载Majorana束缚态（Majorana bound states）的内界面。

Result: 在适当的参数条件下，系统体态内部可以形成由内界面产生的Majorana束缚态，进而实现一种稀薄的Majorana费米子气体（dilute gas of Majorana fermions）。

Conclusion: 通过在Kitaev模型中引入电子-晶格耦合，可以在系统体态内部实现Majorana费米子，而不局限于端点位置。这为在凝聚态系统中构建和操控体态Majorana费米子提供了一种新途径。

Abstract: The Kitaev model describing a one-dimensional topological superconducting chain is known to support two Majorana fermions localized at the systems endpoints when the parameters are tuned to the topological phase. In this work, we investigate the possibility that Majorana fermions may also emerge away from the physical boundaries of the chain. To this purpose, we generalize the Kitaev model by incorporating a local coupling between the electronic density and a classical elastic (lattice) field. This electron-lattice interaction can induce phase separation between superconducting regions characterized by distinct topological invariants, thereby generating internal interfaces that host Majorana bound states. Under these conditions, a dilute gas of Majorana fermions can be realized in the bulk of the system.

</details>


### [130] [On pseudogap phase as precursor to a superconducting dome in high-Tc cuprates: Non-analytic T* as a function of doping](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11056)
*Felix A. Buot*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文推广了量子材料中赝能隙相作为超导穹顶前驱体的条件，揭示了T*作为掺杂函数的非解析行为，并基于纠缠与约束空穴配对（ECHP）机制为高Tc铜氧化物超导体的完整相图提供了微观解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究已观察到赝能隙（pseudogap）相与超导穹顶（SC dome）之间的关联，但缺乏统一的普适条件来描述这一前驱关系，尤其是在不同掺杂类型的高温超导体（high-Tc cuprates）中。

Method: 通过引入配置序参量（configurational-ordering parameter）的变化率作为掺杂函数，结合扩展配对（extended pairing）与无序对（disordered pairs）延展长度的递减关系，推导出赝能隙温度T*的非解析行为，并基于纠缠与约束空穴配对（entanglement and confinement hole pairing, ECHP）机制构建理论框架。

Result: 超导穹顶的产生需要满足两个条件：（1）赝能隙温度T*随掺杂增加而递减，源于掺杂空穴扩展配对尺寸的减小；（2）配置序参量变化率随掺杂增加而递增，源于无序对延展长度的减小。该理论由Buot等人近期提出，揭示了电子掺杂和空穴掺杂高Tc铜氧化物的完整相图微观特征。

Conclusion: 推广后的条件较为普适地描述了赝能隙相作为超导前驱体的机制，ECHP机制为理解高Tc铜氧化物超导体的复杂相图提供了新的微观视角。

Abstract: We generalize the condition under which a quantum material exhibiting a pseudogap phase is a precursor to a superconducting (SC) dome. The result reveals the non-analytic T* as a function of doping. A well-known example is the high-Tc cuprates. Essentially, the SC dome is generated under two conditions: (1) that the pseudogap T* is a decreasing function of doping, due to the decrease in size of extended pairing of doped holes with doping, and most importantly, (2) that the rate of configurational-ordering parameter is an increasing function of doping as a result of the decrease in extended length of the disordered pairs. These two conditions are provided by the new entanglement and confinement pairing mechanism of high-Tc cuprates. This is a theory that has recently been discussed in the literature by Buot et al. It hinges on a novel strong entanglement and confinement hole pairing (ECHP) mechanism that unravels the microscopic features of the entire phase diagram of both electron and hole-doped high-Tc cuprates.

</details>

### [131] [Quantum Otto and Carnot Cycles via Skew Ising Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09911)
*Neda Valizadeh,Nayyere Einali Saghavaz,Zahra Ebadi,Hosein Mohammadzadeh*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究了基于倾斜磁场下两自旋系统（two-spin system）的量子热机与制冷机的热力学性能，比较了量子卡诺循环（Carnot cycle）与奥托循环（Otto cycle），揭示了相互作用和磁场倾斜角对性能的调控作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索量子热机（quantum heat engine）和量子制冷机（quantum refrigerator）在考虑自旋-自旋耦合（spin-spin coupling）及各向异性（anisotropy）条件下的热力学性能，并理解相互作用与能谱结构对循环性能的影响机制。

Method: 以受倾斜磁场（skew magnetic field）作用的两自旋系统为工作物质，采用包含自旋耦合与各向异性的相互作用自旋模型（interacting spin model），分析了量子卡诺循环与量子奥托循环（Otto cycle）的热力学特性。

Result: 卡诺循环展现由熵驱动的普适行为，相边界平滑；奥托循环则呈现由能谱与非平衡布居差异共同决定的丰富结构。在效率（efficiency）和性能系数（coefficient of performance, COP）中均发现随相互作用强度变化的交叉行为，源于相互作用能标与磁场的竞争。倾斜角（skew angle）诱导态杂化（state hybridization），改变能级与占据概率。

Conclusion: 适当调控相互作用与各向异性可增强量子热力学器件的性能；多能级效应（multi-level effects）在量子热机设计中具有重要意义。

Abstract: We investigate the thermodynamic performance of quantum heat engines and refrigerators based on a two-spin system subject to a skew magnetic field. The working substance is described by an interacting spin model that incorporates both spin--spin coupling and anisotropy induced by a tilted magnetic field. We analyze and compare quantum Carnot and Otto cycles, showing that the Carnot cycle exhibits a universal, entropy-driven behavior with smooth phase boundaries, while the Otto cycle displays a much richer structure governed by the interplay between the energy spectrum and nonequilibrium population differences. In particular, we identify a crossover in both efficiency and coefficient of performance as a function of the interaction strength, which arises from the competition between the interaction energy scale and the magnetic field. We further demonstrate that the skew angle induces state hybridization, modifying both the energy levels and occupation probabilities. Our results highlight that interactions and anisotropy, when properly tuned, can enhance thermodynamic performance, and emphasize the importance of multi-level effects in the design of quantum thermal machines.

</details>


### [132] [Computing phase diagrams using a convex hull algorithm](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09921)
*C. P. Dullemond,E. D. Young*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于凸包（convex hull）算法的通用计算方法，用于计算岩石及其熔体在给定温度和压力下的组分相图（compositional phase diagram），并将实现公开为Python包。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统方法在确定相稳定性、相分离、结线（tie line）定位以及固相线（solidus）、液相线（liquidus）、溶线（solvus）、共晶/包晶点（eutectic/peritectic point）等特征时存在复杂性，缺乏一个统一且直观的计算方案。

Method: 基于组分和吉布斯自由能（Gibbs free energy）空间中的点集凸包数学概念，通过计算凸包并补充一个对所得单纯形（simplex）进行物理分类的算法，统一处理相图计算中的各类复杂性。凸包计算使用公开的Qhull包（通过SciPy调用）。

Result: 该方法对于最多四组分的系统具有显著的稳定性和效率，但不适用于多组分（大量组分）系统。实现已被发布为公开可用的Python包。

Conclusion: 该方法简单、通用、直观，可广泛应用于科学研究和教育领域，使相图计算变得更加易于访问。

Abstract: We present a simple universal computational algorithm for computing compositional phase diagrams of rocks and their melts at given temperature and pressure. It makes use of the mathematical concept of the convex hull of a set of points in the space spanned by the composition and the Gibbs free energy. All the complexities of determining the stability or separation of phases, the localization and orientation of tie lines, as well as the determination of characteristic points, curves and surfaces such as the solidus, liquidus, solvus, and the eutectic/peritectic points etc, are taken care of by the algorithm that computes the convex hull, supplemented with an algorithm to physically classify the resulting simplices. For the convex hull computation, the publicly available Qhull package can be used, which is available in SciPy. This makes this method accessible and intuitive for a broad set of scientific and educational applications. Although the method is not practical for systems of a large number of components, it is remarkably stable and efficient for systems of up to four. We present our implementation of the method as a publicly available Python package.

### [133] [The Two Dimensional Dynamical Bulk Boundary Correspondence: Beyond Two Band Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10731)
*Tomasz Masłowski,Nicholas Sedlmayr*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文检验了二维拓扑超导体中动力学体-边对应关系（dynamical bulk-boundary correspondence）的普遍性，发现其并不简单地由淬火前后的平衡态拓扑数决定，还与边界取向有关，暗示可能存在弱拓扑变体。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有研究在一维和二维拓扑模型中提出动力学体-边对应关系的存在，但其确切原因和普遍性尚未明确。

Method: 选取具有丰富相图的二维拓扑超导体（topological superconductor），在不同陈数（Chern numbers）之间进行突然淬火（sudden quench），系统考察动力学自由能（dynamical free energy）及其边界贡献。

Result: 淬火前后平衡态拓扑数之间不存在直接的动力学体-边对应关系；该对应关系依赖于边界取向，可能具有弱拓扑变体（weak topological variant）的特征。

Conclusion: 动力学体-边对应并非简单由平衡态拓扑量决定，其机制更为复杂，且可能受边界几何和弱拓扑性质的影响。

Abstract: A dynamical equivalent of the bulk-boundary correspondence has been suggested to occur in one and two dimensional topological models following sudden quenches. Depending on the topological invariant of the time evolving and initial phases involved large boundary contributions to a dynamical free energy occur. Moreover they occur periodically between the critical times at which this dynamical free energy becomes non-analytic, \emph{i.e.}~at dynamical quantum phase transitions. At these critical times the eigenvalue spectrum of the Loschmidt matrix which underlies the dynamical free energy closes its gap. The boundary contributions are understood to be due to zero-modes or in-gap bands of this matrix, forming a close analogy with equilibrium topological models and their edge modes. The exact cause of this phenomena and its generality remain unknown. In this article we test the dynamical bulk-boundary correspondence for a complicated two dimensional topological superconductor with a rich phase diagram, allowing quenches between many different Chern numbers. We show that there is no straightforward correspondence between the equilibrium phases quenched between and the dynamical bulk boundary correspondence. Furthermore the correspondence can depend on the orientation of the edges, suggesting a possible weak topological variant.

### [134] [Dynamical Partition Functions of Stochastic Dynamics via Variational Flows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10757)
*Zequn Lin,Ying Tang*

TL;DR: 本文提出一种无网格神经变分框架，利用生成流模型（generative flow models）实现Feynman-Kac定理，从而统一计算有限时间和渐近时间轨迹热力学（trajectory thermodynamics），在高维非平衡连续态系统中克服了维度灾难和指数增长副本需求的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非平衡热力学（nonequilibrium thermodynamics）由动力学配分函数（dynamical partition function）控制，但高维连续态动力学中该函数的计算长期面临挑战。Feynman-Kac形式体系虽能为任意路径观测量的生成函数提供严格表示，但实际计算在低维或弱噪声极限之外受到维度灾难（curse of dimensionality）和轨迹方法指数增长副本需求的阻碍。

Method: 开发了一种无网格神经变分框架（mesh-free neural variational framework），利用生成流模型实现Feynman-Kac定理，将倾斜随机演化（tilted stochastic evolution）重新表述为一个时间相关的优化问题。

Result: 该方法可直接以统一方式计算有限时间和渐近时间的轨迹热力学，适用于一般观测量，能够评估功、熵产生（entropy production）和电流涨落（current fluctuations）。在包括高维情形在内的多种非平衡系统中验证了该方法的准确性和可扩展性。

Conclusion: 所提出的神经变分方法有效克服了高维非平衡连续态系统中动力学配分函数计算的传统障碍，为实现大规模轨迹热力学分析提供了一种可扩展的实用方案。

Abstract: Nonequilibrium thermodynamics is governed by the dynamical partition function, and its computation in high-dimensional continuous-state dynamics is a longstanding challenge. The Feynman-Kac formalism provides a rigorous representation for generating functions of arbitrary path observables; however, practical evaluation beyond low dimensions or the weak-noise limit is hindered by the curse of dimensionality and the exponentially growing replica demands of trajectory-based methods. Here we develop a mesh-free neural variational framework that realizes the Feynman-Kac theorem with generative flow models, recasting tilted stochastic evolution as a time-dependent optimization problem. This approach enables the direct computation of both finite-time and asymptotic trajectory thermodynamics in a unified manner. The method applies to general observables, enabling the evaluation of work, entropy production, and current fluctuations. We demonstrate the accuracy and scalability of this method in various nonequilibrium systems including high-dimensional cases.

### [135] [Continuous and discontinuous transitions in the Ising-Heisenberg model on the extended Lieb lattice in a magnetic field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10821)
*David Sivy,Jozef Strecka*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过精确映射将外加磁场下的扩展Lieb晶格自旋-1/2 Ising-Heisenberg模型转化为方格上的有效自旋-1/2 Ising模型，揭示了基态相图包含量子反铁磁相（QAF）、量子单体-二聚体相（MD）、经典亚铁磁相（FRI）和经典铁磁相等四个相区，并利用精确与近似解析计算及蒙特卡罗模拟证实了连续与非连续热相变的存在与性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在低维自旋系统（low-dimensional spin systems）中，Ising-Heisenberg模型能够同时捕捉经典Ising相互作用与量子Heisenberg相互作用，但扩展Lieb晶格（extended Lieb lattice）在外加磁场下的精确解及其相变特性尚未被充分研究，因此本文旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 首先通过严格映射（exact mapping）将自旋-1/2 Ising-Heisenberg模型转化为方格（square lattice）上的有效自旋-1/2 Ising模型；随后采用解析方法（包括精确与近似计算）分析基态相图（ground-state phase diagram）与热相变（thermal phase transitions）特征；最后以蒙特卡罗模拟（Monte Carlo simulation）对理论预测进行数值验证。

Result: 基态相图包含量子反铁磁相（quantum antiferromagnetic, QAF）、量子单体-二聚体相（quantum monomer-dimer, MD）、经典亚铁磁相（classical ferrimagnetic, FRI）和经典铁磁相（classical ferromagnetic）四个相区。MD-FRI基态相边界在有限温度下扩展为穹顶状不连续热跃变曲面，并由Ising临界点（Ising critical point）线所界定。QAF相则被来自QAF-MD和QAF-FRI基态相边界的连续热跃变曲面所包围。

Conclusion: 本文通过解析与数值相结合的方法，完整刻画了扩展Lieb晶格上Ising-Heisenberg模型在外场下的相图结构，并确认了其中连续与非连续热相变的存在性。该结果不仅验证了映射方法的有效性，也为理解具有量子与经典混合相互作用的自旋系统的相变行为提供了可靠的理论依据。

Abstract: The spin-1/2 Ising-Heisenberg model on the extended Lieb lattice in a magnetic field is exactly mapped onto an effective spin-1/2 Ising model on the square lattice. The ground-state phase diagram comprises the quantum antiferromagnetic (QAF), quantum monomer-dimer (MD), classical ferrimagnetic (FRI), and classical ferromagnetic phase. The MD-FRI ground-state phase boundary extends to finite temperatures as a dome-shaped surface of discontinuous thermal transitions bounded by a line of Ising critical points. The QAF phase is enclosed by a surface of continuous thermal transitions evolving from the QAF-MD and QAF-FRI ground-state phase boundaries. Monte Carlo simulations fully confirm the existence and nature of both continuous and discontinuous thermal phase transitions obtained by exact and approximate analytical calculations.

### [136] [Thermodynamic Approach to Momentum Transport in Dense Fluids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10858)
*Christopher Devik Fjeldstad,Jonas Bueie,Astrid S. de Wijn*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个扩展Chapman-Enskog理论的新框架，通过引入与系统热力学性质相关的交换函数（exchange function），替代了传统的有效硬球直径方法。该框架统一了包括修正Enskog理论（MET）在内的现有扩展，并在此基础上提出了一种考虑粒子间势能相互作用的替代方案。该方案在Weeks-Chandler-Anderson（WCA）流体和Lennard-Jones（LJ）流体的剪切粘度预测中，在低至中等密度（ρ^* ≤ 0.3）下实现了2%–4%的平均相对误差，在所有考察密度下的最大平均误差分别为4.4%和8.1%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的Chapman-Enskog理论主要适用于硬球流体模型，在实际流体（如Lennard-Jones流体等）中的应用存在局限性。现有的扩展方法（如修正Enskog理论，modified Enskog theory, MET）多依赖于有效硬球直径，缺乏与系统热力学性质的直接联系。因此，本文旨在发展一个更具普适性的理论框架，以更准确地预测真实流体的输运性质。

Method: 提出了一种新的理论框架，不依赖有效硬球直径，而是引入一个与系统热力学性质直接相关的交换函数（exchange function）来扩展Chapman-Enskog理论。在该框架下，修正Enskog理论（MET）被证明是其特例。基于此框架，进一步提出了一种新的表达式，该表达式明确考虑了流体中粒子间相互作用的势能（potential interaction energy）。

Result: 在Lennard-Jones单位下，对于密度范围ρ^* ∈ [0.05, 0.8]和温度范围T^* ∈ [1.5, 4.0]，新方法应用于WCA流体和LJ流体的剪切粘度（shear viscosity）预测。在低至中等密度（ρ^* ≤ 0.3）下，两类流体的平均相对预测误差为2%–4%。在所有考察密度下，WCA流体的最大平均相对误差为4.4%，LJ流体为8.1%。此外，还考察了包括双原子分子模型在内的其他相互作用模型，以探索方法的局限性。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了一个统一的理论框架，能够将已有的MET等扩展方法纳入其中，并发展出更普适的替代方案。新方法在宽广的密度和温度范围内对Lennard-Jones型流体的剪切粘度给出了较高精度的预测，表明其在实际流体输运性质计算中具有应用潜力。对双原子等模型的研究则有助于明确该方法的适用范围和边界条件。

Abstract: We present a new framework for extending Chapman-Enskog theory beyond the hard-sphere fluid model. Rather than relying on effective hard sphere diameters, the approach makes use of on an exchange function which can be related to the thermodynamic properties of the system. We show that two existing extensions, including modified Enskog theory (MET), fit into this new framework. Based on our approach, we propose an alternative to MET that takes into account the potential interaction energy associated with the inter-particle interactions in the fluid. The proposed expression is applied to predicting the shear viscosity of several different simulated fluid models across a wide set of densities $0.05 \leq ρ^* \leq 0.8$ and temperatures $1.5 \leq T^* \leq 4.0$ in Lennard-Jones units. The fluid models considered include both the Weeks-Chandler-Anderson (WCA) fluid and the Lennard-Jones (LJ) fluid. At low and intermediate density, here taken to be $ρ^* \leq 0.3$, we report mean relative prediction errors between $2\%$ and $4\%$ for both these. Across all densities considered, the largest mean relative errors reported are $4.4\%$ and $8.1\%$ for the WCA fluid and LJ fluid respectively. We also investigate other interaction models, including a diatomic molecular model, in order to better understand the limitations of our approach.

</details>


### [137] [Geometry still matters in quasi-one-dimensional single-file transport](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10991)
*Olivier Bénichou,Aurélien Grabsch*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文证明，在有限宽度的准一维通道中，即使禁止粒子超越（overtaking），集体输运（collective transport）仍受横向平衡结构的控制，导致扩散系数在密度上出现非单调行为，从而挑战了“单列输运等价于严格一维输运”的传统观念。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统观点认为，一旦禁止超越，单列输运（single-file transport）就简化为严格的一维运动。本文旨在检验这一简化在实验相关的有限宽度通道中是否成立，并揭示横向结构对输运定律的定性影响。

Method: 从完整受限几何中的布朗动力学（Brownian dynamics）出发，推导出纵向密度的精确大尺度一维涨落流体力学（fluctuating hydrodynamics），其系数由受限平衡态方程确定。在最小硬核（hard-core）设定下分析集体扩散系数（collective diffusivity）的密度依赖性。

Result: 发现集体扩散系数可在密度上呈现非单调行为，这一几何异常（geometric anomaly）传播至积分电流涨落、示踪粒子位移涨落及相关密度分布的精确大尺度预测。该效应对于相互作用势、通道几何、初始制备和微观动力学均具有鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 准一维单列输运定义了一个独特机制：禁止超越并不会从集体输运中消除几何效应。因此，将单列输运直接约化为严格一维的描述在有限宽度通道中失效。

Abstract: Single-file transport means no overtaking: particles move in a narrow channel while preserving their longitudinal order. This simple constraint has profound dynamical consequences, most notably tracer subdiffusion, and has made single-file transport a paradigmatic form of confined many-body motion, observed from molecular transport in zeolites to single-file diffusion of colloids in narrow channels. The standard view is that, once overtaking is suppressed, collective transport reduces to that of a strictly one-dimensional file. Here we show that this reduction fails in experimentally relevant finite-width channels: even when exchange is forbidden, the transverse equilibrium structure controls the transport laws and can qualitatively reshape them. Starting from the Brownian dynamics in the full confined geometry, we derive an exact large-scale one-dimensional fluctuating hydrodynamics for the longitudinal density, whose coefficients are fixed by the confined equilibrium equation of state. In the minimal hard-core setting, this yields a collective diffusivity that can become non-monotonic in density. This geometric anomaly propagates to exact large-scale predictions for integrated-current fluctuations, tracer displacement fluctuations and the associated density profiles. The effect is robust to the interaction potential, channel geometry, initial preparation and microscopic dynamics. Quasi-one-dimensional single-file transport therefore defines a distinct regime in which forbidding overtaking does not erase geometry from collective transport.

</details>


### [138] [Extensible links in a broad class of single polymer chain models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11041)
*Michael R. Buche,Matthew J. Grasinger,Jason P. Mulderrig*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种普适的渐近理论（asymptotic theory），用于在离散单链热力学模型中引入键的可扩展性（link extensibility），弥补了现有模型缺乏系统推导的空白；该理论在自由连接链（freely jointed chain）中得到了解析验证，在自由旋转链（freely rotating chain）中得到了数值验证，近似精度为逆键刚度的—阶，误差呈二次方递减。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有聚合物单链模型大多由离散序列的键节（links）构成，虽已有很多可扩展变体被提出，但缺乏一般性的普适理论；且大多数处理方法基于启发式而非系统严格的推导。本文旨在填补这一关键空白（critical gap）。

Method: 发展了一个普适的渐近理论（asymptotic theory），用于在广泛类别的离散单链热力学模型中纳入键的可扩展性（link extensibility）；该近似在逆键刚度（inverse link stiffness）上达到一阶精度（first-order accurate），误差呈二次方递减（quadratically decreasing error），并可从单一的刚性键参考计算恢复所有键刚度下的可扩展行为。

Result: 利用自由连接链（freely jointed chain）进行了解析验证，利用自由旋转链（freely rotating chain）进行了数值验证。

Conclusion: 该渐近理论成功实现了对离散单链模型中键节可扩展性的系统、严格推导，提供了一种一般性框架，在保持计算简便性的同时兼具普适性。

Abstract: The physics of polymer chains is often probed using molecular stretching experiments and various idealized single-chain models. The majority of these models consist of a discrete sequence of links, which may be treated as rigid or extensible. Although such models are well established and many specific extensible variants have been proposed, no generally applicable theory has been presented. Moreover, most existing treatments are heuristic rather than systematically and rigorously derived. This critical gap is closed here through the development of a generally applicable asymptotic theory for including link extensibility in a broad class of discrete models for single-chain thermodynamics. The theory is verified analytically using the freely jointed chain and validated numerically using the freely rotating chain. The resulting approximation is first-order accurate in inverse link stiffness, with quadratically decreasing error, and recovers extensible behavior across all link stiffnesses from a single rigid-link reference calculation.

</details>

### [139] [Combined Analysis of Lattice QCD and Experimental Data on the Pion Transition Form Factor](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11181)
*Franziska Hagelstein,Danaheb Naomi Navarro Durán,Timon Esser,Vadim Lensky,Sotiris Pitelis,Vladyslava Sharkovska*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种结合格点量子色动力学（lattice QCD, LQCD）与实验数据的全局单阶段拟合方法，用于精确确定π介子跃迁形状因子（pion transition form factor, TFF），并评估其对μ子反常磁矩中强子轻子-轻子散射贡献的影响。研究表明，引入实验数据可将单虚顶点处不确定性降低至原来的三分之一，而μ子g−2中π介子极点贡献的不确定性改善约1.5倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 精确计算μ子反常磁矩（muon anomalous magnetic moment）中强子轻子-轻子散射（hadronic light-by-light scattering）贡献需要π介子跃迁形状因子（pion transition form factor, TFF）的高精度信息。现有方法中，格点量子色动力学（lattice QCD, LQCD）和e⁺e⁻散射实验各自在不同运动学区域具有优势，但尚未实现两者的严格统计结合。

Method: 采用全局单阶段拟合（global one-stage fitting approach），基于修正的z展开（modified $z$-expansion）方法；通过合成刀切复制抽样（synthetic jackknife replicate sampling）和归一化χ²加权方案（normalized $χ^2$ weighting scheme）实现LQCD与实验数据的统计严谨融合。

Result: 结合实验数据后，单虚顶点（singly-virtual limit）处π介子TFF的不确定性降至原来的三分之一；μ子g−2中π介子极点贡献（pion-pole contribution）的不确定性改善约1.5倍。

Conclusion: 实验数据的引入能显著收紧π介子TFF的约束，但对μ子g−2的改善相对温和，原因在于g−2积分主导来自低Q²区域，而该区域已由物理归一化约束（physical normalization constraints）充分限定。

Abstract: The evaluation of the hadronic light-by-light scattering contribution to the muon anomalous magnetic moment requires precise knowledge of the pion transition form factor (TFF). In this work, we present a feasibility study for a combined analysis of lattice QCD (LQCD) and experimental data. Our methodology is driven by the goal of combining complementary datasets to leverage their respective kinematic advantages: while LQCD provides robust predictions for the doubly-virtual TFF, $e^+e^-$ scattering experiments offer high-precision singly-virtual measurements up to large momentum transfers. To ensure a statistically rigorous combination, we implement a global one-stage fitting approach based on the modified $z$-expansion, utilizing synthetic jackknife replicate sampling and a normalized $χ^2$ weighting scheme. We demonstrate that the inclusion of experimental data substantially tightens the constraints on the pion TFF, yielding up to a factor of three reduction in uncertainty in the singly-virtual limit. In contrast, the uncertainty of the resulting pion-pole contribution to the muon $g-2$ improves by a factor of $1.5$. This more modest improvement reflects the fact that the $g-2$ integral is heavily dominated by the low-$Q^2$ region, which is already well constrained by physical normalization constraints.

</details>


### [140] [Tame the Umklapp Processes in Real-Time Lattice Simulation for Hydrodynamics: An Ising Field Theory Study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09984)
*Xiaojun Yao*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 本文通过格点哈密顿量模拟，计算了由三个稳定标量粒子组成的不可积伊辛场论中应力-能量张量的实时对称关联函数，发现Umklapp过程被抑制且长波长时间下涌现出相对论性流体力学声波模式，并非微扰地提取了体粘滞系数与熵密度之比及声速。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在非可积量子场论中，从微观动力学推导出流体力学行为（hydrodynamization）并计算输运系数（transport coefficients）仍是一个重要难题，需要发展非微扰的实时方法。

Method: 采用格点哈密顿量模拟（lattice Hamiltonian simulation），结合经典精确对角化（exact diagonalization）和矩阵乘积态张量网络（matrix product state tensor network）方法，对不可积伊辛场论（non-integrable Ising field theory）进行实时关联函数计算。

Result: 在格点理论的标度区（scaling region）内，Umklapp过程被抑制；长波长和晚时间下涌现出相对论性流体力学（relativistic hydrodynamics）的声波模式（sound modes）。提取的体粘滞系数与熵密度之比为 ζ/s=14.19±0.90，声速为 c_s/c=0.76±0.02（温度 T≈7.14，以最轻稳定粒子质量为单位）。

Conclusion: 该研究展示了实时格点哈密顿量模拟在描述流体力学化（hydrodynamization）和非微扰计算输运系数方面的有效性。

Abstract: We calculate the real-time symmetric correlation function of the stress-energy tensor for a non-integrable Ising field theory consisting of three stable scalar particles via lattice Hamiltonian simulation. Using classical exact diagonalization and the matrix product state tensor network methods, we find that in the scaling region of the lattice theory, Umklapp processes are suppressed and the sound modes of relativistic hydrodynamics emerge at long wavelength and late time. The extracted ratio of bulk viscosity to entropy density is $ζ/s=14.19\pm 0.90$ and the speed of sound is $c_s/c=0.76 \pm 0.02$ at the temperature $T\approx 7.14$ in units of the lowest stable particle's mass. Our study demonstrates the utility of real-time lattice Hamiltonian simulation for describing hydrodynamization and calculating transport coefficients nonperturbatively.

### [141] [The Scattering Algebra of Physical Space: Wigner-Covariance and Fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10082)
*Moab Croft,Neil Christensen*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文利用物理空间代数（APS）探讨构造性标准模型（CSM）中的Wigner协变性与自旋/螺旋度场，推导了Lorentz旋量的Wigner协变性，给出了自旋-1/2与自旋-1的构造性场，并建立了与量子信息的桥梁；但无质量情形与自旋-1场的对应关系尚不完全，且发现的反对易拉格朗日量密度项暗示了仍需进一步研究的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在前期工作基础上，利用物理空间代数（Algebra of Physical Space, APS）进一步探索构造性标准模型（Constructive Standard Model, CSM）中的Wigner协变性（Wigner-covariance）与自旋/螺旋度（spin/helicity）场结构，旨在为粒子物理标准模型提供更几何化、矩阵无关（matrix-free）且坐标无关（coordinate-free）的表述。

Method: 采用APS中的旋量形式论（spinor formalism）显式推导Lorentz旋量（Lorentz spinors）的Wigner协变性；通过散射代数（Scattering Algebra, SA）证明与CSM的等价性；利用APS给出自旋-1/2和自旋-1的构造性场（constructive fields），并给出实现Wigner协变性所需的映射关系。

Result: APS的自旋-1/2场与CSM中的自旋-1/2场等价，APS的自旋场形式等价于Pauli旋量（Pauli spinors），从而建立了CSM与量子信息（Quantum Information）研究之间的新桥梁。但无质量情形（massless cases）因各种复杂性尚无法在SA框架中处理；自旋-1场的SA对应偏离了CSM原先提出的自旋-1场形式。利用hff（Higgs与两个有质量费米子）拉格朗日量密度导出了首个纯用APS定义的构造性散射振幅，但该结果导致了一个反厄米（anti-Hermitian）作用量项。

Conclusion: 几何代数（Geometric Algebra）在本研究中展现出强大的阐释力：所有物理量均可获得几何解释，且推导可完全在矩阵无关与坐标无关的方式下完成。但无质量情形及自旋-1场在SA中的对应仍存在问题，需要进一步工作加以完善。反厄米作用量项的发现经由传统CSM技术确认，提示了构造性方法中尚存未解问题。

Abstract: Following previous work, the Algebra of Physical Space (APS) is used to explore Wigner-covariance and spin/helicity fields within the Constructive Standard Model (CSM) of Particle Physics. The spinor formalism of the APS is used to derive explicit Wigner-covariance of Lorentz spinors, and equivalencies with the CSM are demonstrated via the Scattering Algebra (SA). Constructive fields for spin-1/2 and spin-1 are given in the APS and the necessary maps for Wigner-covariance are proposed. The forms of these spin fields are equivalent to Pauli spinors, thereby serving as a new bridge between the CSM and the study of Quantum Information. It is further seen that spin-1/2 fields of the APS are equivalent to the spin-1/2 fields in the CSM, but the massless cases cannot yet be handled within the SA due to various complications. Similarly, while spin-1 fields exist inside the APS, their SA equivalents deviate from the originally proposed spin-1 fields of the CSM; so further work is needed to prove correspondence between spin-1 fields of the APS and the CSM. Sample Lagrangian densities of the CSM are analyzed using the methods herein, are given geometric interpretations, and are connected to traditional Pauli Theory. Finally, the hff (Higgs and two massive fermions) Lagrangian density is used to determine the first constructive scattering amplitude that is defined purely in terms of the APS. Concerningly, this leads to an anti-Hermitian action term, and this surprise is later confirmed using traditional CSM techniques. Throughout this paper, the illuminating power of Geometric Algebra is clear: Everything has a geometric interpretation, and results can be accomplished matrix-free as well as coordinate-free.

</details>


### [142] [Doubly-strange hidden-charm pentaquarks from the Fermi statistics of the light-quark cloud](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10122)
*Halil Mutuk*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文将重子-粲偶素图像（baryo-charmonium picture）推广到双奇异扇区 $c\bar c ssq$，通过色魔互动标度（chromomagnetic scaling）和奇异质量增量，预测了两个负宇称三重态，其中高能态形成接近简并的双重态，这一稀疏的固定间距模式将本方案与分子图像（molecular picture）和双夸克图像（diquark picture）区分开来。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将五夸克态（pentaquarks）的重子-粲偶素图像从单奇异扇区拓展到双奇异扇区 $c\bar c ssq$，以检验该框架的普适性并给出可实验检验的新预言。

Method: 质量劈裂完全由轻云（light cloud）决定，新输入量仅为奇异-奇异耦合 $J^{ss}$（通过色魔互动标度（chromomagnetic scaling）确定）和一个加性奇异质量增量（additive strange-mass increment，取自观测到的 $P_c\!\to\!P_{cs}$ 位移）。

Result: 获得两个负宇称三重态：与介子（kaon）关联的最低 $\tfrac12^-$ 态位于约 4.60 GeV，与反质子（antiproton）关联的三重态低约 120 MeV。高能两个与介子关联的态形成近简并双重态（near-degenerate doublet），与轻扇区中分离良好的三重态形成鲜明对比。

Conclusion: 内部劈裂无需调整，直接由实测的 $P_c$ 和 $P_{cs}$ 谱确定；绝对标度依赖于加性奇异质量假设（additive strange-mass ansatz），这是外推的主要假定。预言质量与近期分子耦合道（molecular coupled-channel）和QCD求和规则（QCD sum-rule）结果一致。

Abstract: We extend the baryo-charmonium picture of pentaquarks -- a color-octet $c\bar c$ core bonded to a color-octet light-quark cloud -- to the doubly-strange sector $c\bar c ssq$. The mass splittings are set entirely by the light cloud, so the only new inputs are the strange-strange couplings $J^{ss}$, fixed by a second application of the chromomagnetic scaling, and an additive strange-mass increment taken from the observed $P_c\!\to\!P_{cs}$ shift. We obtain two negative-parity triplets, one produced with a kaon and one with an antiproton, the lowest kaon-associated $\tfrac12^-$ state near $4.60$~GeV and the antiproton-associated triplet some $120$~MeV below. The robust, distinctive prediction is that the upper two kaon-associated states form a near-degenerate doublet, in sharp contrast to the well-separated triplets of the lighter sectors -- a sparse, fixed-spacing pattern that sets the scheme apart from the molecular and diquark alternatives. The internal splittings follow without adjustment from the measured $P_c$ and $P_{cs}$ spectra; the absolute scale relies on the additive strange-mass ansatz, the main assumption of the extrapolation. The predicted masses agree with recent molecular coupled-channel and QCD sum-rule results.

Abstract: Instantons are non-perturbative classical solutions which describe transitions between different QCD vacua. They have never been observed experimentally. We consider the signatures of the instanton (sphaleron) production events and the main QCD backgrounds. Method: 论文从超对称/超引力（SUSY/SUGRA）模量出发，推导该模量到有效原子干涉耦合的映射关系，将原子相位振荡与规范动能函数、Kähler度规、Yukawa耦合、希格斯扇区参数及QCD标度（QCD scale）沿隐藏扇区轻方向（light hidden sector direction）的导数相关联。

Abstract: Atomic interferometry provides a sensitive near Earth probe of high energy physics through precision measurements of quantum phase. In this Letter, we point out that MAGIS and AION like long-baseline atom interferometers can also be used to test supersymmetric hidden sectors, if these sectors contain ultralight moduli, dilatons or hidden scalars that induce coherent phase oscillations. In such a setup, the measured atomic phase does not only constrain an effective phenomenological scalar coupling. It can be related to derivatives of supersymmetric gauge kinetic functions, Kähler metrics, Yukawa couplings, Higgs sector parameters and the QCD scale along light hidden sector directions. We derive the mapping from a generic SUSY/SUGRA modulus to the effective atom interferometric coupling, and show that future phase sensitivities may probe very small visible sector admixtures of otherwise hidden fields. This identifies MAGIS/AION type experiments as non-collider probes of supersymmetric and string-motivated infrared relics, complementary to gravitational wave, astrophysical and collider searches.

### [145] [Matrix element method at NLO: A fine proof of concept in POWHEG](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11083)
*Ulrich Haisch,Jakob Linder,Luc Schnell,Marius Wiesemann,Giulia Zanderighi*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出利用POWHEG方法将矩阵元方法（MEM）扩展至QCD次领头阶（NLO），通过将真实辐射事件投影到Born运动学，成功实现了NLO精度的MEM，并在全轻子W+W-产生过程中验证了其作为近最优分类器区分标准模型与超出标准模型信号的能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 矩阵元方法（MEM）在领头阶（leading-order）已广泛应用，但将其推广到QCD次领头阶（next-to-leading order, NLO）面临红外发散、负权重、额外末态部分子及高维相空间积分等挑战，亟需一种实用路径来实现NLO精度的MEM。

Method: 利用POWHEG方法，通过源自B̃(Φ)函数的映射（mapping），将真实辐射（real-emission）事件投影到Born运动学（Born kinematics）上，从而在保留NLO精度归一化的前提下，一致性地包含最硬QCD辐射。

Result: 以标准模型有效场论（SM effective field theory）中的全轻子W+W-产生过程为概念验证，聚焦于一个CP守恒的维度六三规范玻色子算符。结果表明，该NLO MEM实现可作为近最优分类器（near-optimal classifier），利用末态轻子间自旋与极化相关的关联，高效区分超出标准模型（beyond-the-SM, BSM）事件与标准模型事件。

Conclusion: NLO精度的MEM在电弱过程的精确研究以及微弱BSM效应的探测中展现出重要潜力。

Abstract: The matrix element method (MEM) provides a fully probabilistic approach to confront experimental events with theory, retaining all correlations in the scattering matrix element. While leading-order MEM is widely used and automated, extending it to next-to-leading order (NLO) in QCD is challenging due to infrared divergences, negative weights, extra final-state partons, and multi-dimensional phase-space integration. We demonstrate that the POWHEG method offers a practical path to MEM at NLO accuracy. By projecting real-emission events onto Born kinematics via the mappings inherited from the $\tilde{B} (Φ)$ function, our method consistently includes the hardest QCD radiation while preserving the NLO-accurate normalization. As a proof of concept, we apply it to fully leptonic $W^+ W^-$ production in the Standard Model (SM) effective field theory, focusing on a CP-even dimension-six triple-gauge-boson operator. Our NLO MEM implementation acts as a near-optimal classifier, exploiting spin- and polarization-dependent correlations among the final-state leptons to efficiently distinguish beyond-the-SM (BSM) from SM events. This demonstrates the potential of MEM at NLO for precision studies of electroweak processes and subtle BSM effects.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 现有射电望远镜（如CHIME和FAST）在探测原初黑洞（primordial black hole, PBH）合并——这一最现实的瞬态HFGW源——方面，性能显著优于许多现有实验；同时，它们对单色HFGW发射源（如PBH周围的超辐射形成的超轻玻色子云）也具有独特灵敏度。

Abstract: High-frequency gravitational waves (HFGWs) in the MHz to GHz regime can convert into radio photons in the presence of astrophysical magnetic fields through the inverse Gertsenshtein effect. We show that existing radio telescopes like CHIME and FAST are excellent tools for detecting HFGW sources, significantly outperforming many existing experiments at detecting primordial black hole (PBH) mergers, the most realistic sources of transient HFGWs. Radio telescopes are also uniquely sensitive to sources of monochromatic HFGW emission, such as ultralight boson clouds formed through superradiance around PBHs, and are likely to have excellent sensitivity to generic sources of detectable HFGWs.

### [147] [Efficient AI-Inspired Reduction of Feynman Integrals via Tube Seeding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10698)
*Justin Berman,Francois Charton,Andres Luna,Matthias Wilhelm,Mao Zeng*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文利用机器学习发现了一种新的种子积分选取策略（tube seeding），用于费曼积分（Feynman integrals）的“分部积分归约”（integration-by-parts reduction）。该策略将种子数目随分子幂次的增长从多项式级降为线性级，成功归约了传统 Laporta 算法难以处理的非平面 2 圈 5 点秩 20 积分，并在完整的高秩积分组归约中显著降低了时间和内存开销。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在理论粒子物理和引力波物理的最新计算中，费曼积分的“分部积分归约”（integration-by-parts reduction）是常见瓶颈。现有的种子选取策略会导致种子数目随着分子幂次（numerator power）呈多项式增长，限制了高秩（high-rank）多圈积分（multi-loop integrals）的处理能力。

Method: 使用机器学习（machine learning）发现一种新的种子积分（seed integrals）选取策略——tube seeding，将种子限制在一个连接目标积分（target integral）与主积分（master integrals）的“薄管状区域”（thin tube-like region）内，路径呈“之”字形（zigzag path）。该策略仅需在标准 Laporta 算法（Laporta algorithm）基础上做稀疏种子选取，种子数目随分子幂次呈线性增长。

Result: 成功归约了非平面 2 圈 5 点（non-planar 2-loop 5-point）秩 20（rank 20）积分（在有限域数值运动学下），这是传统 Laporta 算法难以完成的。进一步归约了一组完整的顶层秩 10（top-level rank-10）积分，通过将目标积分划分为若干区块（chunk），每个区块均可由该策略显著降低时间和内存开销。

Conclusion: 本策略使高秩多圈积分的归约在时间和内存上大幅优于现有方法，适用于唯象学（phenomenological）应用。作者已在 GitHub 上提供了概念验证实现（proof-of-principle implementation）。

Abstract: In this paper, we use machine learning to discover a new seeding strategy for integration-by-parts reduction of Feynman integrals, which is a frequent bottleneck in state-of-the-art calculations in theoretical particle and gravitational-wave physics. Our strategy allows us to reduce multi-loop integrals with large numerator powers via essentially the standard Laporta algorithm but with a sparse selection of seed integrals that grows only linearly with the numerator power, whereas existing strategies lead to growth with a polynomial power that increases with the complexity of the integral being reduced. The seeds are restricted to a thin tube-like region that connects the target integral to the master integrals along a zigzag path. We demonstrate the power of our approach by reducing non-planar 2-loop 5-point integrals of rank 20 with numerical kinematics over a finite field, which is prohibitively difficult for the Laporta algorithm with conventional seeding. Going beyond individual integrals, we further demonstrate the reduction of a complete set of top-level rank-10 integrals by dividing the target integrals into several chunks, each of which can be solved by our sparse seeding strategy with considerably less time and a significantly lower memory footprint than other state-of-the-art strategies, making the approach well-suited for phenomenological applications. We provide a proof-of-principle implementation on GitHub at https://github.com/andreslunagodoy/tube_seeding.

</details>


### [148] [The Gravitational Form Factor of the Pion in Perturbative QCD with a Dilaton Interaction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10993)
*Claudio Corianò,Hsiang-nan Li,Dario Melle,Leonardo Torcellini*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文在QCD因子化框架下研究中大动量转移下的π介子引力形状因子（gravitational form factors, GFFs），重点分析了非阿贝尔TJJ关联子中编码的量子迹反常（trace anomaly）效应，并通过Sudakov重求和与高斯横向动量波函数模型处理软胶子端点发散，发现反常诱导的修正显著改变了π介子GFFs在高动量转移下的行为，并在迹扇区和D项上留下独特印记。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究π介子引力形状因子在中大动量转移区域的行为，特别是量子色动力学（QCD）中迹反常（trace anomaly）对硬散射核的贡献，以及如何从场论角度一致地分离夸克与胶子扇区。

Method: 在QCD因子化（QCD factorization）框架下分析非阿贝尔TJJ关联子，该关联子将局域QCD能量-动量张量与两个外胶子场耦合；通过Sudakov重求和（Sudakov resummation）框架结合高斯模型描述π介子的横向动量依赖波函数（transverse-momentum-dependent wave function），以调控硬核中的软胶子端点发散。

Result: 量子反常诱导出类似标量膨胀子（dilaton-like）的贡献到硬散射核；反常诱导的修正显著改变了π介子引力形状因子在高动量转移区域的行为，并在迹扇区（trace sector）和D项（D-term）上留下独特印记。

Conclusion: 迹反常对π介子引力形状因子在高动量转移区域具有不可忽略的影响，其效应可通过因子化方法结合Sudakov重求和得到可靠的唯象预测。

Abstract: We investigate the pion gravitational form factors (GFFs) at intermediate and large momentum transfer within the framework of QCD factorization. Our analysis centers on the non-Abelian $TJJ$ correlator, which couples the local QCD energy-momentum tensor to two external gluon fields and explicitly encodes the perturbative effects of the trace anomaly. We demonstrate how this quantum anomaly induces a scalar, dilaton-like contribution to the hard-scattering kernel. To ensure field-theoretic consistency, a careful separation of the quark and gluon sectors is performed, accounting for the modifications introduced by gauge-fixing terms and Slavnov-Taylor identities on the off-shell gluonic structure. To obtain realistic phenomenological predictions and regulate soft-gluon endpoint divergences in the hard kernel, we implement the Sudakov resummation framework coupled with a Gaussian model for the pion's transverse-momentum-dependent wave function. We show that the resulting anomaly-induced corrections significantly modify the behavior of the pion GFFs at large momentum transfer, leaving a unique imprint on the trace sector and the $D$-term.

</details>


### [149] [Revisiting Cherenkov radiation in anisotropic chiral matter: exact calculation reveals threshold-free emission](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10985)
*R. Martínez von Dossow,Luis F. Urrutia*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文在Carroll-Field-Jackiw电动力学框架下，研究各向异性手性物质中的切伦科夫辐射，推导了柱坐标下的偏振模式解析解与色散关系，揭示了零、一或两个切伦科夫锥的条件，并发现一种无需速度阈值即可在特定频率范围内产生切伦科夫辐射的新奇现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索各向异性手性物质（anisotropic chiral matter）中切伦科夫辐射（Cherenkov radiation）的完整理论描述，特别是在轴子角（axion angle）随空间位置线性变化的Carroll-Field-Jackiw电动力学框架下，揭示标准材料中不存在的新奇辐射行为。

Method: 在柱坐标（cylindrical coordinates）和空频域（space-frequency domain）中，推导电磁场偏振模式（polarization modes）的闭式解析表达式，求解修正的麦克斯韦方程组；通过在无穷远柱面施加出射波边界条件（outgoing wave boundary conditions）确保因果性，从而获得色散关系（dispersion relations）。

Result: 确定了允许零、一或两个切伦科夫锥（Cherenkov cones）的具体角度和频率范围；获得了所有情况下的辐射频谱能量分布（spectral energy distribution）。特别地，模型的一个扇区展现出无需阈值（threshold）的慢速电荷切伦科夫辐射，但仅限特定频率范围，这一行为在标准材料中不存在。此外，基于精确计算结果检验了先前基于格林函数（Green's function）的近似方法的可靠性。

Conclusion: 各向异性手性物质中的切伦科夫辐射展现出比标准介质更丰富的现象，包括无需速度阈值的慢电荷辐射，这为新型电磁辐射源和手性材料探测提供了潜在理论依据。同时，精确解为评估近似方法的有效性建立了基准。

Abstract: We explore Cherenkov radiation in anisotropic chiral matter within the framework of Carroll-Field-Jackiw electrodynamics, where the axion angle exhibits a linear dependence on position. By deriving closed-form expressions for the polarization modes of electromagnetic fields in cylindrical coordinates and the space-frequency domain, we solve the modified Maxwell's equations. To enforce causality, we impose outgoing wave boundary conditions at a cylindrical surface at infinity, which yields the dispersion relations. Our analysis uncovers the specific angles and frequency ranges that allow for zero, one, or two Cherenkov cones. We also obtain the spectral energy distribution of the radiation in all cases. Notably, one sector of the model exhibits a novel phenomenon: Cherenkov radiation can be generated by slowly moving charges without a threshold, but only within a specific frequency range. This behavior is not observed in standard materials. Using our exact calculations, we also investigate the reliability of an approximate method previously proposed based on the calculation of the Green's function for the system.

</details>

### [150] [Exactly solvable non-planar $\mathbb{Z}_{2}$ dimer liquids on checkerboard and ruby lattices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10003)
*Julia Wildeboer,Zohar Nussinov,Thomas Iadecola,Alexander Seidel*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文将具有对偶伊辛规范理论描述的可精确求解量子二聚体模型从三价母格推广到四价母格，引入交叉-中间（crossed-medial）晶格上的新模型，其特征是存在交叉面元和非平面过渡图。作为最简单的实现，提出了棋盘晶格上的可精确求解量子二聚体模型，可精确映射到环面码（toric code），从而建立了后者与安德森短程共振价键（resonating valence bond, RVB）范式之间的直接联系。此外，将Kasteleyn方法扩展至相关非平面图，实现了在保持关联函数高效计算的同时，对哈密顿量进行可控变形。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有可精确求解的量子二聚体模型主要建立在三价母格上，而四价格点上的构造尚未被系统探索；同时，非平面结构（如交叉环）的介入使得传统解析方法失效，亟需建立新的理论框架。

Method: 通过对偶伊辛规范理论（dual Ising gauge theory）将量子二聚体模型从三价母格推广到四价母格；在交叉-中间晶格上构造模型，引入交叉面元；将Kasteleyn方法扩展至非平面图，用于波函数可控变形。

Result: 建立了棋盘晶格上的可精确求解量子二聚体模型，并直接映射到环面码；提出了交叉红宝石晶格（crossed ruby lattice）构造，其对偶为kagome晶格上的伊辛规范理论；展示了一整类交叉-中间量子二聚体模型，可通过迭代生成级联的$\mathbb{Z}_{2}$拓扑二聚体液体。

Conclusion: 该推广框架突破了传统平面设定的限制，为研究非平面拓扑二聚体液体提供了新的解析工具；非平面Kasteleyn方法的引入则拓展了可计算变形的范围，有助于进一步理解拓扑序与共振价键态之间的联系。

Abstract: We generalize an influential framework for exactly solvable quantum dimer models with dual Ising gauge theory descriptions realizing the $\mathbb{Z}_{2}$ topological phase from trivalent to tetravalent parent lattices. The resulting quantum dimer models live on crossed-medial lattices and possess the remarkable feature of having crossed plaquettes, leading to transition graphs with generically intersecting loops. This non-planar structure runs counter to established templates for analytically tractable dimer liquids. As the simplest realization of the construction, we introduce an exactly solvable quantum dimer model on the checkerboard lattice that allows an exact mapping to the toric code, thus providing a particularly direct connection between the latter and Anderson's short range resonating valence bond paradigm. We further show that a corresponding crossed ruby lattice construction, dual to an Ising gauge theory on the kagome lattice, naturally falls within the same framework. More generally, the construction gives rise to a broad class of exactly solvable crossed-medial quantum dimer models and admits natural iteration, generating cascades of solvable $\mathbb{Z}_{2}$ topological dimer liquids beyond the standard planar setting. We furthermore extend Kasteleyn methods to the relevant non-planar graphs, enabling controlled wave-function deformations away from the commuting-projector points while retaining efficient evaluation of correlation functions.

Result: 极化中子衍射成功映射了Dy³⁺的磁化率张量，直接探测到环向磁矩（toroidal moment）；变场中子衍射显示沿c轴的场致磁化，且环向磁矩呈反平行堆叠，提供了环向磁矩的确凿证据；磁测量证实了基态为环向态（toroidal ground state）。

Conclusion: 首次将极化中子衍射、变场中子衍射、从头计算和磁测量联合使用，建立了一套稳健、定量的分子尺度环向磁性（molecular-scale toroidal magnetism）探测方法。该综合方法克服了此前间接方法的局限性，为研究单分子环磁（SMTs）确立了基准框架，并为分子量子材料的设计提供了重要见解。

Abstract: Single-molecule toroics (SMTs) offer a unique platform for next-generation quantum devices utilizing head-to-tail spin alignments in the compounds. Presence of toroidal moments in SMTs has been essentially based on magnetometry and ab initio calculations. Here, we report observation and probe of the toroidal moment in [Dy3(OH)(teaH2)3(paa)3]Cl(OMe) [teaH3: triethanolamine; paaH: N-(2-pyridyl)-acetoacetamide] from mapping of Dy3+ magnetic susceptibility tensors by polarized neutron diffraction (PND). Neutron diffraction under variable magnetic fields demonstrates field-induced magnetization along the c-axis with toroidal moments anti-parallelly stacked, providing definite proof of the toroidal moment. Magnetometry studies confirm the toroidal ground state. For the first time, the combined use of PND, variable-field neutron diffraction, ab initio calculations, and magnetometry is introduced as a robust and quantitative methodology to probe molecular-scale toroidal magnetism. This integrated approach overcomes limitations of earlier indirect methods, establishes a benchmark framework for investigating SMTs, and provides valuable insights for the design of molecular quantum materials.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在DFT和DFT+DMFT两个层次上计算总能量随晶格常数的变化，并引入由声子态密度导出的振动自由能；采用基于主成分分析的机器学习方法，从有限的第一性原理计算结果连续插值出声子色散。

Conclusion: 同时考虑电子熵与振动熵对于准确评估镧系体系的相稳定性至关重要，动态多体关联效应不可忽略。

Abstract: We investigate the thermodynamic properties of elemental cerium by assessing the crucial role of phonon free energy within the framework of dynamical mean-field theory (DMFT). While conventional density functional theory (DFT) often fails to capture the intricate energy landscape of $f$-electron materials, our approach integrates many-body electronic correlations with lattice dynamics to achieve a more rigorous description of the equation of state. We calculate the total energy as a function of the lattice constant at both the DFT and DFT+DMFT levels, subsequently incorporating the vibrational free energy derived from the phonon density of states. Our findings reveal that electronic renormalisation of the force constants significantly alters the phonon spectra, particularly in the strongly correlated $γ$-phase. By applying these phonon corrections to the energy profiles, we observe a substantial refinement in the predicted equilibrium volumes. Using principal-component-based machine learning, we interpolate phonon dispersions continuously from a finite set of first-principles calculations and compare them to experiment, finding significantly closer agreement compared to conventional DFT and DFT+U calculations that neglect dynamical many-body correlations. This study underlines the necessity of accounting for both electronic and vibrational entropy when evaluating the phase stability and structural transitions of lanthanide systems under varying pressures and temperatures.

Conclusion: 该工作为在强关联体系中实现非阿贝尔任意子的相干控制提供了原理性验证，开辟了超越传统自由费米子平台的拓扑量子操控新途径。

Abstract: We study coherent manipulation of Majorana zero modes emerging in overscreened two-channel Kondo systems. In particular, we identify a distinction between non-topological and genuinely topological Y-junction geometries, the latter realizing a non-Abelian geometric holonomy. ### [154] [Improved selector behavior in ultrathin chromium-doped V$_2$O$_3$ films](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10397)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过电学测量（electrical measurements）研究不同厚度薄膜的开关效应；采用透射电子显微镜（transmission electron microscopy）观察微观结构；利用元素映射（elemental mapping）分析铬掺杂剂分布及电极元素的扩散情况。

Result: 开关效应在薄膜厚度低至5 nm时仍能维持，且泄漏电流（leakage current）低、转变更陡峭；在如此薄的情况下，结晶膜（crystalline films）与非晶膜（amorphous films）的行为变得非常相似，且两者均需要形成步骤（forming step）。TiN电极界面处出现一层薄的非晶层；铬掺杂剂分布复杂，且Ti从电极扩散进入薄膜层。

Conclusion: 界面处非晶层的形成以及Ti的扩散可能是导致极薄膜性能改善的原因，这为基于负微分电阻效应的超薄器件在存储和神经形态应用中的可行性提供了依据。

Abstract: Devices based on the negative differential resistance effect in chromium doped V$_2$O$_3$ are considered to be promising as selector elements for use in emerging memory technologies, as well as for neuromorphic applications. It is shown by electrical measurements, that the switching effect is maintained for very thin films down to 5 nm, and even improved properties such as a low leakage current and an abrupt transition are observed. For these thicknesses, the behavior of crystalline and amorphous films becomes very similar; most strikingly, a forming step is required in both. Transmission electron microscopy reveals this to be likely due to a thin amorphous layer that forms at the interface to the TiN electrode. Elemental mapping further shows a complex distribution of the chromium dopants, as well as a diffusion of Ti into the layer from the electrode, which might be responsible for the improved properties.

### [155] [Antiferromagnetic order and magnetic polarons in lightly doped Li$_x$CoO$_2$ (x $\sim$ 0.9)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10419)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用体磁化率（bulk magnetization）、比热（specific heat）、核磁共振（nuclear magnetic resonance, NMR）和电子顺磁共振（electron paramagnetic resonance, EPR）光谱等多种测量手段，分别从宏观响应和微观自旋角度进行表征。

Result: 宏观测量显示该化合物在T_N~10 K以下部分发生反铁磁（antiferromagnetic）转变；同时观察到弱铁磁（ferromagnetic）响应，在低温低场下产生磁化历史依赖性，且在室温以上仍存在。EPR测量中仅有部分自旋贡献，其强度随温度变化表现为类居里顺磁（Curie-like paramagnetic）行为。

Conclusion: 提出高温下存在由掺杂空穴形成的磁极化子（magnetic polarons）导致的铁磁团簇；EPR谱的温度变化可用磁极化子的扩散（diffusion of magnetic polarons）框架解释。

Abstract: We investigate the magnetic properties of Li$_x$CoO$_2$ (x$\sim$0.9) using bulk magnetization, specific heat, nuclear magnetic resonance (NMR) and electron paramagnetic resonance (EPR) spectroscopy measurements. The dc magnetization, specific heat and NMR measurements, which probe the macroscopic response, indeed show that this compound partially undergoes an antiferromagnetic transition below $T_N \sim$ 10 K. In addition, we observed a weak ferromagnetic response, which gives rise to the history dependence in magnetization measurements at low fields and is observed at temperatures above room temperature. We propose that there are ferromagnetic clusters at high temperatures due to the formation of magnetic polarons out of doped holes. In EPR measurements performed at the $X$-band frequency, only a fraction of the total spins contribute and show Curie-like paramagnetic behavior as reflected in the temperature dependence of the EPR intensity. The temperature variation of the EPR spectra can be understood in the framework of the diffusion of magnetic polarons.

</details>

Conclusion: 上述行为与时间反演对称性破缺的超莫尔陈镶嵌（supermoiré Chern mosaic）模型一致，霍尔响应源自松弛结构中相反陈特性的局域畴的非抵消贡献。强磁场下的态则表明场重构的拓扑微带及畴界散射。这些结果确立了松弛超莫尔半导体三层体系为研究超越双层极限的空间有序磁性及拓扑的平台。

Abstract: Helically twisted multilayers offer access to moiré physics beyond the single-superlattice paradigm, yet their correlated and topological transport properties remain largely unexplored in semiconductor moiré materials. Here we report magnetotransport measurements of helical trilayer WSe2, in which two coupled moiré patterns relax into a supermoiré landscape composed of inequivalent local topological domains with distinct electronic structures and unequal spatial areas. By electrostatic tuning, we identify a trilayer-hybridized regime where interactions and real-space reconstruction combine to generate a plethora of magnetic and topological states absent in the twisted bilayers. At moiré filling factor $ν$ = -1, we observe a ferromagnetic insulating state that is robust against magnetic field and accompanied by a non-quantized anomalous Hall response ~-4 kOhms. This behaviour is consistent with a time-reversal-symmetry-breaking supermoiré Chern mosaic, in which the Hall response arises from the non-cancelling contributions of local domains with opposite Chern character arranged by the relaxed structure. Under strong magnetic fields, a symmetry-broken Chern insulating state (C = 1) emerges near $ν$ = -2/3, displaying a much larger positive Hall response together with strongly enhanced longitudinal resistance, suggestive of field-reconstructed topological minibands and domain-boundary scattering. These results establish relaxed supermoiré semiconductor trilayers as a platform for spatially organized magnetism and topology beyond the bilayer limit.

Abstract: Quantum-entangled states underpin many emergent phenomena in quantum materials, yet their direct experimental identification remains a challenge. ### [159] [Interaction-driven dynamics in graphene flakes as a benchmark for quantum simulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10548)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解有限石墨烯薄片中光学泵浦淬火后的超快弛豫动力学，并评估低阶多体过程在何种条件下足以描述弛豫，何种条件下需要高阶贡献。

Method: 在相互作用的紧束缚模型（interacting tight-binding model）中，将精确实时演化（exact real-time evolution）与限制在粒子-空穴激发子空间（particle-hole excitation subspaces）的模拟进行对比，并使用单粒子轨道熵诊断动态关联增长。

Result: 周期性石墨烯薄片可由低阶激发充分描述，而受限几何结构即使相互作用强度较小也需要大量高阶贡献。

Conclusion: 该淬火方案结合了简单的初态制备与强关联动力学，为未来量子计算（quantum computing）模拟提供了一个有前景的基准问题。

Abstract: We study interaction-driven ultrafast dynamics in finite graphene flakes following an optical pump quench in an interacting tight-binding model. By comparing exact real-time evolution with simulations restricted to particle-hole excitation subspaces, we assess when relaxation can be captured by low-order many-body processes and when this is not sufficient. The single-particle orbital entropy provides a compact diagnostic for dynamic correlation growth. For the systems studied here, periodic graphene flakes are well described by low-order excitations, whereas confined geometries require substantial higher-order contributions even for relatively small interaction strengths. The quench protocol combines simple initial-state preparation with strongly correlated dynamics, identifying a promising benchmark problem for future quantum-computing simulations.

### [160] [Propagation and localization of spin excitations at altermagnetic domain walls](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10604)
*Oksana Peschanska,Jeroen van den Brink,Volodymyr P. Kravchuk*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文研究了d波交错磁体（altermagnet）中沿畴壁（domain wall）传播的自旋本征激发，发现交错磁效应（altermagnetic effect）对束缚态（bound state）的影响强烈依赖于畴壁取向。沿[110]或[1̄10]方向时，会出现额外的有能隙束缚态并消除极化简并，且束缚态局域化程度随本征频率显著变化。外加静磁场会导致畴壁两侧局域区域的不对称性，并对传播波矢的绝对值设置上限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 交错磁体（altermagnet, AℓM）对畴壁性质有显著影响，因此自然预期其也会丰富畴壁上磁激发（magnetic excitation）的物理。本文旨在系统地研究沿易轴d波交错磁体中畴壁上的自旋本征激发传播行为。

Method: 本文采用理论分析的方法，计算了易轴d波交错磁体中沿不同取向畴壁传播的自旋本征激发，并考察了外加静磁场沿易轴方向施加时的影响。

Result: 沿节线方向[100]或[010]时，交错磁效应不改变束缚态数量，但导致非线性色散（dispersion）和波前倾斜（tilt of the wavefront）。沿[110]或[1̄10]方向时，交错磁效应最强，表现为：(i) 出现额外有能隙束缚态；(ii) 极化简并被移除；(iii) 局域化长度强烈依赖于本征频率。外加磁场在畴壁两侧诱导局域区域的不对称性，并对传播波矢绝对值设置上限。

Conclusion: 交错磁效应与畴壁取向的耦合可以调控自旋波束缚态的存在性、能隙、极化简并以及局域化程度，外加磁场提供了额外的调控自由度。这些发现为交错磁体中的磁激发工程提供了理论依据。

Abstract: Altermagnets (A$\ell$Ms) are spin-compensated materials in which opposite-spin sublattices are connected by a symmetry that causes a spin splitting in their elementary excitations. As there is a strong effect of altermagnetism on domain wall properties, it is quite natural to also expect an enrichment of the physics of magnetic excitations at A$\ell$M domain walls. Here, we consider the propagation of spin eigen-excitations along domain walls in easy-axial $d$-wave A$\ell$Ms. Investigating the presence of bound states localized on a domain wall, we find that the effect of the A$\ell$M on the bound states strongly depends on the orientation of the domain wall relative to the crystallographic directions. If the domain wall is oriented along a nodal direction [100] or [010], A$\ell$M does not change the number of bound states; however, it leads to a nonlinear dispersion and a tilt of the wavefront. The effect of A$\ell$M is strongest when the domain wall is oriented along the directions [110] or [$\bar{1}$10], i.e., along the directions of the strongest A$\ell$M splitting in the magnon spectrum. In this case, (i) the additional gapped bound states appear, (ii) degeneracy of the eigenstates with respect to their polarization (right-handed or left-handed precession of the N{é}el vector) is removed, and (iii) the localization area of the bound states strongly depends on the eigenfrequency. The latter may lead to strong localization of the bound state at the domain wall. We further consider the influence of a static magnetic field that is applied along the easy axis, and find that the magnetic field induces an asymmetry between the localization regions on opposite sides of the domain wall and sets an upper limit on the absolute value of the propagating eigenstate's wave vector.

### [161] [Nonequilibrium Green Functions Simulations for Large Correlated Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10773)
*Erik Schroedter,Michael Bonitz,Jan-Philip Joost*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为 δNEGF 的量子涨落形式化方法，用于非平衡格林函数（NEGF）的大规模时空相关模拟。该方法通过场算符乘积的涨落表示双时间关联，保持时间线性标度（O(N_t)），同时避免了双粒子格林函数的显式存储和数值不稳定性，将可模拟的基态规模从约 10^2 提升至约 10^4。在二维 Hubbard 晶格扩散和石墨烯纳米带异质结超快弛豫等应用中验证了其稳定性和可扩展性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的非平衡格林函数（NEGF）方法虽然能够保留双时间关联信息，但其计算复杂度随时间步数 N_t 呈三次方增长（O(N_t^3)）。后来提出的 G1–G2 方案虽然将标度降为线性（O(N_t)），但需要传播双粒子关联函数，存在数值不稳定性，且仅适用于基态规模 N_b ~ 10^2 的小系统。因此，亟待发展一种兼具线性标度、数值稳定且可扩展至大规模空间非均匀关联量子系统的方法。

Method: 提出量子涨落形式的非平衡格林函数方法（δNEGF），将动力学双粒子关联通过场算符乘积的涨落 δĜ 来表征，从而保证约化密度矩阵的正定性（positivity）以维持数值稳定。该方法避免了显式存储双粒子格林函数，将传播简化为有限系综的 Hartree–Fock 型轨迹，并结合关联函数的随机低秩分解（stochastic low-rank decomposition），实现时间线性标度（O(N_t)）。

Result: 在格点系统上，δNEGF 与精确结果及 HF-GKBA（Hartree-Fock 广义 Kadanoff–Baym 近似）结果进行比对，验证了其在强耦合条件下也能保持稳定的关联动力学。该方法将可模拟的基态规模从 N_b ~ 10^2 扩展到 N_b ~ 10^4。进一步成功演示了二维 Hubbard 晶格中的扩散过程以及具有长程库仑相互作用的石墨烯纳米带异质结中的超快弛豫现象。

Conclusion: δNEGF 为大规模、空间非均匀关联量子系统的动力学自能（dynamical self-energy）模拟提供了一条可扩展的路径，能够超越现有 NEGF 实现方法的适用范围。

Abstract: Correlated real-time dynamics in large, spatially inhomogeneous quantum systems remain difficult to access with nonequilibrium many-body methods. Two-time nonequilibrium Green functions (NEGF) retain dynamical correlations but their computational runtime grows cubically with the number of time steps $N_\mathrm{t}$. This scaling bottleneck could recently be overcome by introducing the G1--G2 scheme that is linear in $N_\mathrm{t}$, but requires propagation of a two-particle correlation function and may suffer from numerical instabilities. This has restricted simulations to small systems with $N_\mathrm{b} \sim 10^2$ basis states. Here we introduce a quantum-fluctuation formulation of nonequilibrium Green functions, denoted $δ$NEGF, that represents dynamical two-particle correlations through fluctuations of field-operator products, $δ\hat G$. This guarantees stable dynamics by preserving the positivity of the reduced density matrices, avoids the explicit storage of the two-particle Green function, and reduces the propagation to a finite ensemble of Hartree-Fock-like trajectories. Combined with a stochastic low-rank decomposition of the correlation functions, the method retains time-linear scaling while extending dynamical $GW$ and particle-particle and particle-hole $T$-matrix simulations to basis sizes of order $N_\mathrm{b}\sim 10^4$. We benchmark $δ$NEGF against exact and HF-GKBA results for lattice systems, finding stable correlated dynamics also at strong coupling. We further demonstrate large-scale simulations of diffusion in two-dimensional Hubbard lattices and ultrafast relaxation in graphene nanoribbon heterostructures with long-range Coulomb interactions. These results establish $δ$NEGF as a scalable route to dynamical self-energy simulations of large, spatially inhomogeneous correlated quantum systems beyond the reach of existing NEGF implementations.

</details>


### [162] [Fractional shot noise of an SU(N) Kondo system](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10814)
*Damian Krychowski,Stanisław Lipiński*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文利用Kotliar-Ruckenstein奴隶玻色子方法（SBMFA）和费米液体理论，研究了Kondo区多能级相互作用量子点（N-QD）的输运特性，重点分析了从线性到非线性的噪声行为，指出远离电子-空穴对称点时三体关联不可忽略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在Kondo区多能级相互作用量子点的强耦合输运中，非线性散粒噪声（shot noise）的高阶关联机制尚不清晰，特别是多体关联的贡献需要系统研究。

Method: 针对N能级Anderson模型，采用Kotliar-Ruckenstein奴隶玻色子方法（SBMFA）定义SU(N) Kondo系统的有效无相互作用准粒子（$N=2,3,4,5,6$）；利用Kondo共振透射系数描述准粒子分配的线性噪声；在强耦合区应用费米液体理论，将参数表达为SBMFA确定的赝费米子（pseudofermions）磁化率。

Result: 非线性散粒噪声由双准粒子散射主导；但在远离电子-空穴对称点（electron-hole symmetry point）的占据区域，三体关联（three-body correlations）的贡献必须被揭示。

Conclusion: 多体关联效应（尤其是三体关联）在远离对称性的占据区域内对非线性散粒噪声起关键作用，为理解Kondo区多能级量子点的高阶输运提供了理论依据。

Abstract: We consider transport through a multi-level interacting quantum dot (N-QD) in Kondo regime. Using the Kotliar-Ruckentein slave boson approach (SBMFA) for N-level Anderson model we define effectively noninteracting quasiparticles of the SU(N) Kondo system ($N=2,3,4,5,6$). Kondo resonance transmission coefficients determine linear noise describing quasiparticle partitioning. To discuss nonlinear conductance, susceptibilities and shot noise in the strong coupling regime, we apply Fermi liquid theory with parameters expressed by susceptibilities of pseudofermions determined within SBMFA. Nonlinear shot noise is dominated by two-quasiparticle scattering. However, we demonstrate that for occupation regions distant from the electron-hole symmetry point, the role of three-body correlations must be revealed.

</details>


### [163] [Thermal Signatures of the Slater-Mott Crossover in the Hubbard Model: From Double Occupancy to Antiferromagnetic Correlation Length](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10976)
*Mingzhong Lu,Yu-Feng Song,Youjin Deng,Yuan-Yao He*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究通过双占据数温度导数的符号变化，为Hubbard模型中从Slater绝缘体到Mott绝缘体的交叉提供了一个清晰、可实验操作的热力学判据，并利用精确对角化和量子蒙特卡洛模拟确定了二维正方晶格半填充情况下的交叉边界U_cross/t=4.0(2)。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在Hubbard模型的Néel有序基态中，相互作用驱动的从Slater绝缘体到Mott绝缘体的交叉是强关联电子体系的基本范式，但其定量表征长期以来一直难以实现。

Method: 利用双占据数的温度导数(∂D/∂T)_U在零温附近的符号变化作为热力学判据，并采用精确对角化（exact diagonalization）和数值精确的量子蒙特卡洛模拟（quantum Monte Carlo simulations）进行验证。

Result: 确定了半填充二维Hubbard模型中Slater-Mott交叉边界位于U_cross/t=4.0(2)；反铁磁关联长度的最大值独立地给出了一致的交叉边界；这两个热力学特征通过低温下热熵（thermal entropy）关于相互作用U的局部极小值在理论上得到统一。

Conclusion: 该研究提供了一个直接、可测量且物理直观的框架，可用于在光晶格实验（optical lattice experiments）中识别Slater-Mott交叉。

Abstract: The interaction-driven crossover from a Slater insulator to a Mott insulator in the Néel-ordered ground state of the Hubbard model is a fundamental paradigm of strongly correlated electrons, yet its quantitative characterization has remained elusive. Here we establish a clear and experimentally accessible thermal criterion for this crossover via the sign change of the temperature derivative of double occupancy, $(\partial D/\partial T)_U$, near zero temperature. In the Slater regime, $(\partial D/\partial T)_U>0$ reflects the major role of charge fluctuations; in the Mott regime, the anomalous $(\partial D/\partial T)_U<0$, a manifestation of the Pomeranchuk effect, signals the dominance of low-energy spin superexchange physics. Using exact diagonalization and {\it numerically exact} quantum Monte Carlo simulations, we demonstrate that this criterion determines the crossover boundary at $U_{\rm cross}/t=4.0(2)$ for the half-filled two-dimensional Hubbard model. Furthermore, we obtain a consistent boundary independently from the maximum in the antiferromagnetic correlation length, which also arises from the superexchange physics. These two thermal signatures are theoretically unified through the local minimum of thermal entropy versus interaction $U$ at low temperatures. Our results offer a direct, measurable, and physically intuitive framework to identify the Slater-Mott crossover in optical lattice experiments.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: A previously unreported triangular lattice (TL) antiferromagnet, TmZnGaO4, was synthesized as single crystals, and its crystal structure, magnetic susceptibilities, and specific heat were reported. Its crystal structure is isomorphic to that of the transverse-field Ising antiferromagnet TmMgGaO4, with Tm3+ ions located in the TLs, separated by a nonmagnetic bilayer composed mainly of Ga3+ and Zn2+ ions. The magnetic susceptibilities indicate the dominating antiferromagnetic interactions. The magnetization curves (M-H) exhibit strong easy-c-axis anisotropy, with a clear one-third magnetic plateau emerging, consistent with a field-induced up-up-down spin configuration. Instead of forming a conventional long-range magnetic order, the system exhibits two broad anomalies at 0.11 K and 2.81 K in zero-field specific heat measurements, highlighting the persistence of strong spin fluctuations and the potential for exotic quantum spin states. The above results reveal its future interest in exploring exotic quantum spin states in TmZnGaO4.

### [165] [Hybrid Hamiltonian-diagrammatic quantum impurity solver](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11095)
*Yang Yu,Gaurav Harsha,Lei Zhang,Agnieszka Jażdżewska,Dominika Zgid,Xinyang Dong,Emanuel Gull*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出一种结合哈密顿量方法与图解方法的混合策略来解决量子杂质模型（quantum impurity model）：通过添加一个小型辅助浴场（auxiliary bath），将剩余问题降阶到低阶微扰理论（low-order perturbation theory）高度精确且快速收敛的区域。在基准测试中，该混合方法在精度上超越粗线计算（bold-line calculations）数个数量级，并在存在严重符号问题（sign problem）的双轨道模型中以低三个数量级的计算成本达成收敛，同时在真实复杂问题中显著加速了向未知精确结果的收敛。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子杂质模型是强关联电子系统（strongly correlated electron systems）的核心模型，但其求解通常需要非微扰数值方法。基于哈密顿量的方法受限于少量浴场位点或小纠缠（small entanglement），而图解方法则面临符号问题、收敛缓慢或图解截断近似（diagram truncation approximations）等困难。因此，需要一种能融合两类方法优势的混合策略。

Method: 该方法将图解方法与一个小型辅助浴场相结合：通过显式浴场离散化（bath discretization）引入少量辅助态，使剩余问题的相互作用强度降低到低阶微扰理论高度精确且快速收敛的区域，从而以较低的计算代价获得高精度解。

Result: 在简单基准测试中，混合方法的精度超越粗线计算数个数量级；在存在严重符号问题的强相互作用双轨道模型中，以比竞争方法低三个数量级的计算成本达成收敛；在困难的实际问题中，向未知精确结果的收敛速度被显著加速。

Conclusion: 该混合方法为关联量子系统（correlated quantum systems）中高精度量子杂质求解建立了一条实用路径。

Abstract: Quantum impurity models, which describe the coupling between interacting orbitals and a non-interacting bath, play a central role in the physics of strongly correlated electron systems. Solving a quantum impurity model in general requires the use of non-perturbative numerical methods. Hamiltonian-based approaches, which rely on an explicit bath discretization, are typically limited to a small number of bath sites or small entanglement, and diagrammatic methods suffer from sign problems, slow convergence, or diagram truncation approximations. Here we show that these two classes of methods can be combined: augmenting diagrammatic methods with a small auxiliary bath can reduce the residual problem to a regime where low-order perturbation theory is highly accurate and rapidly converging. In a simple benchmark, the precision of the hybrid approach surpasses bold-line calculations by several orders of magnitude; for a strongly interacting two-orbital model with a severe sign problem, convergence is achieved at three orders of magnitude lower computational cost than competing methods; and convergence to the unknown exact result is rapidly accelerated in a difficult realistic problem. Our results establish a practical route to high-precision quantum impurity solutions in correlated quantum systems.
