### [166] [Generating functions for aggregation and fragmentation: review](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10785)
*S. A. Matveev*

Main category: math.DS

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 聚合与碎裂方程在多个物理体系中具有广泛应用，但获得其精确解析解通常十分困难。本文旨在系统回顾并发展生成函数技术，以在更广泛的物理区间（包括自发碎裂与碰撞碎裂）以及多种推广情形下获得这些方程的精确闭式解。

Method: 采用生成函数技术对离散的凝聚-碎裂方程进行解析求解；针对尺寸无关速率（size-independent rates）及单分散初始条件推导显式闭式解；将分析框架推广至连续方程、三粒子碰撞、D粒子碰撞及双组分体系等场景。

Result: 在离散情形下获得了若干显式闭式解；在连续、三粒子、D粒子碰撞及双组分推广情形下也得到精确解。源驱动聚合产生稳态分布，该分布服从普适的s^{-3/2}幂律（power-law）衰减，且截止质量（cutoff mass）按s_{*} ~ t^{2}标度增长。

Conclusion: 生成函数技术是一种有效的解析工具，能够在多种碎裂机制及初始条件下为聚合-碎裂方程提供精确解。源驱动聚合系统的稳态分布具有普适的幂律行为与标度关系，揭示了该体系的关键统计特征。

Abstract: In this work, we review and revisit the generating function techniques that provide exact analytical solutions for aggregation and fragmentation equations across several physical regimes including spontaneous and collisonal shattering. For discrete coagulation-fragmentation equations with size-independent rates under monodisperse initial conditions, we show the derivation of sevaral explicit closed-form solutions. We also briefly report the exact solutions for continuous, three-particle, $D$-particle collisions and two-component generalizations. Source-driven aggregation yields steady distributions featuring a universal $s^{-3/2}$ power-law decay and a cutoff mass scaling $s_{*} \sim t^{2}$.

### [167] [Collective drift and pinning in active rotator networks with Kuramoto coupling and mixed-sign feedback disorder](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10032)
*Arpan Dey*

Main category: nlin.AO

TL;DR: 本文研究了具有Kuramoto耦合的全连接活性转子（active rotator）网络，重点关注本地反馈强度（服从零均值高斯分布）与共同内在驱动之间的竞争。通过数值构建反馈-无序-耦合平面中的相图，发现弱耦合下反馈无序增强会抑制漂移，而强耦合可在反馈无序不太强时恢复正向漂移。混合符号的本地反馈即使在内禀驱动均匀的情况下，也能重塑钉扎与漂移之间的平衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 活性转子模型为可激发和振荡系统提供了最小相位描述，长期以来被用于研究相互牵引、同步和集体相变。本文旨在探讨在均匀内在驱动条件下，混合符号的本地反馈如何影响耦合活性转子网络中的钉扎（pinning）与漂移（drifting）之间的竞争关系。

Method: 采用全连接活性转子网络，耦合方式为Kuramoto耦合；本地反馈幅度取自零均值高斯分布，构成反馈无序。利用平均晚期漂移绝对值以及正、负漂移振子的比例，在反馈-无序-耦合参数平面中构建数值相图。同时分析了解析极限（无耦合和强耦合相干情况），并考察有限尺寸效应和零均值分布的内在频率。

Result: 弱耦合区域中，增大反馈无序强度会抑制漂移；强耦合条件下，当反馈无序不太强时，可恢复正向晚期漂移。这些结果通过无耦合和强耦合相干情况的解析极限得到了阐释。

Conclusion: 混合符号的本地反馈本身即可重塑耦合活性转子网络中钉扎与漂移之间的平衡，即使内在驱动（intrinsic drive）是均匀的，这一机制依然有效。

Abstract: Active rotator models provide a minimal phase description of excitable and oscillatory systems, and have long been used to study mutual entrainment, synchronization, and collective transitions. Here, we investigate fully connected active rotator networks with Kuramoto coupling, where a common intrinsic drive competes with local feedback amplitudes drawn from a zero-mean Gaussian distribution. This produces a competition between local pinning and collective phase alignment. Using mean absolute late-time drift and the fractions of positive and negative drifting oscillators, we construct numerical regime maps in the feedback-disorder-coupling plane. At weak coupling, increasing the feedback disorder strength suppresses drift, while stronger coupling can restore positive late-time drift when feedback disorder is not too strong. We interpret these regimes using analytical limits for the uncoupled and coherent strong-coupling cases. We also examine finite-size effects and zero-mean distributed intrinsic frequencies. Together, these results show that mixed-sign local feedback alone can reshape the balance between pinning and drifting in coupled active rotator networks, even when the intrinsic drive is homogeneous.

### [168] [Full-State and Reduced-Moment Encodings: A Representation-Level View of Equilibrium Quantum Many-Body Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11177)
*Nan Sheng*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过编码器-解码器框架（encoder-decoder framework）统一描述了平衡量子多体方法（equilibrium quantum many-body methods）中不同近似表示的本质差异，指出每种表示均可视为从可容许状态到所表示变量的编码映射，并在此基础上分析了变分原理、重建对应、泛函、核与闭包等结构如何用于补偿非单射编码器导致的信息损失。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有平衡量子多体方法不仅在近似程度上存在差异，而且在所显式表示的信息类型上也有所不同。本文旨在通过统一的编码器视角（encoder perspective）对这一根本性区别进行形式化表述，从而澄清不同方法之间的结构关系。

Method: 本文通过定义一个平衡规范（equilibrium specification），将每种表示形式视为从可容许状态到所表示变量的编码器（encoder）。恒等编码器（identity encoder）对应完整状态表示，非单射编码器（non-injective encoder）则生成约化表示，其变量值标记一个由兼容量子态构成的纤维（fiber of compatible states）。在此基础上，将变分原理、重建对应、泛函、核与闭包统一解释为用于选择、限制或逼近纤维内与任务相关内容的附加结构。

Result: 提出了一个精确解码器存在的条件：在某一状态类中，当且仅当任务在该类的编码器纤维上为常数时，才存在精确解码器。将静态矩（static moments）和虚时关联函数（imaginary-time correlation functions）统一为完整平衡读出泛函（complete equilibrium readout functional）在不同探针族（probe families）上的限制。量子嵌入（quantum embedding）可被理解为通过约化界面编码器（reduced interface encoders）及其共轭场（conjugate fields）实现的全局与局域描述之间的一致性（consistency）或替代（replacement）关系。

Conclusion: 该编码器框架为理解和比较不同平衡量子多体方法提供了一个统一的形式化语言，揭示了方法间差异的本质在于表示信息的编码方式，而非仅仅是近似程度的不同。

Abstract: Equilibrium quantum many-body methods differ not only in approximation, but in which information they represent explicitly. We formulate this distinction by fixing an equilibrium specification and viewing every representation as an encoder from admissible states to represented variables. The identity encoder gives a full-state representation, whereas a non-injective encoder gives a reduced representation whose value labels a fiber of compatible states. For a specified task, an exact decoder exists on a state class if and only if the task is constant on the encoder fibers within that class. Variational principles, reconstruction correspondences, functionals, kernels, and closures are different realizations of additional structure used to select, restrict, or approximate the task-relevant content of a fiber when the retained variable alone is insufficient. Static moments and imaginary-time correlation functions are unified as restrictions of a complete equilibrium readout functional to different probe families. Within the same principle, quantum embedding can be viewed as consistency or replacement between global and local descriptions through reduced interface encoders and their conjugate fields.

</details>


### [169] [The UZH protocol: Separating errors and constructing improved CP2K basis sets and pseudopotentials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11064)
*Hossein Mirhosseini,Tiziano M. A. Müller,Matthias Krack,Thomas D. Kühne,Jürg Hutter*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出 UZH 协议，一种闭环 CP2K 工作流，通过三路对比（CP2K-GTH-UZH、SIRIUS 平面波、全势线性化缀加平面波参考）将 CP2K 的数值误差分解为高斯基组误差与赝势误差，并据此对基组和赝势参数文件进行定向修订与优化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 可靠的密度泛函模拟要求数值设置的残余误差小于待解释的化学与材料趋势。CP2K/Quickstep 同时使用原子中心高斯基组（Gaussian basis sets）和模守恒赝势（norm-conserving pseudopotentials），导致代码间差异（code-to-code discrepancy）通常同时包含两种贡献，难以直接归因和校准。

Method: UZH 协议是一个闭环 CP2K 工作流，先在分子上校准优化后的 MOLOPT 高斯基组，再通过单质晶体状态方程基准（unary-crystal equation-of-state benchmarks）验证设置。核心诊断是三重对比：CP2K-GTH-UZH 计算结果、使用相同 GTH 赝势的系统性平面波表示的 SIRIUS 计算，以及全势线性化缀加平面波（all-electron full-potential linearized augmented-plane-wave, LAPW）SIRIUS 参考，从而将 CP2K 误差分解为高斯基组分量和赝势分量。

Result: 该协议能够区分基组受限的惰性气体和重元素案例与赝势受限的过渡金属案例，指导 CP2K 基组和赝势优化器进行定向修订，最终产出改进后的 MOLOPT 基组和 GTH 赝势参数文件。

Conclusion: UZH 协议是建设性的（constructive）：它不仅仅是在事后测量或减少误差，而是允许将验证异常值（verification outliers）转化为经过验证的 CP2K 参数文件，适用于分子相和凝聚相模拟。

Abstract: Reliable density-functional simulations require numerical settings whose residual errors are smaller than the chemical and materials trends being interpreted. In CP2K/Quickstep, this requirement is complicated by the joint use of atom-centered Gaussian basis sets and norm-conserving pseudopotentials: a code-to-code discrepancy usually contains both contributions. We present the UZH protocol, a closed-loop CP2K workflow that calibrates molecularly optimized Gaussian basis sets on small molecules, validates the resulting settings in unary-crystal equation-of-state benchmarks, identifies whether the limiting approximation is the Gaussian basis or the pseudopotential. The diagnosis is then used to revise the parameter files. The central diagnostic is a three-way comparison between production CP2K-GTH-UZH calculations, SIRIUS calculations using the same Goedecker--Teter--Hutter pseudopotential in a systematic plane-wave representation, and all-electron full-potential linearized augmented-plane-wave SIRIUS references. This construction decomposes the practical CP2K error into a Gaussian-basis component and a pseudopotential component. The protocol distinguishes basis-limited noble-gas and heavy-element cases from pseudopotential-limited transition-metal cases, guides targeted revisions with the CP2K basis and pseudopotential optimizers, and produces improved MOLOPT basis sets and GTH pseudopotentials as explicit outputs of the workflow. The UZH protocol is therefore constructive: it does not merely measure or reduce errors a posteriori, but allows turning verification outliers into validated CP2K parameter files for simulations across molecules and condensed phases.

</details>


<div id='physics.optics'></div>

# physics.optics [[Back]](#toc)

### [170] [Unidirectional-like Edge Transport Induced by Non-Hermitian Skin Effects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10291)
*Junyi Rao,Jinting Ding,Qinghua Guo,Jun He,Xiang Ni*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文从理论和实验上证明，均匀损耗（uniform loss）是一种简单且此前被忽视的机制，能够在光子晶体（photonic crystals, PhCs）中实现类单向（unidirectional-like）的边界波传输。通过设计具有相同陈数（Chern numbers）但不同体极化（bulk polarizations）的纤芯-包层几何结构，均匀损耗激活了非厄米趋肤效应（non-Hermitian skin effects, NHSEs），重塑边缘带（edge bands）的谱拓扑（spectral topology），产生决定单向传播的点间隙缠绕（point gap windings）。近场测量证实损耗将本质上双向的界面态转变为环绕整个畴壁的类单向传播，与理论高度吻合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非厄米趋肤效应能够实现波的显著边界累积，但其实验实现通常需要工程化的非互易性（engineered nonreciprocity）或空间图案化的损耗（spatially patterned loss）。本文旨在探索一种更简单、普适的机制，即仅利用均匀损耗来实现类单向边界传输。

Method: 采用纤芯-包层（core cladding）几何结构设计光子晶体，其中两个畴域具有相同的陈数（Chern numbers）但不同的体极化（bulk polarizations）。通过引入均匀损耗来激活非厄米趋肤效应，从而重塑边缘带的谱拓扑结构，产生点间隙缠绕（point gap windings）。实验上采用近场测量（near field measurements）验证传输特性。

Result: 均匀损耗能够激活非厄米趋肤效应，使本质上双向的界面态转变为环绕整个畴壁的类单向（unidirectional-like）传播。近场测量结果与理论预测高度吻合。

Conclusion: 均匀损耗是一种通用且结构简单的途径，可用于实现类单向波传输，为克服传统非互易性或空间图案化损耗方案的复杂性提供了新思路。

Abstract: Non-Hermitian skin effects (NHSEs) enable dramatic boundary accumulation of waves, yet their experimental realization typically demands engineered nonreciprocity or spatially patterned loss. Here we demonstrate theoretically and experimentally that uniform loss provides a simple and previously overlooked mechanism for enforcing unidirectional-like edge transport in photonic crystals (PhCs) that breaks time-reversal symmetry in the presence of nonchiral edge states. Using a core cladding geometry where domains share identical Chern numbers but possess distinct bulk polarizations, we show that uniform loss activates NHSEs that reshape the spectral topology of edge bands, giving rise to point gap windings that dictate a one way propagation. Near field measurements confirm that loss converts intrinsically bidirectional interface states into a unidirectional-like circulation around the entire domain wall, showing excellent agreement with theory. Our results establish uniform loss as a universal and structurally simple route for achieving unidirectional-like wave transport.

### [171] [Topological origin of flow distributions in disordered porous media](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10919)
*Jose Arnal,Guillem Sole-Mari,Tomás Aquino*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 本文基于孔隙网络模型（pore-network model）发展了二维无序圆形障碍物多孔介质中稳态斯托克斯流（steady Stokes flow）的统计理论。研究发现孔隙体的流速分布服从伽马分布（Gamma distribution），且该分布可直接由孔隙喉道宽度的几何变异系数（coefficient of variation）参数化。理论预测与计算流体动力学（CFD）模拟结果高度吻合，优于忽略局部流速相关性的平均场模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统平均场模型忽略了多孔介质中局部流速的拆分与合并相关性，导致预测精度不足。本文旨在发展一种能够捕获局部流动相关性、同时仅需最少几何信息的统计理论，以更准确地描述无序多孔网络中的流速分布。

Method: 采用孔隙网络模型作为理论框架，将多孔介质抽象为孔隙体（pore body）和孔隙喉道（pore throat）构成的网络。通过分析局部流动相关性，推导出孔隙体流速的伽马分布形式，并由此确定孔隙喉道的流速分布。将伽马分布的形状参数与孔隙喉道宽度的变异系数建立直接联系，实现模型参数化。

Result: 孔隙体流速服从伽马分布，孔隙喉道流速分布可由该伽马分布完全确定。伽马分布可与孔隙喉道宽度的变异系数直接关联。理论预测与计算流体动力学（CFD）模拟结果高度一致，精度显著优于忽略局部流速相关性的平均场模型。

Conclusion: 局部流速的拆分与合并过程是塑造无序多孔网络中流速分布的关键机制。所发展的理论模型仅需最小限度的几何信息即可参数化，为多孔介质流动的统计描述提供了一种高效且准确的解析框架。

Abstract: We investigate steady Stokes flow through porous media composed of two-dimensional disordered arrays of circular obstacles. We develop a theory for the statistics of flow rates based on a pore-network model that captures local flow correlations. We show that the flow rate distribution across the ensemble of pore bodies follows a Gamma distribution, and that the flow rate distribution through pore throats is fully determined in terms of it. Furthermore, this Gamma distribution can be directly linked to simple geometrical properties such as the coefficient of variation of pore throat widths, rendering the model parameterisable from minimal medium information. The resulting predictions agree closely with computational fluid dynamics simulations and show markedly better agreement than prior mean-field models that neglect local flow-rate correlations, clarifying how local splitting and merging shape flow in disordered porous networks.

### [172] [Multifractal Signatures of Ageing and Dementia Development: A Multifractal Space-Filling Curve Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10222)
*Marta Lotka,Jacek Grela,Zbigniew Drogosz,Jeremi K. Ochab,Paweł Oświęcimka*

Main category: q-bio.NC

TL;DR: 本文提出一种名为多重分形空间填充曲线分析（MFSCA）的新方法，用于量化多维数据的相关结构。该方法将多维数据通过分形空间填充曲线投影至一维信号，再利用多重分形算法进行分析。在人工生成数据和真实数据（特别是阿尔茨海默症患者的MRI数据）上的实验表明，大脑空间组织的多重分形性随年龄增长和痴呆发展逐渐减弱，出现从多重分形向单分形的转变，表明MRI数据的多重分形特征可作为脑结构变化的标记物。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多重分形（multifractality）是量化复杂数据中非线性、无标度性质的有效形式体系。该研究旨在开发一种新颖且高效的方法，以量化多维数据的相关结构，并探索其在脑影像分析中的应用。

Method: 该方法称为多重分形空间填充曲线分析（Multifractal Space-filling Curve Analysis, MFSCA）。其核心步骤为：首先利用分形空间填充曲线（fractal space-filling curve）将原始多维数据投影至一维表示，同时保留数据的局部和长程组织特性；随后对得到的一维信号应用多重分形算法进行分析。

Result: 对阿尔茨海默症不同阶段患者的MRI数据分析显示：大脑空间组织的多重分形程度随年龄增长和痴呆发展而逐步减弱；在年轻对照组与老年对照组之间，以及在相似年龄但处于不同疾病阶段的痴呆患者（早期痴呆与轻度认知障碍）之间，均观察到了从多重分形向单分形（monofractality）的转变。这表明在恶化条件下，大脑空间组织的异质性特征退化，趋向于同质且弱相关的结构。

Conclusion: MFSCA方法能够有效捕捉大脑组织的关键特征；MRI数据的多重分形性可以作为脑结构变化的标记物（marker）。

Abstract: Multifractality is an effective formalism for quantifying the nonlinear, scale-free properties of complex data. In this study, we propose a novel and efficient methodology, termed Multifractal Space-filling Curve Analysis (MFSCA), for quantifying the correlation structure of multidimensional data. Within this framework, the original multidimensional data - while preserving both local and long-range organisational properties - are projected onto a one-dimensional representation using a fractal space-filling curve. The resulting one-dimensional signal is then analysed using multifractal algorithms. We demonstrate the utility of the method using both artificially generated multifractal structures and real data. In particular, we apply MFSCA to analyse magnetic resonance imaging (MRI) data from Alzheimer patients at different stages of dementia. Based on the results, we estimate the multifractal profiles of the brain for healthy subjects of different ages as well as for dementia patients. The analysis reveals that the spatial organization of brain structures, as measured by the degree of multifractality, progressively weakens with age and the development of dementia. A transition from multifractality to monofractality is observed both in control groups, when comparing the Young Control and Elderly Control groups, and among dementia subjects of similar age but at different stages of the disease, namely early dementia and mild cognitive impairment. Thus, from the perspective of multiscaling properties, the heterogeneous characteristics of spatial brain organization deteriorate under worsening conditions, leading to a homogeneous and weakly correlated structure. These findings not only effectively capture key aspects of brain organisation, but also demonstrate that the multifractality of MRI data can serve as a marker of structural brain changes.

</details>

### [173] [Neural-network solution of subtracted three-body Faddeev integral equations near the Efimov limit](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10343)
*Lucas A. Souza*

Main category: nucl-th

TL;DR: 本文提出将深度神经网络（DNN）作为对称化 spectator 矢量（symmetrized spectator vector）的变分拟设（ansatz），用于求解减除后的三体 Faddeev 积分方程（subtracted three-body Faddeev integral equation），并以残差最小化训练网络，在 Efimov 极限附近以高精度复现了束缚尺度标度律与散射长度连续演化，验证了 DNN 可作为重整化少体积分方程的一种紧致可微表示。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统确定性对角化方法求解三体 Faddeev 积分方程的计算成本较高，且解的形式不够灵活；本文试图探索 DNN 是否能够以紧致可微的形式逼近该积分方程的重整化解，从而为少体量子系统提供一种新的数值求解范式。

Method: 以 DNN 参数化对称化 spectator 矢量，通过最小化离散积分方程的残差来训练网络，并将与三体能量相关的正束缚标度（binding scale）作为可训练参数；确定性对角化仅用作事后数值基准。方法先在与解析解可比的氢原子径向问题上验证，再应用于共振态（unitarity）下的三体 Efimov 态。

Result: 在共振态（unitarity）下，DNN 再现了 Efimov 基态束缚标度，与确定性解的偏差为 0.022%；第一激发态的偏差为 0.002%。确定性求解器恢复了普适 Efimov 标度比 $e^{2π/s_0}\simeq 515.03$，神经方法通过从共振解连续延拓，追踪了束缚态分支随逆散射长度 $1/a$ 的变化。

Conclusion: 基于 DNN 的残差最小化能够为离散标度不变性（discrete scale invariance）主导区域内的重整化少体积分方程提供一种紧致且可微的表示，初步验证了神经求解器在少体量子问题中的可行性。

Abstract: We apply a deep-neural-network (DNN) ansatz to the symmetrized spectator vector of the subtracted three-body Faddeev integral equation for identical bosons near the Efimov limit. The network is trained by minimizing the residual of the discretized integral equation, while the positive binding scale associated with the three-body energy is treated as a trainable parameter. Deterministic diagonalization of the same discretized kernel is used only as an a posteriori numerical benchmark. As preliminary validation, the neural-solver strategy is tested on the analytically solvable hydrogen radial problem. At unitarity, the DNN reproduces the Efimov ground-state binding scale with a DNN--deterministic deviation of $0.022\%$, while the first excited state is recovered to $0.002\%$. The deterministic solver recovers the universal Efimov scaling ratio $e^{2π/s_0}\simeq 515.03$, and the neural method traces the bound-state branches as a function of the inverse scattering length $1/a$ by continuation from the unitary solution. These results indicate that DNN-based residual minimization can provide a compact and differentiable representation of a renormalized few-body integral-equation solution in a regime governed by discrete scale invariance.

</details>

Conclusion: 精确的总粲产量测量，结合来自初始硬散射的粲夸克产生计算方面的进步，可用于反推预平衡阶段的相关信息。

A non-negligible contribution to the overall charm quark production is found albeit large theoretical uncertainties are limiting factors. We conclude that precise total charm production measurements combined with progress on charm production calculations from the initial hard scatterings can be used to infer information on the pre-equilibrium stage.

*Charles Kacir,Joseph Moscoso,Amy Nicholson,Thomas R. Richardson,Cade Rodgers*

Method: 采用两种互补方法：(1) 数值晶格计算（numerical lattice computation），用于在离散格点上模拟关联函数的统计行为；(2) 大同种物种数极限（large number of identical species limit）下的解析展开（analytic expansion），从解析角度推导关联函数概率分布的渐近形式。

Conclusion: 本文展示了初步的探索性研究结果，并规划了未来更深入的调查方向，以进一步完善对通用n体团簇谱的理论理解。

### [177] [Frenet turns](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10606)
*Boris Shapiro*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文研究了A. Agrachev提出的问题：在$\mathbb R^n$中，一个标准圆需要绕行多少圈才能通过处处Frenet标架非退化的曲线进行形变。答案依赖于所采用的拓扑：在$C^n$曲线拓扑下，平面圆的最小圈数$k(2)=1, k(3)=2, k(n)=1\ (n\ge4)$；在Agrachev原意下的Frenet控制问题中，对$n\ge4$存在球面Fenchel障碍。为保留非平凡圈数计数问题，引入了修饰圈数（decorated turn）数据，并证明了在偶数维和奇数维空间中不同条件下的可达性结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该问题起源于A. Agrachev的一个提问：在$\mathbb R^n$中，一个普通圆需绕行多少圈，才能通过一条处处Frenet标架（Frenet frame）非退化的曲线形变得到。该问题涉及曲线拓扑与微分几何的交叉，其答案依赖于所选取的拓扑结构。

Method: 本文区分了两种不同拓扑解释下的问题：其一是字面意义的$C^n$曲线拓扑（literal $C^n$ curve topology），其二是Agrachev原意中的Frenet控制（Frenet-control）问题。针对后者，引入修饰圈数（decorated turn）数据——在$\mathbb R^4$中为记录切平面和法平面圈数的一对$(p,q)$，在偶数维$\mathbb R^{2r}$中为向量$(p_1,\ldots,p_r)$，并通过常值Frenet控制（constant Frenet controls）分析可达性。

Result: 在$C^n$曲线拓扑下，平面圆允许任意小非退化扰动的最少圈数为$k(2)=1,\ k(3)=2,\ k(n)=1\ (n\ge4)$。在Agrachev原意解释下，对所有$n\ge4$存在简单的球面Fenchel障碍（spherical Fenchel obstruction）。对修饰圈数数据，在$\mathbb R^4$中，每一对非共振（nonresonant）的正数$(p,q)$（$p\ne q$）均可通过小的正常值Frenet控制实现；在$\mathbb R^{2r}$中，任意分量两两互异的正向量均可通过常值控制实现；奇数维空间则需要显含时间的开合（time-dependent openings），因为常值控制无法闭合基曲线。

Conclusion: Agrachev问题的答案高度依赖于所采用的拓扑和维度。$C^n$拓扑下的圈数结果在$n=4$时出现非平凡行为（与$n\ge4$不同），而Agrachev原意下的Frenet控制问题在高维存在Fenchel障碍。通过引入修饰圈数数据，偶数维空间可获得完备的可达性刻画，奇数维空间则必然需要时变控制。

Abstract: We discuss a problem posed by A.~Agrachev asking how many times a usual circle in $\mathbb R^n$ should be traversed to admit a deformation by curves with nowhere degenerating Frenet frame. It turns out that the answer depends on a specific topology which we consider. For the literal $C^n$ curve topology, the least number of turns of a plane circle admitting arbitrarily small nondegenerate perturbations is \[
  k(2)=1,\qquad k(3)=2,\qquad k(n)=1\quad(n\ge4). \] This jet-level problem is different from the original Frenet-control problem by Agrachev. We show that in the literal interpretation of Agrachev's problem one has a simple spherical Fenchel obstruction in all dimensions $n\ge4$.
  To retain a nontrivial turn-counting problem, we introduce decorated turn data. In $\R^4$ the datum is a pair $(p,q)$ recording tangent-plane and normal-plane turns; we prove that every nonresonant pair $(p,q)$ with $p,q>0$, $p\ne q$, is accessible by small positive constant Frenet controls. In even dimension $2r$ the analogous datum is a vector $(p_1,\ldots,p_r)$, and every vector with pairwise distinct positive entries is accessible by constant controls. Odd dimensions require genuinely time-dependent openings since constant controls cannot close the base curve.

</details>
